# ORACLE_TEXT_EFFECT_MAP

Purpose: quickly map oracle text phrases to the correct effect class + slot. Search this file for keywords from the card's oracle text to find the matching effect without reading EFFECTS_QUICK_REFERENCE.md.

- "When [this] dies, return it to the battlefield transformed under your control at the beginning of the next end step." -> `EffectSlot.ON_DEATH` + `RegisterDelayedReturnSourceTransformedEffect()`.
- "When you sacrifice this creature, return it to the battlefield transformed under its owner's control at the beginning of the next end step." -> `EffectSlot.ON_DEATH` + `RegisterDelayedReturnSourceTransformedEffect(true, true)` (onlyIfSacrificed + underOwnerControl). Collected from the sacrifice path via `CardEffect.onlyTriggersOnSacrifice()`, not on other deaths.
- "When [this] dies, return it to its owner's hand." -> `EffectSlot.ON_DEATH` + `ReturnSourceCardFromGraveyardToOwnerHandEffect()` (Endless Cockroaches).
- "When [this] dies, return it to its owner's hand at the beginning of the next end step." -> `EffectSlot.ON_DEATH` + `RegisterDelayedReturnCardFromGraveyardToHandEffect(null)` (The Locust God). Handler falls back to the stack-entry source card when `cardId` is null.
- "When target creature dies this turn, return that card to the battlefield under its owner's control." (Graceful Reprieve) -> target a creature + `EffectSlot.SPELL` + `ReturnTargetCardOnDeathThisTurnEffect()`. Delayed trigger; the death pipeline pushes the return automatically. Pass `ReturnTargetCardOnDeathThisTurnEffect(true)` to return the card **tapped** (Supernatural Stamina — also adds `BoostTargetCreatureEffect(2, 0)` on the same target).
- "[Deals N damage to target creature.] When a creature dealt damage this way dies this turn, create a ... token." (Skeletonize) -> target a creature + `EffectSlot.SPELL` + `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(N)` + `CreateTokenOnTargetDeathThisTurnEffect(new CreateTokenEffect(...))`. Delayed trigger; the death pipeline creates the token under the spell's controller immediately when the damaged creature dies.
- "When [this] dies, put it on top of its owner's library." -> `EffectSlot.ON_DEATH` + `PutSourceCardFromGraveyardIntoLibraryNFromTopEffect(0)` (Undying Beast).
- "When [this] is put into your graveyard from the battlefield, put it into your library third from the top." -> `EffectSlot.ON_DEATH` + `PutSourceCardFromGraveyardIntoLibraryNFromTopEffect(2)` (Enigma Sphinx; 0-indexed position, 2 = third from top).
- "When [this] dies, exile it." -> `EffectSlot.ON_DEATH` + `ExileSourceCardFromGraveyardEffect()` (Cyclopean Mummy).
- "When [this] dies, create a N/N [color] [Subtype] creature token ... at the beginning of the next end step." -> `EffectSlot.ON_DEATH` + `RegisterDelayedCreateTokenEffect(new CreateTokenEffect(...))` (Rukh Egg). The wrapped `CreateTokenEffect` is resolved at the next end step, not immediately.
- "Whenever a spell or ability an opponent controls causes a land to be put into your graveyard from the battlefield, return that card to the battlefield." (Sacred Ground) -> `EffectSlot.ON_ALLY_LAND_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD_BY_OPPONENT` + `ReturnTriggeringLandFromGraveyardToBattlefieldEffect(null)`. The engine reads `GameData.currentlyResolvingControllerId` (set in `StackResolutionService`) to confirm an opponent's spell/ability caused it.
- Reanimation Aura — "Enchant creature card in a graveyard. When this Aura enters, return enchanted creature card to the battlefield under your control and attach this Aura to it. When this Aura leaves the battlefield, that creature's controller sacrifices it." (Animate Dead) -> put a graveyard-targeting `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).source(ALL_GRAVEYARDS).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).targetGraveyard(true).build()` in `EffectSlot.SPELL` (this drives cast-time graveyard targeting/validation and marks the stack entry's target zone `GRAVEYARD`), plus the static boost in `EffectSlot.STATIC` (e.g. `StaticBoostEffect(-1, 0, GrantScope.ENCHANTED_CREATURE)`) and `SacrificeEnchantedCreatureOnLeaveEffect()` in `EffectSlot.ON_SELF_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD`. `StackResolutionService.resolveEnchantmentSpell` detects `isAura() && targetZone == GRAVEYARD`, reanimates the enchanted card via `GraveyardReturnSupport.reanimateTargetedCard`, and attaches the Aura. `EffectResolution` treats such an Aura's cast target as the graveyard card (not a battlefield permanent).

## Damage

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "deals N damage to any target" | `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect(N, false)` | SPELL | Targeting auto-derived |
| "deals N damage to any target that was dealt damage this turn" | `target(new AnyTargetPredicateTargetFilter(new PermanentDealtDamageThisTurnPredicate(), new PlayerDealtDamageThisTurnPredicate(), msg)).addEffect(SPELL, DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect(N))` | SPELL | Needle Drop. The `AnyTargetPredicateTargetFilter` restricts both the permanent and player side of an any-target effect; never a new damage-effect class |
| "at the beginning of your upkeep, ~ deals N damage to any target" | `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect(N)` | `UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` | Form of the Dragon. Upkeep triggers whose effect is true "any target" (`targetSpec()` is `ANY_TARGET` — includes players AND permanents) route through the upkeep any-target pipeline (target chosen at trigger time, CR 603.3d) |
| "Kinship — At the beginning of your upkeep, you may look at the top card of your library. If it shares a creature type with this creature, you may reveal it. If you do, [effects]" | `KinshipEffect(List.of(...revealEffects))` | `UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` | Morningtide Kinship. Wrap the "If you do" effects (resolved against the source permanent) — e.g. Kithkin Zephyrnaut: `BoostSelfEffect(2,2) + GrantKeywordEffect(FLYING, SELF) + GrantKeywordEffect(VIGILANCE, SELF)`. Share check counts Changeling as every creature type; the reveal is a `PendingMayAbility` |
| "deals N damage to the player or planeswalker it's attacking" | `DealDamageToAttackedTargetEffect(N)` | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ATTACKS`/attack trigger | Uses the attacking creature's `attackedTargetId` context captured by `CombatAttackService`; not a targeted ability |
| "Whenever equipped creature attacks, it deals damage equal to its power to the player or planeswalker it's attacking" | `EquippedCreatureDealsPowerToAttackedTargetEffect()` | `ON_ATTACK` (on the Equipment) | Mage Slayer. Non-targeting: the handler finds the equipped creature via the Equipment's `attachedTo`, reads the recipient from the creature's live `attackTarget`, and deals `power` damage with the **equipped creature** as source (its power sets the amount; its keywords, e.g. infect, apply). Fires even when the creature is blocked |
| "Whenever a creature you control with a +1/+1 counter on it attacks, you may have that creature deal 1 damage to target player or planeswalker" | `target(new PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(new PermanentIsPlaneswalkerPredicate(), "…")).addEffect(...)` + `TriggeringPermanentConditionalEffect(new PermanentHasCountersPredicate(CounterType.PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE), new MayEffect(new DealDamageToTargetPlayerOrPlaneswalkerEffect(1), "…"))` | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ATTACKS` | Rage Forger. The permanent-conditional filters by the attacking permanent's counters; the `MayEffect` becomes a CR 603.5 resolution-time may whose source permanent is the attacker ("that creature"). The card-level planeswalker filter restricts permanent targets to planeswalkers (players auto-added) |
| "Whenever a [subtype] you control attacks and isn't blocked, it gets +X/+Y until end of turn" | `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect(new CardSubtypePredicate(subtype), new BoostSelfEffect(X, Y))` | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ATTACKS_UNBLOCKED` | Stinkdrinker Bandit (Rogue, +2/+1). Fires once per unblocked attacker during declare-blockers (in `CombatBlockService`); the unblocked creature is the trigger's non-targeting `sourcePermanentId`, so `BoostSelfEffect` applies to "it" |
| "Whenever a creature attacks you or a planeswalker you control, reveal the top card... if it's a [type], remove that creature from combat. Then put... on the bottom" | `RevealTopCardRemoveTargetFromCombatIfMatchEffect(CardPredicate)` | `ON_CREATURE_ATTACKS_YOU` | Fires once per attacking creature on the defending player's side; the attacking creature is set as the non-targeting `targetId`. Used by Lost in the Woods (`CardSubtypePredicate(FOREST)`) |
| "Whenever a creature with flying attacks you, this deals N damage to it" | `DealDamageToTriggeringAttackerEffect(N, new PermanentHasKeywordPredicate(FLYING))` | `ON_CREATURE_ATTACKS_YOU` | The predicate restricts which attackers fire the trigger (checked at attack declaration in `CombatAttackService`); damage is dealt to the attacking creature (non-targeting `targetId`) on resolution. Used by Raking Canopy (4 damage) |
| "Whenever a creature attacks, this artifact deals N damage to it" | `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(N)` | `ON_ANY_CREATURE_ATTACKS` | Fires once per attacking creature, on every permanent with the slot across all battlefields, regardless of who controls the attacker or whom it attacks. The attacking creature is set as the non-targeting `targetId`, so the plain target-creature damage effect hits it. Used by Caltrops |
| "Whenever a creature becomes the target of a spell or ability, return that creature to its owner's hand" | `ReturnToHandEffect.target()` | `ON_ANY_CREATURE_BECOMES_TARGET_OF_SPELL_OR_ABILITY` | Global watcher; fires on every permanent with this slot across all battlefields for ANY creature/ANY spell or ability. Targeted creature set as non-targeting `targetId`. Used by Cowardice |
| "When this creature becomes the target of a spell, sacrifice it" | `new SacrificeSelfEffect()` | `ON_BECOMES_TARGET_OF_SPELL` | Illusion self-sacrifice (Labyrinth Guardian; Jace, Cunning Castaway's tokens). Spells only, not abilities. A non-targeting effect (`TargetSpec.NONE`) in this slot goes straight on the stack with `sourcePermanentId` set, unlike Livewire Lash's damage which uses the any-target interaction |
| "Whenever this creature becomes the target of a spell or ability for the first time each turn, counter that spell or ability" | `new CounterSpellEffect()` | `ON_BECOMES_TARGET_OF_SPELL_OR_ABILITY` | Glyph Keeper. `TriggerCollectionService` special-cases any `CounterSpellingEffect` in this slot: fires at most once per turn per permanent (`Permanent.becomeTargetCounterUsedThisTurn`) and targets the triggering spell/ability's card in the STACK zone so it counters the object that targeted it. No controller restriction (counters your own spells too) |
| "You get an emblem with \"Whenever an opponent casts their first spell each turn, counter that spell.\"" | `JaceUnravelerOfSecretsEmblemEffect()` | loyalty ability | Jace, Unraveler of Secrets −8. Emblem stores `CounterOpponentFirstSpellEachTurnEffect.Marker`; on opponent cast with `getSpellsCastThisTurnCount == 1`, queues `CounterSpellEffect` targeting that spell (`Zone.STACK`). Triggers on any turn, once per opponent per turn |
| "Reveal cards from the top of your library until you reveal N nonland cards. Put the nonland cards into your hand, then put the rest on the bottom of your library in any order" | `RevealUntilNonlandCardsToHandRestToBottomEffect(N)` | SPELL | Used by Fathom Trawl. Reveals a variable number of cards (until N nonland found); lands go to bottom via async `LibraryReorder` |
| "Look at the top five cards of your library. If you control more creatures than each other player, put two of those cards into your hand. Otherwise, put one of them into your hand. Then put the rest on the bottom of your library in any order" | `new LookAtTopCardsEffect(new Fixed(5), new FixedIfControlMoreCreaturesThanEachOtherPlayer(2, 1), null, LookDestination.BOTTOM_OF_LIBRARY, false)` | SPELL | Advice from the Fae. The conditional `chooseCount` amount decides how many are kept |
| "Look at the top X cards of your library, where X is the amount of mana spent to cast this spell. Put two of them into your hand and the rest on the bottom of your library in a random order" | `LookAtTopCardsEffect.chooseNToHandRestOnBottomRandom(new ManaSpentToCast(), 2)` + `FlashbackCast` when present | SPELL | Memory Deluge. `ManaSpentToCast` is snapshotted into stack `xValue` at cast (`EffectResolution.hasManaSpentToCastAmount`); rest use `LookDestination.BOTTOM_OF_LIBRARY_RANDOM` (no reorder prompt) |
| "Look at the top five cards of your library, put one of them into your hand, and exile the rest" | `LookAtTopCardsEffect.chooseOneToHandRestToExile(new Fixed(5))` | activated ability | Browse (`{2}{U}{U}`). `LookDestination.EXILE` rest-destination; feeds the shared `LibraryRevealChoice` interaction |
| "Look at the top four cards of your library. You may reveal a creature card and/or a land card from among them and put the revealed cards into your hand. Put the rest on the bottom of your library in any order" | `LookAtTopCardsRevealTwoTypesToHandThenRestEffect.creatureAndLandToHandRestOnBottom(4)` | SPELL | Gift of the Gargantuan. Bounds the pick to **at most one creature AND at most one land** (unlike `LookAtTopCardsEffect.mayRevealUpToToHandRestOnBottom` with a creature-or-land predicate + maxReveal 2, which would allow two creatures). Runs as two sequential `LibrarySearch` picks (creature, then land) via `LibrarySearchFollowUp.forSecondBoundedPick(LAND, false)`; the land pick bottoms the rest |
| "Reveal the top five cards of your library. You may put a creature card and/or an enchantment card from among them into your hand. Put the rest into your graveyard" | `LookAtTopCardsRevealTwoTypesToHandThenRestEffect.creatureAndEnchantmentToHandRestToGraveyard(5)` | SPELL | Benefaction of Rhonas. Same two-bounded-pick shape as Gift of the Gargantuan but reveals publicly, offers creature then enchantment, and bins the rest into the graveyard (`restToGraveyard`) instead of the library bottom |
| "Search your library and graveyard for five cards and exile the rest. Put the chosen cards on top of your library in any order. You lose half your life, rounded up" | `DoomsdayEffect()` | SPELL | Doomsday. Loses half life (rounded up), then holds library+graveyard out as one pool; keeps up to 5 on top (ordered via async `LibraryReorder`), exiles the rest. Uses the `DoomsdayChoice` interaction (`CHOOSE_MULTIPLE_CARDS` prompt) |
| "Reveal cards from the top of your library until you reveal a land card. Put that card onto the battlefield and the rest on the bottom of your library in any order" | `RevealUntilLandToBattlefieldRestToBottomEffect()` | SPELL | Recross the Paths. The land enters under the caster; the non-lands go to bottom via async `LibraryReorder`. Combine with a clash reward by nesting as the `ClashEffect` pre-clash body: `new ClashEffect(List.of(new RevealUntilLandToBattlefieldRestToBottomEffect()), ReturnToHandEffect.selfSpell(), false)` |
| "Reveal the top N cards of your library, then put those cards on the bottom of your library in any order. If a card named [this] was revealed this way, [this] deals D damage to any target" | `RevealTopCardsBottomThenDamageIfCopyRevealedEffect(N, D)` | SPELL | Stomping Slabs (N=7, D=7). Always targets any target on cast (per ruling — no damage if no copy revealed); reveals top N, damages the target only when a card sharing the source's name is revealed, then bottoms all N via async `LibraryReorder` |
| "At the beginning of your upkeep, reveal the top card of your library. If it's a land card, put it into your graveyard and repeat this process." | `RevealTopCardPutLandsIntoGraveyardRepeatEffect()` | `UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` | Countryside Crusher. Reveals the controller's library one card at a time, binning each land into the graveyard until a non-land (stays on top) or empty library. Pair with `ON_ALLY_LAND_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD_FROM_ANYWHERE` |
| "Look at the top card of your library. If it's a land card or a creature card with mana value less than or equal to the number of loyalty counters on [this], you may put that card onto the battlefield." | `LookAtTopCardPutLandOrCreatureWithinLoyaltyEffect()` | loyalty ability | Nissa, Steward of Elements 0. Private look; if the top card is a land, or a creature whose MV ≤ the source permanent's loyalty counters, the controller may put it onto the battlefield (else it stays on top). Loyalty threshold read from the source permanent at resolution |
| "Whenever a land card is put into your graveyard from anywhere, put a +1/+1 counter on this creature." | `PutCountersOnSelfEffect(CounterType.PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE)` | `ON_ALLY_LAND_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD_FROM_ANYWHERE` | Countryside Crusher. Fires once per non-token land card entering the controller's graveyard from any zone (battlefield, hand, library, …) via `GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard` |
| "Whenever a creature card is put into your graveyard from anywhere, remove an omen counter from this artifact. Then if it has no omen counters on it, transform it." | `SequenceEffect.of(RemoveCounterFromSourceEffect(OMEN, 1), ConditionalEffect(NotCondition(SourceCounterThreshold(1, OMEN)), TransformSelfEffect))` | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_CARD_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD_FROM_ANYWHERE` | Soulcipher Board. Printed creature-card types only (not tokens; not animated noncreature cards). Pair with `EnterWithCountersEffect(OMEN, Fixed(3))` + own-library `LookAtTopCardsOfTargetLibraryEffect(2, PUT_ONE_INTO_GRAVEYARD)` (no target). Back face: `CanBlockOnlyIfAttackerMatchesPredicateEffect(Flying)` + loot `{3}{U}` |
| "When this enters, reveal the top four cards of your library. Put all creature cards of the chosen type revealed this way into your hand and the rest on the bottom of your library in any order." | `RevealTopCardsChosenSubtypeToHandRestToBottomEffect(4)` | `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` | Brass Herald. Reads the source permanent's chosen creature type (Changeling-aware); pair with `ChooseSubtypeOnEnterEffect` for the "As this enters, choose a creature type" line. Rest go to the bottom in any order (async `LibraryReorder`) |
| "Creatures of the chosen type get +1/+1." (all controllers) | `BoostCreaturesOfChosenSubtypeEffect(1, 1, null, true)` | `STATIC` | Brass Herald. `allControllers=true` boosts every creature of the chosen type, not just yours — contrast Vanquisher's Banner "Creatures you control of the chosen type" = `(1, 1)`. Pair with `ChooseSubtypeOnEnterEffect` |
| "Players play with their hands revealed" | `PlayWithHandsRevealedEffect()` | `STATIC` | Every player's hand visible to everyone (Zur's Weirding). Contrast `RevealOpponentHandsEffect` (Telepathy) which only shows opponents' hands to the controller |
| "If you would draw a card, draw two cards instead" | `DoubleDrawReplacementEffect()` | `STATIC` | Thought Reflection. Controller-scoped draw doubling detected in `DrawService.resolveDrawCard`; the two replacement draws use `performDrawCard` directly so they aren't recursively re-doubled |
| "If a player would draw a card, they reveal it instead. Then any other player may pay 2 life. If a player does, put that card into its owner's graveyard. Otherwise, that player draws a card" | `ZursWeirdingDrawReplacementEffect()` | `STATIC` | Zur's Weirding. Global draw-replacement detected in `DrawService`; the opponent is offered a may-ability (pay 2 life → card to drawer's graveyard, else drawer draws). Usually paired with `PlayWithHandsRevealedEffect` |
| "If you would draw a card, instead reveal the top three cards of your library. Put all creature cards revealed this way into your hand and the rest on the bottom of your library in any order" | `SagesOfTheAnimaDrawReplacementEffect()` | `STATIC` | Sages of the Anima. Controller-scoped mandatory draw replacement detected in `DrawService.resolveDrawCard` via the capability interface `RevealTopCardsCreaturesToHandDrawReplacementEffect` (reveal count is read as a fact, no concrete `instanceof`). The draw is fully replaced — creatures are put into hand (not "drawn", so no draw triggers), and an empty library reveals nothing without losing the game. 2+ non-creatures are bottomed via an async `LibraryReorder` (player chooses order) |
| "{X}, {T}: The next time you would draw a card this turn, instead look at the top X cards of your library, put all but one on the bottom in a random order, then draw a card. X can't be 0" | `new ActivatedAbility(true, "{X}", List.of(new RegisterNextDrawLookAtTopReplacementEffect()), "…")` | activated ability | Aladdin's Lamp. One-shot, turn-scoped **delayed draw replacement**: the handler stores X (from the entry's `xValue`) in `GameData.pendingNextDrawLookAtTop` keyed by player; consumed on the player's next draw in `DrawService.resolveDrawCard` (looks at top X via a `LibrarySearch` with `DRAW_CHOSEN_REST_TO_BOTTOM_RANDOM`, keeps the chosen card on top, shuffles the rest to the bottom, then draws it as a real draw). Cleared at cleanup |
| "As this enters, choose an opponent and a card name … The chosen player reveals each card they draw. When they draw a card with the chosen name, sacrifice this and it deals 10 damage to that player" | `ChooseCardNameOnEnterEffect(List.of(CardType.LAND))` (`ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD`) + `BoobyTrapEffect()` (`STATIC`) | — | Booby Trap. Chosen player = the (single) opponent; `chosenName` stamped on the permanent. Reveal + name-match trigger handled in `DrawService.performDrawCard`; trigger uses `SacrificeSelfThenDealDamageToTargetPlayerEffect(10)`. `List.of(CardType.LAND)` prevents naming basic lands |
| "Reveal the first card you draw each turn. Whenever you reveal a basic land card this way, draw a card" | `RevealFirstDrawDrawOnBasicLandEffect()` | `STATIC` | Rowen. Reveal + basic-land trigger handled in `DrawService.performDrawCard` (`checkRevealFirstDrawTriggers`); gated to the turn's first draw via `cardsDrawnThisTurn == 1`; the resulting `DrawCardEffect(1)` trigger goes on the stack and its extra draw is not revealed |
| "CARDNAME can't attack unless [condition]" | `CantAttackUnlessEffect(Condition, "unless clause")` | `STATIC` | Map the unless-clause to a Condition: "you control an [X]" = `ControlsPermanentCount(1, filter)`; "defending player controls an [X]" = `DefendingPlayerControlsPermanent(filter)`; "there are N or more [X] on the battlefield" = `AnyPlayerControlsPermanentCount(N, filter)`; "defending player is poisoned" = `DefendingPlayerPoisoned()`; "an opponent was dealt damage this turn" = `OpponentDealtDamageThisTurn(1)` (higher threshold for "N or more damage", e.g. Spinerock Knoll `OpponentDealtDamageThisTurn(7)`). Never a new class. |
| "CARDNAME can't attack or block unless [condition]" | `CantAttackOrBlockUnlessEffect(Condition, "unless clause")` | `STATIC` | Block-side counterpart of `CantAttackUnlessEffect` (same Condition mapping). "you control another [X]" = `ControlsAnotherPermanent(filter)` (excludes the source, e.g. Blind-Spot Giant "another Giant"); "you control at least N other [X]" = `ControlsOtherPermanentCount(N, filter)` (count analogue excluding the source, e.g. the Amonkhet gods' Oketra the True "at least three other creatures"). |
| "CARDNAME can't block unless [condition]" (attacking unrestricted) | `CantBlockUnlessEffect(Condition, "unless clause")` | `STATIC` | Block-ONLY (do NOT use `CantAttackOrBlockUnlessEffect`, which would also bar attacking). Same Condition mapping. "you control another Zombie" = `ControlsOtherPermanentCount(1, new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(ZOMBIE))` (excludes the source), e.g. Marauding Boneslasher. Evaluated in `GameQueryService.canBlock`. |
| "CARDNAME can't attack unless a creature with greater power also attacks. CARDNAME can't block unless a creature with greater power also blocks." | `CantAttackOrBlockUnlessGreaterPowerAlsoDoesEffect()` | `STATIC` | Okk. Combat-set-dependent (not a `Condition`): validated at declaration time against the other attackers/blockers in the same combat (strictly greater power). Comparison is checked only as attackers/blockers are declared. |
| "CARDNAME can't attack unless at least two other creatures attack. CARDNAME can't block unless at least two other creatures block." | `CantAttackOrBlockUnlessCountAlsoDoesEffect(2)` | `STATIC` | Orcish Conscripts. Combat-set-dependent (not a `Condition`): validated at declaration time against the count of other attackers/blockers in the same combat. Swap the `otherCount` for other "at least N other creatures" thresholds. |
| "Enchanted creature can't attack or block, and its activated abilities with {T} in their costs can't be activated." | `EnchantedCreatureCantAttackOrBlockEffect()` + `EnchantedCreatureCantActivateTapAbilitiesEffect()` | `STATIC` | Serra Bestiary. Tap-only ability lock (non-tap activated abilities stay usable) — contrast Arrest's `EnchantedCreatureCantActivateAbilitiesEffect` which blocks all abilities. Pair with the upkeep sacrifice-unless-pay `ForcedCostOrElseEffect(PayManaCost("{W}{W}"), List.of(SacrificeSelfEffect()), true)`. |
| "Enchanted creature can't attack, block, or transform." | `EnchantedCreatureCantAttackOrBlockEffect()` + `EnchantedCreatureCantTransformEffect()` | `STATIC` | Bound by Moonsilver. Transform lock is an Aura marker checked in `GameQueryService.isTransformPrevented` (not `PreventTransformEffect`, which is controller-scoped). |
| "Enchanted creature can't attack unless its controller pays {N}." | Aura: `target(PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(PermanentIsCreaturePredicate, ...))` + `STATIC EnchantedCreatureCantAttackUnlessPaysEffect(N)` | `STATIC` | Brainwash ({3}). Per-creature attack tax scoped to the enchanted creature (paid as an additional cost to declare it); contrast the uniform `RequirePaymentToAttackEffect` (Windborn Muse). |
| "Target creature can't attack this turn." (resolved spell/ability, not an Aura) | `LockTargetPermanentEffect(true, false, false, EffectDuration.UNTIL_END_OF_TURN)` | activated ability / spell | Edifice of Authority (1st ability). Stamps a `FloatingContinuousEffect` on the target; `CombatAttackService.canCreatureAttack` reads the `PermanentLockEffect` fact. Wears off at cleanup. Duration-scoped, per-target — unlike the static Aura restrictions above. |
| "Until your next turn, target creature can't attack or block and its activated abilities can't be activated." (Detain) | `LockTargetPermanentEffect(true, true, true, EffectDuration.UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN)` | activated ability / spell | Edifice of Authority (2nd ability). Detain: floating `PermanentLockEffect` on the target read by `CombatAttackService` (attack), `GameQueryService.findBlockDenial` (block), and `AbilityActivationService.validateNotBlockedByStaticAbilityLock` (activated abilities, mana abilities included; triggered abilities unaffected). Expires at the ability controller's next turn start. |
| "This creature can't block creatures with power P or greater unless you pay {N}." | `STATIC CantBlockHighPowerCreaturesUnlessPaysEffect(P, N)` | `STATIC` | Hipparion (`(3, 1)`). Block-side counterpart of the attack tax — charged per qualifying block in `CombatBlockService.declareBlockers` via the `BlockCostEffect` capability interface. The block stays legal; only the {N} cost gates it. |
| "This creature can't block creatures with power P or greater." | `STATIC CantBlockCreaturesWithPowerAtLeastEffect(P)` | `STATIC` | Ironclaw Orcs (`(2)`). Hard fixed-threshold restriction (no cost, not self-referential). Compared against the attacker's effective power in `GameQueryService.findBlockDenial`. |
| "Enchanted creature can't block creatures with power equal to or greater than the enchanted creature's toughness." | Aura: `target(PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(PermanentIsCreaturePredicate, ...))` + `STATIC CantBlockCreaturesWithPowerGreaterOrEqualToOwnToughnessEffect()` | `STATIC` | Ironclaw Curse (pair with `StaticBoostEffect(0, -1, ENCHANTED_CREATURE)`). Self-referential hard restriction (not a cost): `GameQueryService.findBlockDenial` compares the attacker's effective power against the blocker's effective toughness. Read on the blocker's own STATIC effects or via an aura attached to it. |
| "deals N damage to target creature" | `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(N)` | SPELL | Creature-only targeting |
| "deals N damage to target creature. Other creatures can't attack this turn." | `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(N)` + `OtherCreaturesCantAttackThisTurnEffect()` | SPELL | Intimidation Bolt. Two SPELL effects sharing one creature target; the rider installs a turn-scoped lock (`GameData.otherCreaturesCantAttackExemptCreatureIds`) that exempts only the targeted creature — if it dies to the damage, nothing can attack; bars creatures entering later too. Cleared at each turn transition |
| "deals N damage to target creature or planeswalker" | `DealDamageToTargetCreatureOrPlaneswalkerEffect(N)` | SPELL | |
| "deals N damage to target opponent or planeswalker" | `DealDamageToTargetOpponentOrPlaneswalkerEffect(N)` | SPELL | Amount may be a `DynamicAmount`; pair with `SacrificeCreatureCost(false, true)` + `new XValue()` for "damage equal to the sacrificed creature's power to target opponent or planeswalker" (Final Strike) |
| "deals N damage to target opponent and N damage to up to M target creatures that player controls" | `DealDamageToTargetOpponentAndUpToCreaturesThatPlayerControlsEffect(N, N, M)` | `ON_TRANSFORM_TO_BACK_FACE` | Two-step transform trigger target choice; use M=1 for "up to one" |
| "deals N damage to target player" | `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(N, DamageRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)` | SPELL | Only recipient that targets. Amount is any `DynamicAmount` |
| "deals N damage to each opponent" | `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(N, DamageRecipient.EACH_OPPONENT)` | SPELL/trigger | No targeting. Amount evaluates once — for dynamic amounts pass a `DynamicAmount`, e.g. `new CountersOnSource(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE)` (Hallar). NOT for per-opponent amounts (Molten Psyche keeps its own record) |
| "deals N damage to each player" | `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(N, DamageRecipient.EACH_PLAYER)` | SPELL | No targeting |
| "At the beginning of each player's end step, if that player didn't cast a spell this turn, deals N damage to that player" | `DealDamageIfDidntCastSpellThisTurnEffect(N)` | `END_STEP_TRIGGERED` | Impatience. Intervening-if checked at trigger (StepTriggerService bakes the end-step/active player into `targetId`) and at resolution; a countered spell still counts as cast |
| "At the beginning of each opponent's end step, if that player didn't cast a creature spell this turn, create a [token]" | `ConditionalEffect(new EndStepPlayerDidntCastCreatureSpell(), new CreateTokenEffect(...))` | `OPPONENT_END_STEP_TRIGGERED` | Predatory Advantage. Fires only on an opponent's end step (not the controller's); StepTriggerService bakes the end-step player into `targetId` and the `EndStepPlayerDidntCastCreatureSpell` condition reads it. Intervening-if checked at trigger and resolution; a countered creature spell still counts as cast. Token is created under the ability's controller |
| "At the beginning of your end step, if you control a creature with power 5 or greater, you may have this creature deal N damage to target player or planeswalker" | `ConditionalEffect(new ControlsPermanentCount(1, new PermanentPowerAtLeastPredicate(5)), new MayEffect(new DealDamageToTargetPlayerOrPlaneswalkerEffect(N), "…"))` | `CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED` | Exuberant Firestoker. Sibling of Sunseed Nurturer (same intervening-if) but the inner effect targets: the `ControlsPermanentCount` end-step branch in `StepTriggerService` routes a targeting wrapped effect through `EndStepTriggerTarget` (target chosen as the trigger goes on the stack), then the `MayEffect` prompt fires at resolution |
| "deals N damage to each creature" | `MassDamageEffect(N)` | SPELL | No targeting |
| "deals N damage to each creature and each planeswalker" | `MassDamageEffect(N, false, false, true, null)` | SPELL | damagesPlaneswalkers=true |
| "deals damage equal to the number of Giants you control to each non-Giant creature" | `DealDamageToEachMatchingPermanentEffect(new PermanentCount(HasSubtype(GIANT), CONTROLLER), Not(HasSubtype(GIANT)), ALL_PLAYERS)` | trigger | Thundercloud Shaman ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD. Handler restricts hits to creatures; amount is any `DynamicAmount` |
| "deals N damage to each white creature and each player who controls a white creature" | `DealDamageToEachPlayerControllingMatchingPermanentEffect(N, whiteCreature)` + `DealDamageToEachMatchingPermanentEffect(N, whiteCreature, ALL_PLAYERS)` | SPELL | Disorder. `whiteCreature = PermanentAllOfPredicate(IsCreature, ColorWhite)`. Add the player-damage effect FIRST so a creature dying to the mass damage doesn't spare its controller (simultaneous resolution) |
| "deals X damage to any target" | `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect(new XValue())` | SPELL | X-cost; also cost-snapshotted X (Fling's sacrificed power, Soulblast). Add `(…, false, true)` for "if it would die this turn, exile it instead" (Red Sun's Zenith) |
| "deals X damage to any target. If X is 5 or more, this spell can't be countered and the damage can't be prevented" | `CantBeCounteredEffect(new SpellXAtLeast(5))` (STATIC) + `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect(new XValue(), new SpellXAtLeast(5))` (SPELL) | STATIC + SPELL | Banefire. The conditional `CantBeCounteredEffect` is evaluated against the spell's stack entry X (`GameQueryService.isUncounterable`); the damage effect's `unpreventableWhen` gate suppresses prevention for that one damage event when X≥5. | "deals X damage to target creature" | `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(new XValue())` | SPELL | X-cost; also cost-snapshotted X (Corpse Lunge, Harvest Pyre) |

| "Destroy target Wall. It can't be regenerated. | "Whenever this creature blocks a creature, it deals damage to that creature's controller equal to this creature's power" | `DealDamageToCombatOpponentControllerEffect(new SourcePower())` | `ON_BLOCK` | Meglonoth. | "target creature fights another target creature" | `FightTargetsEffect()` | SPELL | Multi-target, any two creatures; distinct is the default |
| "you may have enchanted creature fight target creature an opponent controls" | `MayEffect(EnchantedCreatureFightsTargetCreatureEffect())` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD (Aura) | Cartouche of Strength. The fighter is the Aura's `attachedTo` (enchanted creature), NOT the Aura permanent. The fight target is chosen at resolution via the may path — do NOT use `FightTargetsEffect(0,1)` (the may path fills only one target slot) |
| "Choose two target creatures that share no creature types. Those creatures fight" | two `target(creature)` + `FightTargetsEffect()` + `setMultiTargetConstraint(MultiTargetConstraint.SHARE_NO_CREATURE_TYPES)` | SPELL | Rivals' Duel. The cross-target "share no creature types" restriction can't live in a per-target `TargetFilter` (it sees one target at a time); `MultiTargetConstraint` is checked over the whole chosen set at announcement by `TargetLegalityService`/`ValidTargetService`. Changeling counts as having every creature type. |

## Creature pump / boost

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "target creature gets +X/+Y until end of turn" | `BoostTargetCreatureEffect(X, Y)` | SPELL | Targeting auto-derived. Fixed `(int,int)` ctor; for dynamic pumps pass `DynamicAmount`s. Optional 3rd arg is a `PermanentPredicate filter` narrowing the target (e.g. `(-2, 0, AllOf(IsCreature, Not(ControlledBySourceController)))` = "target creature an opponent controls" — Ominous Sphinx's cycle/discard trigger) |
| "target creature gets +X/+X until end of turn" (X = mana paid) | `BoostTargetCreatureEffect(new XValue(), new XValue())` | SPELL | Untamed Might; `(new XValue(), new Fixed(0))` for +X/+0 (Kessig Wolf Run) |
| "target creature gets +P/+T for as long as CARDNAME remains tapped" | `BoostTargetCreatureWhileSourceTappedEffect(P, T)` | ability | Tawnos's Weaponry; records a `WHILE_SOURCE_TAPPED` floating `BuffTargetCreatureIndefinitelyEffect` keyed to the source. Ends when the source untaps (`CreatureControlService.onSourceUntapped`) or leaves. Pair with `MayNotUntapDuringUntapStepEffect` static + `{T}` cost so the source can be kept tapped |
| "target creature gets +X/+X, where X is the number of creatures you control" | `BoostTargetCreatureEffect(new PermanentCount(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), CountScope.CONTROLLER), same)` | ability | Elder of Laurels; count resolves against the effect's controller |
| "if toughness 5+, +4/-4; otherwise +4/-X where X is toughness minus 1" | `BoostTargetCreatureEffect(new Fixed(4), new Scaled(new Min(new Fixed(4), new Sum(new TargetToughness(), new Fixed(-1))), -1))` | SPELL | Blood Lust. Both branches = toughness `-min(4, t-1)` (drops to 1 below 5, else -4); `Min` is the clamp combinator |
| "target creature gets +X/+0 until end of turn, where X is 1 plus the number of cards named CARDNAME in your graveyard" | `BoostTargetCreatureEffect(new Sum(new Fixed(1), new CardsInGraveyard(new CardNamedPredicate("CARDNAME"), CountScope.CONTROLLER)), new Fixed(0))` + `GrantKeywordEffect(TRAMPLE, TARGET)` | SPELL | Ancestral Anger; count at resolution (spell not yet in graveyard) |
| "creatures you control get +X/+Y until end of turn" | `BoostAllOwnCreaturesEffect(X, Y)` | SPELL | No targeting; `int` ctor wraps in `Fixed` |
| "creatures you control get +X/+Y until end of turn" (with predicate) | `BoostAllOwnCreaturesEffect(X, Y, predicate)` | SPELL | Filtered |
| "creatures you control get +X/+X, where X is the greatest power among creatures you control" | `BoostAllOwnCreaturesEffect(new GreatestPowerAmongControlled(), new GreatestPowerAmongControlled())` | SPELL | Overwhelming Stampede; amount snapshotted once before boosts land |
| "creatures you control get +X/+X, where X is the number of creature cards in your graveyard" | `BoostAllOwnCreaturesEffect(new CardsInGraveyard(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), CONTROLLER), same)` | ability | Garruk, the Veil-Cursed |
| "all creatures get +X/+Y until end of turn" | `BoostAllCreaturesEffect(X, Y)` | SPELL | Affects all; `int` ctor wraps in `Fixed` |
| "all creatures get +X/-X (or -X/-X) until end of turn, where X was paid/sacrificed" | `BoostAllCreaturesEffect(new XValue(), new Scaled(new XValue(), -1))` / `(new Scaled(new XValue(), -1), same)` | SPELL | Flowstone Slide (+X/-X), Ichor Explosion (-X/-X); X comes from stack entry `xValue` |
| "each blocked creature gets +1/+0 and gains trample until end of turn" | `BoostAllCreaturesEffect(1, 0, new PermanentIsBlockedPredicate())` + `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.TRAMPLE, GrantScope.ALL_CREATURES, new PermanentIsBlockedPredicate())` | ACTIVATED_ABILITY | Affects all players' blocked attackers; `PermanentIsBlockedPredicate` = attacker with a blocker on it. Tattermunge Witch |
| "creatures target player controls get +X/+Y until end of turn" | `BoostAllCreaturesEffect(X, Y, EachPermanentScope.TARGET_PLAYER)` | SPELL | Targets a player (player-targeting spec when `TARGET_PLAYER`); pair with `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.CHANGELING, GrantScope.TARGET_PLAYERS_CREATURES)` for "and gain all creature types"; Shields of Velis Vel |
| "CARDNAME gets +X/+Y until end of turn" | `BoostSelfEffect(X, Y)` | ability effect | Self-pump |
| "CARDNAME gets +N/+M for each [permanent] you control" | `BoostSelfEffect(new PermanentCount(predicate, CountScope.CONTROLLER), ...)` | STATIC (or ability/trigger for until-EOT) | Any "for each" self-boost = `BoostSelfEffect` + `DynamicAmount` (see EFFECTS_INDEX "Dynamic amounts") — never a new effect class. "each *other*" → `excludeSource=true`; opponents' → `CountScope.OPPONENTS`; whole battlefield → `ANY_PLAYER` |
| "CARDNAME gets +N/+M for each [card] in your graveyard" | `BoostSelfEffect(new CardsInGraveyard(cardPredicate, CountScope.CONTROLLER), ...)` | STATIC | Multani, Yavimaya's Avatar |

| "Whenever this creature attacks, reveal the top card of your library. If it's a creature card, you gain life equal to that card's toughness, lose life equal to its power, then put it into your hand." | `RevealTopCardCreatureGainToughnessLosePowerToHandEffect()` | `ON_ATTACK` | Sapling of Colfenor. Non-creature stays revealed on top of the library (no life change). Gain (toughness) then lose (power) via `LifeSupport` before going to hand |
| "Reveal the top card of your library and put that card into your hand. You lose life equal to its mana value. | "Whenever CARDNAME attacks and isn't blocked, defending player [effect]" | effect (e.g. `DiscardEffect(1, DiscardRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER, false)`) in `EffectSlot.ON_ATTACKS_UNBLOCKED` | ON_ATTACKS_UNBLOCKED | Fires once per unblocked attacker during the declare-blockers step (before combat damage; fires even if the creature's damage is later prevented). | "Whenever a creature you control becomes blocked, it gets +N/+M until end of turn" | `BoostSelfEffect(N, M)` (self-scoped to "it"; wrap in `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect` to filter the blocked creature) | ON_ALLY_CREATURE_BECOMES_BLOCKED | Unstoppable Ash. | "Whenever this creature blocks, it deals N damage to target attacking creature" | `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(N)` in `ON_BLOCK` **plus** a card-level `target(new PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(new PermanentIsAttackingPredicate(), "…"))` | ON_BLOCK (targeting) | Elite Javelineer. | "Whenever CARDNAME blocks or becomes blocked by a [filter] creature, destroy that creature at end of combat" | `DestroyCombatOpponentAtEndOfCombatEffect(filter, false)` in **both** ON_BLOCK and ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED (`TriggerMode.PER_BLOCKER`) | ON_BLOCK + ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED | Basilisk-style delayed destroy. Deathgazer's "a nonblack creature" = `PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(CardColor.BLACK)))`. Destroys at end of combat (the creature still deals combat damage), not immediately |
| "Whenever CARDNAME blocks or becomes blocked by one or more [filter] creatures, it gets +X/+Y until end of turn" | `BoostSelfWhenCombatOpponentMatchesEffect(filter, X, Y)` in **both** ON_BLOCK and ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED (plain, non-PER_BLOCKER) | ON_BLOCK + ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED | Dwarven Soldier ("one or more Orcs", +0/+2 = `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(CardSubtype.ORC)`). Non-targeting self-boost: the trigger always resolves and the handler applies the boost only if a combat opponent (a creature this blocks / a creature blocking it) matches the filter, firing once. The self-boost analog of Deathgazer's `DestroyCombatOpponentAtEndOfCombatEffect` |
| "When this creature blocks/attacks, destroy it at end of combat" | `DestroySelfAtEndOfCombatEffect()` | ON_BLOCK / ON_ATTACK | Self-destroy delayed to end of combat (regeneration/indestructible apply — the destroy analog of Fog Elemental's `SacrificeAtEndOfCombatEffect`). Cinder Wall (ON_BLOCK only, it's a Defender Wall) |
| "When this creature blocks, it loses defender" | `RemoveKeywordEffect(Keyword.DEFENDER, GrantScope.SELF, EffectDuration.PERMANENT)` | ON_BLOCK | Elder Land Wurm. **Indefinite** loss (no "until end of turn") — pass `EffectDuration.PERMANENT` so it survives cleanup and the Wurm can attack on later turns. A plain 2-arg `RemoveKeywordEffect(...)` would only strip defender until end of turn |
| "Whenever this creature blocks a creature, that creature can't attack during its controller's next turn" | `CantAttackNextTurnCombatOpponentEffect()` | ON_BLOCK | Wall of Dust. Auto-targets the blocked attacker (a `CombatOpponentReferencingEffect`, non-targeting). At resolution sets the opponent's `Permanent.cantAttackNextTurn`; `TurnProgressionService` promotes it to `cantAttackThisTurn` at the start of that creature's controller's next turn (scoped to that controller's turn so it never arms on an opponent's turn), and `CombatAttackService.canCreatureAttack` then bars it. Self-clears after that one turn |
| "When this creature attacks or blocks, at end of combat, sacrifice it and it deals N damage to you" | `SacrificeAtEndOfCombatEffect(N)` | ON_ATTACK + ON_BLOCK | Time Elemental (N=5). Delayed to end of combat; the N self-damage to the controller fires even if the creature already died in combat (last-known information). Bare `SacrificeAtEndOfCombatEffect()` = sacrifice only (Fog Elemental) |
| "When this creature attacks or blocks, sacrifice it at the beginning of the next end step" | `SacrificeSelfAtEndStepEffect()` | ON_ATTACK + ON_BLOCK | Brackwater Elemental. Delayed to the **next end step** (not end of combat, so the creature survives that combat and can block/attack again if things change). Queues a `SacrificeAtEndStep` on the source; sacrifice, not destruction |
| "Whenever this creature attacks or blocks, put a -1/-1 counter on it at end of combat" | `PutMinusOneCounterOnSourceAtEndOfCombatEffect()` | ON_ATTACK + ON_BLOCK | Wicker Warcrawler. **Delayed** to end of combat (the creature is full size for combat damage) — different from the immediate `PutCountersOnSourceEffect(-1,-1,1)` used by Dusk Urchins. Add the effect to both ON_ATTACK and ON_BLOCK |
| "At end of combat, put a -0/-2 counter on each creature blocking or blocked by this creature" | `PutCounterOnCombatOpponentAtEndOfCombatEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ZERO_MINUS_TWO, 1)` in **both** ON_BLOCK and ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED (`TriggerMode.PER_BLOCKER`) | ON_BLOCK + ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED | Greater Werewolf. The combat opponent is queued a `PutCounterOnPermanentAtEndOfCombat` delayed action, applied in `CombatService.processEndOfCombatOpponentCounters`. `MINUS_ZERO_MINUS_TWO` counters subtract 2 toughness each |
| "At end of combat, if this creature attacked or blocked this combat, remove a +1/+0 counter from it" | `RemoveCounterFromSourceAtEndOfCombatEffect(CounterType.PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ZERO)` in **both** ON_ATTACK and ON_BLOCK | ON_ATTACK + ON_BLOCK | Clockwork Beast. **Delayed** to end of combat (full size for combat damage); removal-analog of Wicker Warcrawler. Scheduling only from ON_ATTACK/ON_BLOCK encodes the "attacked or blocked" condition. Drained in `CombatService.processEndOfCombatCounterRemovals`. `PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ZERO` counters add 1 power each |
| "This creature enters with seven +1/+0 counters on it" | `EnterWithCountersEffect(CounterType.PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ZERO, new Fixed(7))` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD | Clockwork Beast. `PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ZERO` counters add 1 power each (`Permanent.getEffectivePower`) |
| "{X}, {T}: Put up to X +1/+0 counters on this creature; can't raise the total above seven. Activate only during your upkeep" | `ActivatedAbility(true, "{X}", List.of(new PutCappedCountersOnSourceEffect(CounterType.PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ZERO, new XValue(), 7)), desc, ActivationTimingRestriction.ONLY_DURING_YOUR_UPKEEP)` | ACTIVATED_ABILITY | Clockwork Beast. X paid flows to `entry.getXValue()`; the cap clamps the total of that counter type |
| "Whenever CARDNAME blocks or becomes blocked by a creature, that creature gains [keyword] until end of turn" | `GrantKeywordEffect(keyword, GrantScope.TARGET)` in **both** ON_BLOCK and ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED (`TriggerMode.PER_BLOCKER`) | ON_BLOCK + ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED | Witherscale Wurm. The combat opponent is carried as the trigger's non-targeting target; a `GrantScope.TARGET` grant on ON_BLOCK auto-targets the blocked attacker (CombatBlockService), and ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED PER_BLOCKER already targets each blocker |
| "Whenever CARDNAME deals damage to an opponent, remove all -1/-1 counters from it" | `RemoveAllCountersFromSelfEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE)` | ON_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Witherscale Wurm. Any damage to a player (not just combat); the source permanent is the non-targeting sourcePermanentId |
| "Target creature you control gains hexproof until end of turn. Remove all -1/-1 counters from it." | `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.HEXPROOF, GrantScope.TARGET)` + `RemoveAllCountersFromTargetPermanentEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE)` on one `target(PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(AllOf(IsCreature, ControlledBySourceController)))` group | SPELL | Hapatra's Mark. `RemoveAllCountersFromTargetPermanentEffect` is the TARGET analog of `RemoveAllCountersFromSelfEffect` — removes every counter of the given type from the target, no-op if none |
| "Whenever CARDNAME deals N or more damage to an opponent, destroy target land that player controls" | `DestroyPermanentDamagedPlayerControlsEffect(new PermanentIsLandPredicate(), N)` | ON_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Deus of Calamity (N=6). Mandatory (no MayEffect); only fires when N+ damage was dealt. Controller chooses one matching permanent the damaged player controls to destroy. Destroy analog of `ExilePermanentDamagedPlayerControlsEffect` |
| "Whenever CARDNAME deals combat damage to a player, choose target creature that player controls. The player sacrifices that creature." | `SacrificePermanentDamagedPlayerControlsEffect(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), 0)` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Ashling, the Extinguisher. Mandatory; controller chooses one matching permanent the damaged player controls, that player sacrifices it (ignores indestructible). Sacrifice analog of `DestroyPermanentDamagedPlayerControlsEffect` |
| "Whenever CARDNAME deals damage to an opponent, you may return target card from your graveyard to your hand" | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(GraveyardChoiceDestination.HAND).targetGraveyard(true).build()` | ON_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Charnelhoard Wurm. `CombatDamageService` routes any graveyard-targeting (`targetSpec().category().isGraveyard()`) combat-damage trigger through the shared `SpellGraveyardTargetTrigger` flow — the controller picks the graveyard target as the trigger goes on the stack (drained by `AutoPassService`). The trigger path allows an empty selection, so "you may return target" reads as up-to-one (decline = 0 chosen); **no** `MayEffect` wrapper |
| "Whenever CARDNAME deals combat damage to a player, you may [targeted effect on **any** creature]" | `target(PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(PermanentIsCreaturePredicate, ...)).addEffect(ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER, new MayEffect(<permanent-targeting effect>, "..."))` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Hapatra, Vizier of Poisons ("you may put a -1/-1 counter on target creature" = `PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 1)`). Unlike the "damaged player controls" effects (which bake the defender in with a NONE target spec), a wrapped effect whose `targetSpec()` includes permanents is queued with a null target so its target (any creature) is chosen at resolution via the combat-damage may flow — see `CombatDamageService` |
| "Whenever you put one or more -1/-1 counters on a creature, create a 1/1 green Snake creature token with deathtouch" | `addEffect(ON_YOU_PUT_MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE_COUNTERS_ON_CREATURE, new CreateTokenEffect("Snake", 1, 1, CardColor.GREEN, List.of(CardSubtype.SNAKE), Set.of(Keyword.DEATHTOUCH), Set.of()))` | ON_YOU_PUT_MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE_COUNTERS_ON_CREATURE | Hapatra, Vizier of Poisons. Fires **once per creature per placement instance** regardless of how many counters were placed at once (contrast Nest of Scarabs' `ON_YOU_PUT_MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE_COUNTER_ON_CREATURE`, which fires per individual counter to make "that many"). Controller-restricted: an opponent's counters do not trigger it |
| "Whenever this creature deals combat damage to a creature, put a -1/-1 counter on that creature" + "Whenever you put one or more -1/-1 counters on a creature, each opponent loses 1 life and you gain 1 life" | `PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 1)` on `ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_CREATURE` + `LoseLifeEffect(1, EACH_OPPONENT)` + `GainLifeEffect(1)` on `ON_YOU_PUT_MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE_COUNTERS_ON_CREATURE` | both slots | Obelisk Spider. Combat slot bakes the damaged creature as non-targeting `targetId`. Drain slot is the Hapatra once-per-creature cadence (both halves share one stack entry) |
| "Enchanted/Equipped creature gets +N/+M for each [X]" | `AttachedBoostEffect(amount, amount, GrantScope.ENCHANTED_CREATURE / EQUIPPED_CREATURE)` | STATIC | Attached-scope sibling of `BoostSelfEffect` — any "for each" aura/equipment boost = `AttachedBoostEffect` + `DynamicAmount`, never a new effect class. `CountScope.CONTROLLER` = the aura/equipment's controller ("you control", CR 109.5). Blanchwood Armor (`PermanentCount(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(FOREST), CONTROLLER)`), Blackblade Reforged (`PermanentIsLandPredicate`), Wreath of Geists (`CardsInGraveyard(CREATURE, CONTROLLER)`), Bonehoard (`…, ANY_PLAYER`) |
| "Enchanted/Equipped creature gets -N/-M for each [X]" | `AttachedBoostEffect(new Scaled(amount, -1), new Scaled(amount, -1), scope)` | STATIC | Negative per-count boost. Quag Sickness (-1/-1 per Swamp you control) |
| "Equipped creature gets +1/+1 for each land ... with the same name as the exiled card" | `AttachedBoostEffect(new LandsMatchingImprintedName(), same, GrantScope.EQUIPPED_CREATURE)` | STATIC | Strata Scythe (imprint on ETB, count matching-name lands on all battlefields) |
| "CARDNAME's power and toughness are each equal to the number of lands you control" | `SetPowerToughnessToAmountEffect(a, a)` where `a = new PermanentCount(new PermanentIsLandPredicate(), CountScope.CONTROLLER)` | STATIC | Pass the same amount instance for both fields |
| "CARDNAME's power and toughness are each equal to the number of creatures you control" | `SetPowerToughnessToAmountEffect(a, a)` where `a = new PermanentCount(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), CountScope.CONTROLLER)` | STATIC | Swap the predicate/amount for other "…are each equal to the number of X" wordings: `CardsInGraveyard`, `CardsInHand`, `ControllerLifeTotal`, etc. |
| "CARDNAME's power and toughness are each equal to twice the number of creatures you control" | `SetPowerToughnessToAmountEffect(a, a)` where `a = new Scaled(new PermanentCount(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), CountScope.CONTROLLER), 2)` | STATIC | Majestic Myriarch. Counts itself → at least 2/2 on the battlefield |
| "At the beginning of each combat, this creature gains [keyword] until end of turn if you control a creature with [keyword]" | `ConditionalEffect(new ControlsPermanent(new PermanentAllOfPredicate(List.of(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), new PermanentHasKeywordPredicate(K)))), new GrantKeywordEffect(K, GrantScope.SELF))` per keyword on `EACH_BEGINNING_OF_COMBAT_TRIGGERED` | `EACH_BEGINNING_OF_COMBAT_TRIGGERED` | Majestic Myriarch. One ability with N conditional grants (all mandatory effects share one stack entry); each keyword checked at resolution. Use `EACH_BEGINNING_OF_COMBAT_TRIGGERED` (not `BEGINNING_OF_COMBAT_TRIGGERED`) so it fires on every combat |
| "As long as CARDNAME isn't attacking, its P/T equal the number of Forests you control; as long as it is attacking, they equal the number of Forests defending player controls" | `SetPowerToughnessToAmountEffect(a, a)` where `a = new IfSourceAttacking(new PermanentCount(FOREST, CountScope.DEFENDING_PLAYER), new PermanentCount(FOREST, CountScope.CONTROLLER))` | STATIC | Gaea's Liege. `IfSourceAttacking(whileAttacking, otherwise)` switches on the source's combat state; `CountScope.DEFENDING_PLAYER` = the attacked player (or attacked planeswalker's controller), evaluating to nothing when not attacking |
| "switch target creature's power and toughness" | `SwitchPowerToughnessEffect()` | SPELL | |
| "switch this creature's power and toughness" (activated ability) | `SwitchPowerToughnessEffect(true)` | ability | Self variant; no target, affects the source (e.g. Turtleshell Changeling) |
| "target creature has base power and toughness X/Y" | `SetBasePowerToughnessEffect(X, Y)` | SPELL | scope defaults to `TARGET` (until end of turn); pass a `GrantScope` (e.g. `ENCHANTED_CREATURE`) for continuous static auras |
| "this creature has base power and toughness X/Y until end of turn" (non-targeting self ability) | `SetBasePowerToughnessEffect(X, Y, GrantScope.SELF)` | ability | One-shot on the source (until EOT); no target. Marsh Flitter |
| "This creature becomes a [Subtype] with base power and toughness X/Y" (permanent, non-targeting self) — optionally "If this creature is a [Prereq], it becomes …" | `BecomeCreatureTypeWithBasePowerToughnessEffect(X, Y, CardSubtype.SUBTYPE[, CardSubtype.PREREQ])` | ability | **Indefinite** (not until EOT): adds the subtype and sets base P/T permanently. | "creatures you control have base power and toughness X/X until end of turn" | `SetAllOwnCreaturesBasePowerToughnessEffect(X, X)` | ability/SPELL | Group base-P/T set (layer 7b, modifiers apply on top). `DynamicAmount` ctor for X-cost (Mirror Entity: `new XValue()`); `int` ctor for fixed. | "put a [type] counter on target creature. The ETB effect installs it once (idempotent); the upkeep trigger just places the counter. Aven Mimeomancer (feather counter, 3/1, flying) |
| "double target creature's power and toughness" | `DoubleSelfPowerToughnessEffect()` | — | Self only |

## Keywords / abilities

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "Conspire (As you cast this spell, you may tap two untapped creatures you control that share a color with it. When you do, copy it and you may choose a new target for the copy.)" | none — nothing to add on the card; driven by the Scryfall `CONSPIRE` keyword | — | Handled entirely by the casting flow: `GameService.playCardWithConspire` validates+taps two color-sharing untapped creatures, flags the spell in `gameData.conspiredSpellIds`, and `TriggerCollectionService.checkSpellCastTriggers` queues one `CopyControllerCastSpellEffect` above the spell. Just implement the spell's normal effect(s). Test via `harness.castWithConspire(...)`. Mine Excavation |
| "each [filter] spell you cast has conspire" | `GrantConspireToSpellsEffect(CardPredicate filter)` | STATIC | grants conspire (CR 702.78) to matching spells you cast without the innate keyword; the casting flow still handles the tap/copy. Build the filter with `CardAllOfPredicate`/`CardAnyOfPredicate` of `CardTypePredicate`/`CardColorPredicate`. Wort, the Raidmother (red or green instant or sorcery) |
| "whenever this creature blocks two or more creatures, it gains [keyword] until end of turn" | `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.X, GrantScope.SELF)` in `EffectSlot.ON_BLOCKS_MULTIPLE_CREATURES` | TRIGGER | fires once (not per blocker) when the creature is declared blocking 2+ attackers; resolved against the blocker itself. Lairwatch Giant. Usually paired with `GrantAdditionalBlockEffect(1)` in STATIC |
| "target creature gains [keyword] until end of turn" | `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.X, GrantScope.TARGET)` | SPELL | default duration is `END_OF_TURN` |
| "creatures you control gain [keyword] until end of turn" | `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.X, GrantScope.OWN_CREATURES)` | SPELL | |

| "creatures your opponents control lose [keyword] until end of turn" | `RemoveKeywordEffect(Keyword.X, GrantScope.OPPONENT_CREATURES)` | SPELL | One-shot mass removal from every creature opponents control (floats a per-permanent layer-6 removal). | "all creatures lose [keyword] until end of turn. ~ deals N damage to each creature and each non-Bolas planeswalker" | `RemoveKeywordEffect(Keyword.X, GrantScope.ALL_CREATURES)` + `MassDamageEffect(N, false, false, true, Not(HasSubtype(BOLAS)))` | SPELL | Hour of Devastation. Strip first so indestructible can't save from the damage; filter excludes Bolas planeswalkers only (creatures still match `Not(BOLAS)`) |
| "creatures your opponents control lose flying if {G} was spent; creatures you control gain flying if {U} was spent" | `ConditionalEffect(new ColorSpentToCast(GREEN), new RemoveKeywordEffect(Keyword.FLYING, GrantScope.OPPONENT_CREATURES))` + `ConditionalEffect(new ColorSpentToCast(BLUE), new GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.FLYING, GrantScope.OWN_CREATURES))` | SPELL | Invert the Skies (`{3}{G/U}`). Each conditional gated on which hybrid color was spent; same shape as Moonhold |
| "target creature gains [keyword] until your next turn" | `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.X, GrantScope.TARGET, GrantDuration.UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN)` | SPELL | pass `GrantDuration` for non-default expiry |
| "target creature gets +N/+M and gains [keyword]. (This effect lasts indefinitely.)" | `BuffTargetCreatureIndefinitelyEffect(N, M, Set.of(Keyword.X))` | SPELL | Riding the Dilu Horse. Indefinite (no-duration) continuous effect (CR 611.2b) — NOT the until-EOT `BoostTargetCreatureEffect` + `GrantKeywordEffect` pair (that's Riding Red Hare). Records a `PERMANENT` floating continuous effect on the target: +N/+M in sublayer 7c, keywords in layer 6; two copies stack additively. Boost-only overload `(N, M)` omits keywords. Requires a creature target |
| "target creature gets +N/+N; if it's a [type/subtype/supertype], it also gains [keyword]" | boost effect + `GrantKeywordEffect.toTargetIf(Keyword.X, predicate)` | SPELL | the boost (or other rider) applies to any legal target; only the keyword grant is conditional on `predicate` at resolution. Vampire's Zeal (`PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(VAMPIRE)`), Blessing of Belzenlok (`PermanentHasSupertypePredicate(LEGENDARY)`). Do NOT put the predicate in `filter` — that would restrict targeting |
| "each player creates a [token] for each [permanent] they control" | `EachPlayerCreatesTokenEffect(new CreateTokenEffect(new PermanentCount(filter, CountScope.CONTROLLER), name, p, t, color, subtypes, Set.of(), Set.of()))` | SPELL | Waiting in the Weeds — each player (turn order) creates the wrapped token under their own control; the token's `CONTROLLER`-scoped amount is re-evaluated per creating player (like `EachPlayerDrawsCardEffect`), so it reads each player's own board (untapped Forests = `PermanentAllOfPredicate(FOREST subtype, NOT tapped)`) |
| "create a ... token. Keep innate keywords separate from the granted set. Use this when the grant is *unconditional*; for a conditional grant on those same tokens use `GrantScope.TOKENS_CREATED_THIS_RESOLUTION` (next row) |
| "create N ... tokens. Clash with an opponent. If you win, those creatures gain [keyword] until end of turn" | `CreateTokenEffect(N, ...)` + `ClashEffect(new GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.X, GrantScope.TOKENS_CREATED_THIS_RESOLUTION))` (both `SPELL`) | SPELL | Gilt-Leaf Ambush. The token-creation handler records the new tokens on `StackEntry.createdPermanentIds`; `GrantScope.TOKENS_CREATED_THIS_RESOLUTION` grants the keyword to exactly those tokens (created earlier in the same resolution), so the grant is conditional (only on the clash win) unlike `grantedKeywordsUntilEndOfTurn` |
| "enchanted creature has [keyword]" | `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.X, GrantScope.ENCHANTED_CREATURE)` | STATIC | |
| "As long as enchanted creature is [colour], it has 'Whenever this creature deals damage to an opponent, [effect]'" | `EnchantedPermanentConditionalEffect(new PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(colour)), triggerEffect, null)` in `EffectSlot.ON_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER` | aura trigger | Helm of the Ghastlord (SHM): blue → `DrawCardEffect()`, black → `DiscardEffect(1, DiscardRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER, false)`. `checkAttachedCombatDamageToPlayerTriggers` in `CombatDamageService` unwraps the `EnchantedPermanentConditionalEffect` against the enchanted creature that dealt the damage, so the granted trigger only fires on the matching branch. Pair each with a `StaticBoostEffect(1, 1, GrantScope.ENCHANTED_CREATURE, colourPredicate)` for the "+1/+1" clause (Steel of the Godhead pattern). Only combat damage collects `ON_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER` for attached auras |
| "equipped creature has [keyword]" | `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.X, GrantScope.EQUIPPED_CREATURE)` | STATIC | |
| "Banding" (innate) | none — auto-loaded from the Scryfall `BANDING` keyword; nothing to add on a vanilla bander | — | Fully modeled (CR 702.22): band declaration (`declareAttackers` takes an optional `bands` list of attacker-index groups; each band needs ≥1 banding + ≤1 non-banding, all attacking the same target), band shared-blocking (702.22h — blocking one band member blocks the whole band, applied in `CombatBlockService`), and the two combat-damage reversals (702.22j: a banding blocker → the **defending** player assigns the attacker's damage; 702.22k: a blocker blocking a banding attacker → the **active** player divides the blocker's damage). All handled in `service/combat/`. "Bands with other" is NOT modeled. Timber Wolves, Pikemen, etc. |
| "target creature/this creature gains/Walls you control have banding" | grant via `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.BANDING, scope)` exactly like any keyword | ACTIVATED/STATIC/TRIGGER | Helm of Chatzuk (`GrantScope.TARGET`), Fortified Area (`GrantScope.OWN_CREATURES` + Wall predicate, STATIC), Battering Ram (`GrantScope.SELF` in `BEGINNING_OF_COMBAT_TRIGGERED`), Urza's Avenger (banding is one option in `GrantChosenKeywordToSelfEffect`) |
| "other [subtype] creatures you control have [keyword]" | `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.X, GrantScope.OWN_CREATURES, predicate)` | STATIC | |
| "each creature you control with [property] has [keyword]" (includes this source if it matches) | `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.X, GrantScope.ALL_OWN_CREATURES, predicate)` | STATIC | Use `ALL_OWN_CREATURES` (not `OWN_CREATURES`) when the source itself should also gain the keyword if it passes the filter. Bramblewood Paragon (TRAMPLE + `PermanentHasCountersPredicate(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE)`). The source-self grant is applied by `GrantKeywordSelfEffectHandler` |
| "wither" (native or granted) | `Keyword.WITHER` (auto-loaded from Scryfall; grant via `GrantKeywordEffect`) | keyword | Damage this source deals to a creature is dealt as -1/-1 counters (like infect vs creatures), but damage to players is normal life loss (NOT poison). Engine decides via `GameQueryService.dealsCounterDamageToCreatures` (= INFECT or WITHER). Corrosive Mentor grants it as a color lord |
| "all damage is dealt as though its source had wither" | `AllDamageDealtWithWitherEffect()` | STATIC | Everlasting Torment. Global — every source deals creature damage as -1/-1 counters (player damage stays normal). Pairs with `PlayersCantGainLifeEffect()` + `DamageCantBePreventedEffect()` on that card |
| "If a source you control would deal noncombat damage to a creature an opponent controls, put that many -1/-1 counters on that creature instead" | `NoncombatDamageToOpponentCreaturesAsMinusCountersEffect()` | STATIC | Soul-Scar Mage. Only noncombat damage from your sources to opponents' creatures (combat unaffected). Pair with prowess via `SpellCastTriggerEffect` on `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL` |
| "If one or more -1/-1 counters would be put on a creature you control, that many -1/-1 counters minus one are put on it instead" | `ReduceMinusOneMinusOneCountersEffect()` | STATIC | Vizier of Remedies. Replacement marker on the source; every -1/-1 placement site routes its count through `GameQueryService.reduceMinusOneMinusOneCounters` and subtracts one per marker the affected creature's controller controls (floored at zero). Covers spell/ability counters, wither/infect damage, proliferate, enters-with, persist, put-counter costs (Devoted Druid combo). Multiple copies stack |

Protection not modelled |

## Destruction / sacrifice

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "destroy target [permanent type]" | `DestroyTargetPermanentEffect(false)` | SPELL | + PermanentPredicate filter |
| "Destroy target nonland permanent and all other permanents with the same name as that permanent" | `DestroyTargetNonlandPermanentAndAllWithSameNameEffect()` | SPELL | Maelstrom Pulse. Card supplies the `PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentIsLandPredicate)` nonland target filter; the effect destroys the target plus every same-name permanent across all battlefields (regeneration/indestructible respected). Destroy analog of `ExileTargetCreatureAndAllWithSameNameEffect` |
| "destroy target creature. It can't be regenerated" | `DestroyTargetPermanentEffect(true)` | SPELL | cantRegenerate=true |
| "Destroy target [filter] creature. It can't be regenerated. Create a black Spirit token whose power/toughness equal that creature's. Sacrifice the token at the beginning of the next end step" | `DestroyTargetCreatureAndCreateSpiritCopyToSacrificeEffect()` | SPELL | Broken Visage. Card supplies the target filter (`PermanentIsAttackingPredicate` + non-artifact). Token created even if the target is indestructible |
| "destroy target attacking creature. You gain life equal to its power" | `GainLifeEffect(new TargetPower())` + `DestroyTargetPermanentEffect(false)` | SPELL | target = `PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(PermanentIsAttackingPredicate)`; gain life FIRST so power is read before destruction (Chastise) |
| "destroy target creature. Its owner gains N life" | `DestroyTargetPermanentThenEffect(new GainLifeEffect(N), ThenEffectRecipient.TARGET_OWNER)` | SPELL | target = creature filter; `TARGET_OWNER` routes life to the creature's owner (not current controller — differs only for stolen creatures). | "destroy target artifact. It can't be regenerated. Regeneration/indestructible apply. |

| "at the beginning of your upkeep, ~ deals N damage to you unless you pay {cost}" | `ForcedCostOrElseEffect(PayManaCost("{cost}"), List.of(DealDamageToPlayersEffect(N, DamageRecipient.CONTROLLER)), true)` | UPKEEP_TRIGGERED | Force of Nature (`{G}{G}{G}{G}`, 8 damage) — `PayManaCost` is the payable side of `ForcedCostOrElseEffect` (`optional=true`, always prompts "you may pay"); accepting charges the mana, declining or being unable to pay resolves the fallback penalty |

| "At the beginning of your upkeep, put a +1/+1 counter on this creature. Then you may pay {X}, where X is the number of +1/+1 counters on it. ## Bounce / tuck

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "return target [permanent] to its owner's hand" | `ReturnToHandEffect.target()` | SPELL | + card `target(...)` filter; `.targetAndControllerLosesLife(1)` for "its controller loses 1 life" (Vapor Snag); `.targetAndControllerDraws(1)` for "its controller draws a card" (Call to Heel) |
| "return all creatures to their owners' hands" | `ReturnToHandEffect.allPermanentsMatching(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate())` | SPELL | Mass bounce (null filter = every permanent) |
| "return this permanent to its owner's hand" | `ReturnToHandEffect.self()` | ability/trigger | Self-bounce |
| "return [this spell] to its owner's hand" | `ReturnToHandEffect.selfSpell()` | SPELL | The resolving instant/sorcery returns itself to hand off the stack (instead of graveyard); sets `returnToHandAfterResolving`. Redeem the Lost (MOR): `ClashEffect(ReturnToHandEffect.selfSpell())` as a won-clash reward |
| "return all permanents target player controls to their owners' hands" | `ReturnToHandEffect.permanentsTargetPlayerControls(filter)` | SPELL | River's Rebuke |
| "Whenever a permanent is returned to a player's hand, that player discards a card" | `new DiscardEffect(1, DiscardRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER, false)` | `ON_ANY_PERMANENT_RETURNED_TO_HAND` | Global watcher fired from the `PermanentRemovalService.removePermanentToHand` choke point (`TriggerCollectionService.checkPermanentReturnedToHandTriggers`); fires once per returned permanent across all battlefields. The owner the permanent returned to is the non-targeting `targetId`, so `TARGET_PLAYER` effects act on "that player". Warped Devotion |
| "return all artifacts target player owns to their hand" | `ReturnToHandEffect.permanentsTargetPlayerOwns(new PermanentIsArtifactPredicate())` | SPELL | Owner-based (Hurkyl's Recall) |
| "Return all permanents to their owners' hands. Each player chooses up to seven cards in their hand, then shuffles the rest into their library. Each player loses all unspent mana." | `ReturnToHandEffect.allPermanentsMatching(null)` + `EachPlayerKeepsCardsShufflesRestIntoLibraryEffect(7)` + `EachPlayerLosesUnspentManaEffect()` | SPELL ×3 | Worldpurge (SHM). The keep-choice is interactive per player (APNAP order); the mana-loss step resumes after all players choose |
| "put target [permanent] on top of its owner's library" | `PutTargetOnTopOfLibraryEffect()` | SPELL | |
| "{cost}: Put this [Aura/permanent] on top of its owner's library" | `PutTargetOnTopOfLibraryEffect.self()` | ability | Bounces the source permanent to the top of its owner's library. Soaring Hope |
| "When this creature enters, put a creature you control on top of its owner's library" | `PutControlledCreatureOnTopOfLibraryEffect()` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD | Nulltread Gargantuan. **Non-targeted** — the creature is chosen as the ability resolves (self is a legal choice; forced to top itself when it's the only creature you control). One candidate → auto-resolved; several → `PutControlledCreatureOnTopOfLibrary` permanent choice. No card `target(...)` filter |
| "put target [permanent] on the bottom of its owner's library" | `PutTargetOnBottomOfLibraryEffect()` | SPELL | |
| "Put target card from your graveyard on the bottom of your library" | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BOTTOM_OF_OWNERS_LIBRARY).targetGraveyard(true).build()` | SPELL or ability | Mistveil Plains. Targets a card in the controller's graveyard; owner-of-library resolved at resolution time |
| "(you may) put target card from your graveyard on top of your library" (ETB/trigger) | `MayEffect(ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(TOP_OF_OWNERS_LIBRARY).build())` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD / trigger | Hag Hedge-Mage. The ETB pipeline has no graveyard-target selector for this effect, so leave `targetGraveyard` false → resolution-time search-and-choose from the controller's own graveyard (identical in practice). The search-and-choose `GraveyardChoice` supports `TOP_OF_OWNERS_LIBRARY` / `BOTTOM_OF_OWNERS_LIBRARY` destinations (handled in `GraveyardChoiceHandlerService`), not just HAND/BATTLEFIELD |
| "Return target permanent to its owner's hand. If that permanent is [predicate], put it on top of its owner's library instead" | `ReturnTargetPermanentToHandOrLibraryTopByPredicateEffect(predicate)` | SPELL | Consign to Dream — destination-replacement bounce: the target goes to hand, or to the top of its owner's library when it matches the predicate (Consign uses `PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(RED, GREEN))`). Not additive — one destination or the other |
| "Clash with an opponent, then return target creature to its owner's hand. If you win, you may put that creature on top of its owner's library instead." | `ClashEffect(null)` + `ConditionalEffect(new WonClash(), new MayEffect(new PutTargetOnTopOfLibraryEffect(), prompt))` + `ReturnToHandEffect.target()` | SPELL | Whirlpool Whelm (LRW). Order matters: the bare clash records its result (read by `WonClash`); on a win the optional tuck resolves **before** the trailing bounce, so accepting puts the creature on top of its library (the bounce then no-ops) while declining/losing falls through to the bounce — the "instead" replacement |

## Counter spells

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "Exile all other spells and counter all abilities" | `ExileOtherSpellsAndCounterAbilitiesEffect()` | SPELL | Summary Dismissal. Non-targeting. Exiles every other spell still on the stack (including uncounterable — exile is not a counter event, so Guile does not apply). Counters all activated/triggered abilities on the stack (respects uncounterable / color-protection). Resolving spell is already off the stack |
| "counter target spell" | `CounterSpellEffect()` | SPELL | Targeting auto-derived |
| "Counter up to two target spells" | `target(null, 0, 2).addEffect(SPELL, new CounterEachTargetSpellEffect())` | SPELL | Double Negative. One 0–2 spell-on-stack target group (`null` filter = any spell); the each-target effect counters every spell chosen for its group (mirrors `DealDamageToEachTargetEffect`). Chosen spells ride in the flat `targetIds` list; the non-modal multi-spell-target path is gated by `SpellCastingService`'s `multipleSpellTargets` (`!wasModal && !unwrappedNeedsTarget && getMaxTargets() > 1`) and validated by `TargetLegalityService.validateMultiSpellTargetsOnStack` (0..max distinct spells) |
| "Counter target spell with mana value X" (`{X}{U}` instant) | `target(new StackEntryPredicateTargetFilter(new StackEntryManaValueEqualsXPredicate(), msg))` + `CounterSpellEffect()` | SPELL | Spell Blast. The chosen X is threaded through the cast-time stack-target check; the spell is a legal target only if its mana value equals X |
| "When this creature enters, counter target spell with mana value X or less, where X is the number of [type] you control" | `target(new StackEntryPredicateTargetFilter(new StackEntryManaValueAtMostControlledCountPredicate(new PermanentHasAnySubtypePredicate(Set.of(subtype))), msg))` + `CounterSpellEffect()` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD | Spellstutter Sprite. The ETB spell-target pipeline (`ETBSpellTargetTrigger`) chooses the spell as the ability goes on the stack; when the effect's spec is only `SPELL_ON_STACK`, it reads the legal-spell restriction from the card's `StackEntryPredicateTargetFilter`. Faerie count includes the source |

| "As this creature enters, it becomes your choice of a 3/3 …, a 2/2 … with flying, or a 1/6 Wall … with defender." | `addEffect(ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD, new ChoosePrimalClayFormOnEnterEffect())` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD | Primal Clay (a `*/*` artifact creature). Card-specific modal "becomes" choice: `StackResolutionService.resolveArtifactSpell` prompts a `ChoiceContext.PrimalClayFormChoice`; when it resolves, `ChoiceHandlerService.handlePrimalClayFormChoice` stamps the chosen `PrimalClayForm`'s base P/T (durable `permanentBasePowerOverride`/`permanentBaseToughnessOverride`, layered 7b), keyword (durable `Permanent.persistentGrantedKeywords` — survives `resetModifiers`, seeded by the layered pass like `grantedSubtypes`), and Wall subtype (durable `grantedSubtypes`). Use `persistentGrantedKeywords` for any "as it enters/becomes" keyword that must outlive the turn |
| "As this creature enters, choose a number between 0 and 7. At the beginning of your upkeep, you may choose a number between 0 and 7. CARDNAME's power is equal to the last chosen number and its toughness is equal to 7 minus that number." | `addEffect(ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD, new ChooseNumberOnEnterEffect(0, 7))` + `addEffect(UPKEEP_TRIGGERED, new MayEffect(new ChooseNumberEffect(0, 7), "…?"))` + `addEffect(STATIC, new SetPowerToughnessToAmountEffect(new ChosenNumberOnSource(), new Sum(new Fixed(7), new Scaled(new ChosenNumberOnSource(), -1))))` | mixed | Shapeshifter. The chosen number is stored on the permanent (`Permanent.getChosenNumber()`, default 0); the CDA reads it via the `ChosenNumberOnSource` amount (power = N, toughness = 7 − N via `Sum(Fixed(7), Scaled(ChosenNumberOnSource, -1))`).
