| "Choose an artifact card name. Search target opponent's graveyard, hand, and library for any number of cards with the chosen name and exile them. Then that player shuffles." | `ChooseCardNameAndExileFromZonesEffect(List.of(), CardType.ARTIFACT)` + `target(PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT))` | SPELL | Dispossess (AKH). `requiredType = ARTIFACT` restricts the offered names to artifact card names; the card-level opponent filter enforces "target opponent". "Any number" = the controller picks 0..N of the matching copies to exile |
| "Choose a nonland card name. Target player reveals their hand. [Source] deals 3 damage to that player for each card with the chosen name revealed this way. Search that player's graveyard, hand, and library for all cards with that name and exile them. Then that player shuffles." | `ChooseNameRevealHandDamagePerCopyAndExileEffect(List.of(CardType.LAND), 3)` | SPELL | Thought Hemorrhage (ARB). Damage counts only the copies revealed **from hand**; the exile is mandatory (all copies, no "any number" choice — unlike Memoricide's `ChooseCardNameAndExileFromZonesEffect`) |
| "Counter target spell. You may shuffle up to one target card from your graveyard into your library." | `CounterSpellEffect()` + `ShuffleCardFromControllerGraveyardIntoLibraryEffect(null)` | SPELL + SPELL | Put Away (SHM). Counter is the cast-time spell target; the graveyard shuffle is a resolution-time optional single-card choice from the controller's own graveyard (may decline) |
| "{cost}: You may cast a spell from your hand without paying its mana cost if it has the same name as a spell that was cast this turn" | `MayCastFromHandSharingNameWithSpellCastThisTurnEffect()` | activated ability | Twinning Glass (`{1}, {T}`). Reuses the Counterlash routing: queues a per-card PendingMayAbility (`MayCastFromHandWithoutPayingManaCostEffect`) for each nonland hand card whose name matches a spell **any** player cast this turn; casting one clears the rest |
| "this spell can't be countered" | `CantBeCounteredEffect()` | STATIC | Optional `CantBeCounteredEffect(condition)` makes it conditional on the stack entry (Banefire's `new SpellXAtLeast(5)`) |
| "Creature spells can't be countered" | `CreatureSpellsCantBeCounteredEffect()` | STATIC | Gaea's Herald — every creature spell, any controller |
| "Creature spells you control with power N or greater can't be countered" | `ControllerCreatureSpellsCantBeCounteredEffect(N)` | STATIC | Spellbreaker Behemoth (N=5). Only the controller's creature spells of power ≥ N; pair with `CantBeCounteredEffect()` for the source's own spell, which this static can't protect |
| "return target spell [you don't control] to its owner's hand" | `ReturnTargetSpellToHandEffect()` | SPELL / trigger | Not countering — uncounterable spells still bounce. Pair with a `StackEntryNotPredicate(StackEntryControlledByPredicate())` filter for "you don't control". Hullbreaker Horror (via modal trigger) |
| "Target spell can't be countered" | `MakeTargetSpellUncounterableEffect()` | activated ability (no target filter — the `SPELL_ON_STACK` spec auto-derives "any spell on the stack") | Vexing Shusher (`{R/G}`). Marks the target spell's card id in `GameData.spellsMadeUncounterable`, read back by `GameQueryService.isUncounterable` |
| "If a spell or ability you control would counter a spell, instead exile that spell and you may play that card without paying its mana cost" | `ReplaceControlledCounterWithExileAndPlayEffect()` | STATIC | Guile. Intercepts every counter effect the permanent's controller controls (in `CounterSupport`); exiles the spell and queues a `MayPlayExiledCounteredCardEffect` free-play. Only spells, not abilities; uncounterable spells unaffected |
| "This creature can't be blocked except by three or more creatures" | `CantBeBlockedByFewerThanNCreaturesEffect(3)` | STATIC | Generalized menace (validated in CombatBlockService). Menace itself = minBlockers 2; use this effect for other minimums (Guile = 3) |
| "This creature can't be blocked as long as it's attacking alone" | `CantBeBlockedIfAttackingAloneEffect()` | STATIC | Dream Prowler. Unblockable only when it's the sole declared attacker (validated in CombatBlockService/GameQueryService) |
| "This creature can't be blocked except by black creatures" | `CanBeBlockedOnlyByFilterEffect(new PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(CardColor.BLACK)), "black creatures")` | STATIC | Fear-style per-creature evasion (Dread Warlock). Validated in `GameQueryService.getBlockRestriction` |
| "This creature can't be blocked by creatures with horsemanship" | `CantBeBlockedByCreaturesMatchingPredicateEffect(new PermanentHasKeywordPredicate(Keyword.HORSEMANSHIP))` | STATIC | Negative evasion (Taoist Mystic). Blockers matching the predicate can't block this creature. Validated in `GameQueryService.getBlockingIllegalityReason` |
| "Cowards can't block Warriors" | `MatchingCreaturesCantBlockMatchingCreaturesEffect(new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(COWARD), new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(WARRIOR), "Cowards can't block Warriors")` | STATIC | Boldwyr Intimidator. Global board-wide restriction: any blocker matching the first predicate can't block any attacker matching the second. Validated in `GameQueryService.getBlockRestriction` |
| "Target creature blocks this turn if able" | `MustBlockThisTurnIfAbleEffect()` + creature `TargetFilter` | ability/SPELL | Nacatl Hunt-Pride (`{G}, {T}`). General "must block if able" with no specific attacker (unlike Provoke's `MustBlockSourceEffect`). Sets `Permanent.mustBlockThisTurnIfAble`; the target must be declared as a blocker of some attacker if it can legally block any. Enforced in `CombatBlockService.validateMustBlockIfAbleRequirements`, cleared at end of turn |
| "Creatures your opponents control with counters on them can't attack or block" | `MatchingCreaturesCantAttackOrBlockEffect(new PermanentAllOfPredicate(List.of(new PermanentNotPredicate(new PermanentControlledBySourceControllerPredicate()), new PermanentHasCountersPredicate(CounterType.ANY))), "…")` | STATIC | Kulrath Knight. Global: creatures matching the predicate can't attack OR block. Predicate is source-controller-relative (so `PermanentControlledBySourceControllerPredicate` = "you"; `PermanentNotPredicate(...)` = "your opponents"). Enforced in `CombatAttackService` (attack) + `GameQueryService` (block) |
| "Black creatures can't attack or block" | `MatchingCreaturesCantAttackOrBlockEffect(new PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(CardColor.BLACK)), "Black creatures can't attack or block")` | STATIC | Light of Day. Global board-wide restriction: any creature matching the predicate (either player's) can't attack and can't block. Attack side in `CombatAttackService`, block side in `GameQueryService.canBlock`. Swap the predicate for other "[X] creatures can't attack or block" cards |
| "Target creature becomes a Coward until end of turn" (no "in addition") | `TargetCreatureBecomesSubtypeUntilEndOfTurnEffect(CardSubtype.COWARD)` | ability | Type-**replacing** (overwrites all creature types, CR rulings). Boldwyr Intimidator. Sets `Permanent.transientCreatureTypeOverride`; contrast additive/permanent `GrantSubtypeToTargetCreatureEffect` |
| "Until end of turn, this creature becomes a[n] [type], gets +X/+X, and gains [keywords]" | `SourceBecomesSubtypeUntilEndOfTurnEffect(CardSubtype.X)` + `BoostSelfEffect(X, X)` + `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.Y, GrantScope.SELF)` per keyword | ability | Self (no target), type-**replacing** (loses other creature types, CR rulings). Paragon of the Amesha (becomes an Angel, +3/+3, flying + lifelink). Self analog of `TargetCreatureBecomesSubtypeUntilEndOfTurnEffect` |
| "Black creatures you control can't be blocked this turn except by black creatures" | `GrantCanBeBlockedOnlyByFilterToOwnCreaturesEffect(new PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(CardColor.BLACK)), new PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(CardColor.BLACK)), "black creatures")` | SPELL | Dread Charge. Grants the `CanBeBlockedOnlyByFilterEffect` restriction to each matching own creature until end of turn (transient on `Permanent`, cleared by `resetModifiers`). First filter = which of your creatures; second = allowed blockers |

## Draw / discard

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "draw N cards" / "draw a card" | `DrawCardEffect(N)` | SPELL/trigger | |
| "Draw a card and reveal it. If it isn't a land card, discard it." | `DrawCardRevealDiscardUnlessLandEffect()` | activated ability | Sindbad (`{T}:`). Draws + reveals (public); non-land drawn card is discarded (own discard; fires discard triggers). Card-filtering — only lands kept |
| "draw X cards" | `DrawCardEffect(new XValue())` | SPELL | X-cost |
| "As an additional cost to cast this spell, pay X life. Draw X cards." | `PayXLifeDrawXCardsEffect()` | SPELL | Necrologia. Single resolution-time X choice: pick X (≤ current life), pay X life, draw X. Pair with `setSpellCastTimingRestriction(YOUR_END_STEP)` |
| "draw a card for each creature you control" | `DrawCardEffect(new PermanentCount(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), CountScope.CONTROLLER))` | trigger/ability | Tishana; Slate of Ancestry (activated, `DiscardHandCost` cost) |
| "draw a card for each creature card in your graveyard" | `DrawCardEffect(new CardsInGraveyard(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), CountScope.CONTROLLER))` | SPELL | Grim Flowering |
| "draw a card for each charge counter on [source]" | `DrawCardEffect(new CountersOnSource(CounterType.CHARGE))` | ability | Culling Dais; survives sacrifice via sourcePermanentSnapshot |
| "Target opponent reveals their hand. You draw a card for each [subtype] and [color] card in it" | `RevealTargetHandDrawPerMatchingCardEffect(List.of(CardSubtype.MOUNTAIN), List.of(CardColor.RED))` + `target(PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT))` | SPELL | Baleful Stare; each card counted once |
| "Target opponent reveals their hand. You choose a [color] creature card from it. You gain life equal to that creature card's toughness, then that player discards that card" | `RevealHandChooseCreatureGainLifeDiscardEffect(List.of(CardColor.GREEN, CardColor.WHITE))` + `target(PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT))` | SPELL | Talara's Bane. Reuses the `RevealedHandChoice` discard flow (discard mode + `gainLifeToChooserEqualToChosenToughness`); the chooser gains life before the opponent-caused discard. Empty color list = any color |
| "Choose a creature type. Draw a card for each permanent you control of that type" | `DrawCardPerChosenTypeCountEffect()` | SPELL | Distant Melody. Prompts a resolution-time creature-type choice (stored on `GameData.chosenSpellSubtype`), then draws = count of the controller's permanents of that type (Changeling-aware). Same two-phase flow as `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEqualToChosenTypeCountEffect` |
| "Choose a creature type. You gain N life for each permanent you control of that type" | `GainLifePerChosenTypeCountEffect(N)` | SPELL | Luminescent Rain. Prompts a resolution-time creature-type choice (stored on `GameData.chosenSpellSubtype`), then gains `count*N` life (Changeling-aware). Life sibling of `DrawCardPerChosenTypeCountEffect` |
| "Choose a creature type. Target creature gets -1/-1 until end of turn for each permanent of the chosen type you control" | `BoostTargetCreaturePerChosenTypeCountEffect(-1, -1)` | SPELL | Pack's Disdain. Prompts a resolution-time creature-type choice (stored on `GameData.chosenSpellSubtype`), then applies `count*powerPer`/`count*toughnessPer` until end of turn (Changeling-aware). Boost sibling of `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEqualToChosenTypeCountEffect`; give it a `PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(PermanentIsCreaturePredicate)` |
| "draw cards equal to the number of cards target opponent discarded this turn" | `DrawCardEffect(new CardsDiscardedByTargetPlayerThisTurn())` | SPELL | Dream Salvage. **Controller** draws; pair with `target(PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT))`. `DrawCardEffect`'s spec targets a player only for this target-relative amount. Discards tracked in `GameData.cardsDiscardedThisTurn` (any discard, any source), cleared each turn |
| "target player draws N cards" | `DrawCardForTargetPlayerEffect(N)` | SPELL | For explicit `target(player…)` groups use the 3-arg `DrawCardForTargetPlayerEffect(N, false, true)` so the group advertises a player target (unless another effect in the group already targets a player via its spec) |
| "target player draws X cards" | `DrawCardForTargetPlayerEffect(new XValue(), false, true)` | SPELL | Blue Sun's Zenith |
| "target player draws 2ˣ cards" | `DrawTwoToTheXCardsForTargetPlayerEffect()` | SPELL | 2^X from stack xValue; target a player. Mathemagics |
| "each player draws N cards" | `EachPlayerDrawsCardEffect(N)` | SPELL | |
| "each player draws a card for each creature card in their graveyard" | `EachPlayerDrawsCardEffect(new CardsInGraveyard(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), CountScope.CONTROLLER))` | SPELL | Nature's Resurgence. The amount is re-evaluated per drawing player (`CONTROLLER` scope = that player's own objects), so player-relative counts work; fixed/X amounts are unaffected |
| "At the beginning of each player's draw step, that player puts the cards in their hand on the bottom of their library in any order, then draws that many cards" | `PutHandOnBottomOfLibraryAndDrawEffect()` | EACH_DRAW_TRIGGERED | Teferi's Puzzle Box; acts on `entry.getTargetId()` (the draw-step player) |

Reveals whole hand, random discard restricted to the type; pair with `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT)` |
| "target player reveals a card at random from their hand, then loses life equal to that card's mana value" | `RevealRandomCardFromTargetPlayerHandLoseLifeEqualToManaValueEffect()` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD | Singe-Mind Ogre; pair with `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(ANY)`. Reveal + life loss is atomic (the amount is the revealed card's mana value); empty hand = no reveal, no loss |
| "Target opponent may pay 10 life. If that player doesn't, they reveal a card at random from their hand. Exchange ownership of the revealed card and ~. Put the revealed card into your hand and ~ into that player's graveyard" (ante) | `TempestEfreetAnteExchangeEffect(10)` | activated ability | Tempest Efreet ({T}, `SacrificeSelfCost`); pair with `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT)`. Payable opponent gets a may-pay-life prompt, else the exchange happens. Ante "permanent ownership change" is out of single-game scope — resolved as zone movements only, no runtime `ownerId` change |
| "Exile ~ and target nontoken permanent an opponent owns. That player may pay 10 life. If they do, put this card into its owner's graveyard. Otherwise, that player owns this card and you own the other exiled card" (ante) | `BronzeTabletAnteExchangeEffect(10)` | activated ability | Bronze Tablet ({4}, {T}); pair with `PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(PermanentAllOfPredicate[nontoken, not owned by source controller])`. Both cards are exiled unconditionally; the permanent's owner gets a may-pay-life prompt — pay → source moves from exile to its owner's graveyard, else the ante swap leaves both exiled. Ante ownership change is out of single-game scope — zone movements only, no runtime `ownerId` change |
| "Each player may ante the top card of their library. If a player does, that player's life total becomes 20" (ante) | `RebirthAnteEffect()` | SPELL | Rebirth (non-targeting). Seeds an accept/decline prompt per player (APNAP, active first; empty-library players skipped); accepting antes that player's top card and sets their life to 20. Ante is out of single-game scope — the anted card is removed from the game (moved to exile), the same approximation as Tempest Efreet |
| "target player loses 1 life and reveals their hand" | `LoseLifeEffect(1, LoseLifeRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)` + `RevealTargetHandEffect()` | activated ability | Thoughtcutter Agent ({U}{B}, {T}); both effects act on the ability's targeted player. `RevealTargetHandEffect` just logs the whole hand |
| "each player discards N cards" | `DiscardEffect(N, DiscardRecipient.EACH_PLAYER)` | SPELL | APNAP order; `EACH_PLAYER` + `random=true` for Burning Inquiry |

| "destroy target creature. If that creature was green or white, its controller discards a card" | `ConditionalEffect(TargetPermanentMatches(PermanentColorInPredicate(...)), DiscardEffect(1, DiscardRecipient.TARGET_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER))` + `DestroyTargetPermanentEffect()` | SPELL | Gloomlance. `TARGET_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER` = the controller of the *targeted permanent* discards; list the discard **before** the destroy so the creature (and its colour/controller) is still on the battlefield |
| "deals 5 damage to target red creature or red planeswalker. If that permanent is a Chandra planeswalker, you may discard a card. If you do, draw a card." | `DealDamageToTargetCreatureOrPlaneswalkerEffect(5, PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(RED)))` + `ConditionalEffect(new TargetPermanentMatches(PermanentAllOfPredicate(IsPlaneswalker, HasSubtype(CHANDRA))), new MayEffect(new DiscardAndDrawCardEffect(), prompt))` | SPELL ×2 | Chandra's Defeat. Damage effect's `targetRestriction` enforces "red"; the loot half is a resolution-time intervening-if on the shared target (list it after the damage) |
| "destroy target nongreen creature. Its controller loses N life if you've cast another black spell this turn" | `ConditionalEffect(new ControllerCastAnotherSpellThisTurn(new CardColorPredicate(BLACK)), new LoseLifeEffect(N, LoseLifeRecipient.TARGET_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER))` + `DestroyTargetPermanentEffect()` | SPELL | Soul Reap. `LoseLifeRecipient.TARGET_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER` = the controller of the *targeted permanent* loses life (fires "loses life" triggers via `applyLifeLoss`); list the life loss **before** the destroy so the creature (and its controller) is still on the battlefield. Nongreen target = `PermanentAllOfPredicate(PermanentIsCreaturePredicate, PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentColorInPredicate({GREEN})))` |
| "each player discards their hand" / "discard your hand" | `DiscardHandEffect(DiscardRecipient)` (no-arg = controller) | SPELL/trigger/saga | Whole hand, no count or choice; APNAP order for each-player. Mindslicer (`EACH_PLAYER`, ON_DEATH), The Flame of Keld (`CONTROLLER`) |
| "Whenever ~ deals damage to an opponent, that player discards their hand." | `DiscardHandEffect(DiscardRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)` | ON_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Nicol Bolas (DRB). `TARGET_PLAYER` implements `CombatDamageTriggerContextEffect` (`DAMAGED_PLAYER`), so CombatDamageService bakes the damaged player as `targetId`; no `target(...)` needed |
| "counter target spell if it's red" | `ConditionalEffect(new TargetSpellMatches(new StackEntryColorInPredicate(Set.of(CardColor.RED))), new CounterSpellEffect())` | SPELL | Hydroblast mode 0. "if it's red" is NOT a targeting restriction — any spell is a legal target; the counter is a resolution-time intervening-if. Contrast Red Elemental Blast ("counter target blue spell"), which *does* restrict targeting via a `StackEntryPredicateTargetFilter`. Pyroblast is the mirror with `CardColor.BLUE` |
| "destroy target permanent if it's red" | `ConditionalEffect(new TargetPermanentMatches(new PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(CardColor.RED))), new DestroyTargetPermanentEffect())` | SPELL | Hydroblast mode 1. Any permanent is a legal target; the color check is a resolution-time intervening-if |
| "destroy target creature if it has the least power or is tied for least power among creatures on the battlefield" | `ConditionalEffect(new TargetPermanentMatches(new PermanentHasLeastPowerAmongAllCreaturesPredicate()), new DestroyTargetPermanentEffect())` + creature target filter | SPELL | Wretched Banquet. Any creature is a legal target; the least-power check is a resolution-time intervening-if (ties allowed, across every player's battlefield) |
| "target player discards their hand unless they pay N life" | `DiscardHandUnlessPaysLifeEffect(N)` via `target(new PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(new PlayerRelationPredicate(PlayerRelation.ANY), ...))` | SPELL | Tyrannize (7 life). Target player chooses pay-life vs discard-whole-hand; can't-pay auto-discards |
| "Target player reveals N cards from their hand. You choose M of them. That player discards those cards." | `TargetRevealsCardsControllerChoosesDiscardEffect(N[, M])` | SPELL | Blackmail (reveal 3, choose 1 — M defaults to 1); Noggin Whack (reveal 3, choose 2). Target picks which N to reveal (whole hand if fewer); controller sees only those and picks M to discard (fewer if the hand held fewer). player-targeting spec — no explicit `target(...)` needed |
| "look at target player's hand" | `LookAtHandEffect()` | SPELL | |
| "Look at target player's hand and choose X cards from it. That player discards those cards." | `ChooseCardsFromTargetHandEffect(new XValue(), List.of(), HandChoiceDestination.DISCARD)` | SPELL | Mind Warp (`{X}{3}{B}`). `count` is a `DynamicAmount`, so `XValue()` reads the cast-time X; caster looks at the whole hand and picks X (capped to hand size), that player discards them. player-targeting spec — no explicit `target(...)` needed |
| "look at target player's hand. You may choose a nonland card from it. If you do, that player reveals the chosen card, puts it on the bottom of their library, then draws a card" | `LookAtHandChooseNonlandToBottomAndDrawEffect()` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD | Vendilion Clique. ## Life

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "you gain N life" / "gain N life" | `GainLifeEffect(N)` | SPELL/trigger | |
| "Draw a card at the beginning of the next turn's upkeep" | `RegisterDrawCardsAtNextUpkeepEffect(N)` | SPELL/trigger | Blessed Wine (`()` = 1). Queues a `DrawCardsAtNextUpkeep` for the resolving controller; drained in `StepTriggerService.handleUpkeepTriggers` at the next upkeep regardless of active player. Same delayed-draw plumbing as Library of Lat-Nam |
| "When a non-[Subtype] creature you control dies, transform ~ at the beginning of the next upkeep" | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_DIES` + `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect(CardNotPredicate(CardSubtypePredicate(subtype)), RegisterTransformSourceAtNextUpkeepEffect())` | trigger | Archangel Avacyn (non-Angel). Delayed `TransformToBackFaceEffect` at next upkeep; no-op if already transformed. Back face: `ON_TRANSFORM_TO_BACK_FACE` `MassDamageEffect(3, false, false, Not(IsSource))` + `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(3, EACH_OPPONENT)` |
| "At the beginning of your end step, if you both own and control ~ and a creature named X, exile them, then meld them into Y" | `CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED` + `ConditionalEffect(AllOf(ControlsPermanentCount(1, IsSource+Owned), ControlsPermanentCount(1, Named(X)+Creature+Owned)), MeldWithNamedCreatureEffect(X))` + `setBackFaceCard(Y)` | trigger | Gisela, the Broken Blade (`X` = Bruna, the Fading Light; `Y` = Brisela). `AllOf` intervening-if at trigger + resolution; meld result is the source's back face |
| "You gain N life. Then if you have more life than an opponent, [effect]" | `GainLifeEffect(N)` + `ConditionalEffect(new ControllerHasMoreLifeThanAnOpponent(), effect)` | SPELL | Feudkiller's Verdict — gain-life effect added first so the life is read before the condition; condition true if strictly more life than any one opponent |
| "you gain 1 life for each [permanent]" | `GainLifeEffect(new PermanentCount(predicate, scope))` | SPELL/trigger | scope: "you control" = CONTROLLER, "on the battlefield" = ANY_PLAYER; "N life for each" = wrap in `Scaled(count, N)`; independent counts summed ("each creature and each artifact", artifact creatures count twice) = `Sum(count1, count2)` (War Report ruling) |
| "you gain N life for each [permanent] target opponent controls" | `GainLifeEffect(new Scaled(new PermanentCount(predicate, CountScope.TARGET_PLAYER), N), GainLifeRecipient.CONTROLLER, true)` + `target(PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT))` | SPELL | Renewing Dawn. `targetsPlayer=true` makes the spell target the opponent (controller still gains) so `TARGET_PLAYER` reads their board |

The `MayEffect` routes through queueMayAbility, so the target is chosen at resolution |

| "at the beginning of each end step, each opponent loses life equal to the life they lost this turn" | `EachOpponentLosesLifeEqualToLifeLostThisTurn()` | END_STEP_TRIGGERED | Wound Reflection. Per-opponent life loss from `GameData.lifeLostThisTurn` (damage counts). Not `LoseLifeEffect(EACH_OPPONENT)` — that would apply one shared amount to every opponent |
| "you gain life equal to the total life lost by all players this turn" | `GainLifeEffect(new LifeLostThisTurn(CountScope.ANY_PLAYER))` | activated ability | Tainted Sigil (`{T}, Sacrifice this: ...`). Sums `GameData.lifeLostThisTurn` over all players (damage counts as life loss; life gained does not offset it) |
| "At the beginning of each of your postcombat main phases, add {R} for each 1 life your opponents have lost this turn" | `AwardManaEffect(ManaColor.RED, new LifeLostThisTurn(CountScope.OPPONENTS))` | `POSTCOMBAT_MAIN_TRIGGERED` | Neheb, the Eternal. Damage counts as life loss; only opponents' loss. Stack trigger (not a mana ability). Fires on each postcombat main including extras from additional combats |
| "at the beginning of your end step, you gain N life if this creature is untapped. Otherwise, each opponent loses N life" | `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new SourceUntapped(), new LoseLifeEffect(N, LoseLifeRecipient.EACH_OPPONENT), new GainLifeEffect(N))` | CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED | Sphinx Sovereign. `baseEffect` = tapped branch, `upgradedEffect` = untapped branch; the branch is chosen at resolution (not an intervening-if, so the trigger always fires) |
| "at the beginning of each end step, if an opponent lost N or more life this turn, you may [effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new OpponentLostLifeThisTurn(N), new MayEffect(innerEffect, "prompt?"))` | END_STEP_TRIGGERED | Sygg, River Cutthroat (`OpponentLostLifeThisTurn(3)` + `MayEffect(DrawCardEffect(1))`). Intervening-if checked at trigger and resolution; `OpponentLostLifeThisTurn` reads `lifeLostThisTurn` (damage counts). `StepTriggerService` skips the trigger when no opponent met the threshold |
| "creatures without flying can't attack you" | `CreaturesCantAttackControllerUnlessPredicateEffect(new PermanentHasKeywordPredicate(Keyword.FLYING))` | STATIC | Form of the Dragon. Defender-scoped (only this controller); exemption predicate matches the creatures that CAN still attack. Contrast global `CreaturesCantAttackUnlessPredicateEffect` |
| "creatures with flying can't attack you or planeswalkers you control" | `CreaturesCantAttackControllerUnlessPredicateEffect(new PermanentNotPredicate(new PermanentHasKeywordPredicate(Keyword.FLYING)), true)` | STATIC | Sandwurm Convergence. Exemption = non-flying (they may still attack); `protectsPlaneswalkers=true` also bars attacks on the controller's planeswalkers |
| "Creatures with power greater than the number of cards in your hand can't attack" | `CreaturesWithPowerGreaterThanAmountCantAttackEffect(new CardsInHand(CountScope.CONTROLLER))` | STATIC | Ensnaring Bridge. Global (both players); threshold is a `DynamicAmount` evaluated from the source's controller. Swap the amount for other "power greater than X can't attack" thresholds |
| "Wall creatures can attack as though they didn't have defender" | `MatchingCreaturesCanAttackAsThoughNoDefenderEffect(new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(CardSubtype.WALL))` | STATIC | Rolling Stones. Global grant to all creatures (any controller) matching the predicate; self-only variant is `CanAttackAsThoughNoDefenderEffect` |
| "{cost}: This creature gets +X/-Y until end of turn and can attack this turn as though it didn't have defender" | `new ActivatedAbility(false, "{cost}", List.of(new BoostSelfEffect(X, -Y), new CanAttackAsThoughNoDefenderEffect()), "...")` | ACTIVATED | Wall of Wonder (+4/-4). In an activated ability `CanAttackAsThoughNoDefenderEffect` resolves into an until-EOT floating grant (creature keeps defender); no new class |
| "{0}: This creature can attack this turn as though it didn't have defender. Exile it at the beginning of the next end step" | `new ActivatedAbility(false, "{0}", List.of(new CanAttackAsThoughNoDefenderEffect(), new ExileSelfAtEndStepEffect()), "...")` | ACTIVATED | Dark Maze. `ExileSelfAtEndStepEffect` schedules the source (no target) for exile at the next end step |
| "Enchanted Wall can attack as though it didn't have defender" (Aura) | `CanAttackAsThoughNoDefenderEffect()` in `EffectSlot.STATIC` | STATIC | Animate Wall. Enchant restriction via `PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(CardSubtype.WALL), "Target must be a Wall")`. `GameQueryService.canAttackDespiteDefender` reads the effect off attached Auras via `hasAuraWithEffect`, so putting the plain self-scoped effect on the Aura grants the permission to the enchanted creature |
| "Enchanted creature can attack as though it had haste" (Aura) | `EnchantedCreatureCanAttackAsThoughHasteEffect()` in `EffectSlot.STATIC` | STATIC | Instill Energy. Attack-only summoning-sickness bypass read off attached Auras in `CombatAttackService.canCreatureAttack` via `hasAuraWithEffect`. Do NOT use `GrantKeywordEffect(HASTE, ENCHANTED)` — real haste also lifts summoning sickness for `{T}` ability activation, which this card must not grant. Pair with an untap ability (`UntapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.ENCHANTED)`) for the full card |
| "players can't gain life" | `PlayersCantGainLifeEffect()` | STATIC | |
| "Players can't get counters. Counters can't be put on artifacts, creatures, enchantments, or lands." | `CountersCantBePlacedEffect()` | STATIC | Solemnity. One global lock — checked at `GameQueryService.cantHaveCounters` (permanent clause, gated to artifact/creature/enchantment/land so planeswalkers keep loyalty) and `canPlayerGetPoisonCounters` (player clause). Also replaces "enters with counters" |
| "Whenever ~ deals damage to a player, that player can't gain life for the rest of the game" | `TargetPlayerCantGainLifeRestOfGameEffect()` | ON_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Stigma Lasher. Non-targeting; the damaged player is baked in as `targetId`. Any damage (combat or noncombat) triggers it. Persists per-player via `GameData.playersWhoCantGainLifeRestOfGame` |
| "Whenever ~ deals damage to a player, that player loses N life at the beginning of their next draw step unless they pay {M} before that draw step" | `RegisterLoseLifeAtNextDrawStepUnlessPaysEffect(N, M)` | ON_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Nafs Asp (`(1, 1)`). Non-targeting; damaged player baked in as `targetId` (`DAMAGED_PLAYER`). Queues a `LoseLifeAtNextDrawStepUnlessPays` delayed action drained at that player's next draw step in `StepTriggerService` as a `ForcedCostOrElseEffect(PayManaCost, [LoseLifeEffect], true)` pay-or-lose-life may-prompt. Life loss, not damage — won't re-trigger. Modelling the payment at the draw step is outcome-equivalent to "before that draw step" |
| "Whenever this creature deals damage, you gain that much life" | `GainLifeEffect(new EventValue())` | ON_SELF_DEALS_DAMAGE | El-Hajjâj. Fires only for this creature's own damage (combat or noncombat, to any target); the summed damage total is snapshotted onto the trigger's `eventValue`, so the `EventValue` amount gains exactly that much. Still fires when the creature dies dealing the damage |
| "if you would gain life, you gain twice that much life instead" | `DoubleLifeGainEffect()` | STATIC | Boon Reflection. Controller-only replacement applied in `LifeSupport.applyGainLife`; multiple stack multiplicatively (2^count) |
| "if you tap a permanent for mana, it produces twice as much of that mana instead" | `ManaReflectionEffect()` | STATIC | Mana Reflection. Controller-only replacement applied in the mana-ability resolution (`ActivatedAbilityExecutionService`) via `GameQueryService.manaProductionMultiplier` (2^count). Doubles the mana any tapped permanent produces (fixed and any-color); not `DoubleManaPoolEffect` (which doubles the whole pool once) |

## Graveyard / library hate (static, global)

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "you may activate abilities of creatures you control as though those creatures had haste" | `ActivateCreatureAbilitiesAsThoughHasteEffect()` | STATIC | Thousand-Year Elixir. Lifts summoning-sickness on ability activation only (does NOT grant haste — don't use `GrantKeywordEffect(HASTE, …)`, which would let them attack). Checked via `GameQueryService.canActivateCreatureAbilitiesAsThoughHaste(gd, playerId)` |
| "you may spend white mana as though it were red mana" | `SpendWhiteManaAsRedEffect()` | STATIC | Sunglasses of Urza. Permission — white mana keeps its color but may also pay red pips. Rides a per-player `ManaPool` flag (`isWhiteSpendableAsRed`) that `ManaCost.canPay`/`pay` honor; set via `GameQueryService.canSpendWhiteManaAsRed(gd, playerId)` at the payment/playability sites |
| "players can't cast spells from graveyards" | `PlayersCantCastSpellsFromZonesEffect(Set.of(Zone.GRAVEYARD))` | STATIC | Ashes of the Abhorrent. Gated in flashback/graveyard-cast paths via `GameQueryService.canPlayersCastSpellsFromZone(gd, Zone.GRAVEYARD)` |
| "exile the top N cards of your library face down" (controller only, tracked to source) | `ExileTopCardsToSourceEffect(N)` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD | Colfenor's Plans. Controller-only; pair with `AllowCastFromCardsExiledWithSourceEffect(false)` for "you may play lands and cast spells from among those cards" |
| "Whenever this creature becomes tapped, exile the top N cards of target opponent's library face down" | `TriggeringPermanentConditionalEffect(new PermanentIsSourceCardPredicate(), new ExileTopCardsOfOpponentLibraryToSourceEffect(N))` | ON_ALLY_PERMANENT_BECOMES_TAPPED | Grimoire Thief. The conditional restricts the shared tap trigger to the source itself; two-player resolves against the single opponent (no target choice) |
| "{cost}, {Q}: Target opponent exiles the top card of their library. Until end of turn, you may play that card." | `ActivatedAbility(...).withRequiresUntap()` + `ExileTopCardOfOpponentLibraryControllerMayPlayThisTurnEffect()` | activated ability | Knacksaw Clique (`{1}{U}, {Q}`). Controller gets end-of-turn play permission (normal costs/timing, lands included); two-player resolves against the single opponent (no target choice) |
| "+2: Target opponent exiles cards from the top of their library until they exile a nonland card. Until end of turn, you may cast that card without paying its mana cost." | `ExileTopUntilNonlandOfTargetOpponentMayCastThisTurnEffect()` + `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT)` | loyalty ability | Nicol Bolas, God-Pharaoh. Digs until a nonland (lands stay exiled with no permission); grants `exilePlayPermissions` + `exilePlayPermissionsExpireEndOfTurn` + `exilePlayWithoutPayingManaCost` on the nonland only |
| "+1: Each opponent exiles two cards from their hand." | `EachOpponentExilesFromHandEffect(2)` | loyalty ability | Nicol Bolas, God-Pharaoh. Non-targeting; APNAP hand exile via `EXILE_FROM_HAND_CHOICE` (fewer than N ⇒ whole hand) |
| "{X}...: Choose a color. Target opponent exiles the top X cards of their library. For each card of the chosen color exiled this way, create a [token]." | `ActivatedAbility("{X}...", ExileTopCardsOfTargetOpponentCreateTokenPerChosenColorEffect(new XValue(), tokenTemplate), PlayerRelation.OPPONENT filter)` | activated ability | Oona, Queen of the Fae. Resolution pauses for the controller's colour choice (`ChoiceContext.ExileTopCardsChosenColorTokensChoice`); a card is "of the chosen colour" per printed colours, lands excluded (mirrors Persecute). Token count = number of matching exiled cards (template `amount` ignored) |
| "Whenever ~ deals combat damage to a player, you may pay {2}{G}. If you do, choose a color, then create a 1/1 green Saproling creature token for each permanent of that color." | `MayPayManaEffect("{2}{G}", new CreateTokenPerPermanentOfChosenColorEffect(new CreateTokenEffect("Saproling", 1, 1, CardColor.GREEN, List.of(CardSubtype.SAPROLING), Set.of(), Set.of())), "Pay {2}{G}?")` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Rith, the Awakener. Resolution pauses for the controller's colour choice (`ChoiceContext.CreateTokensPerPermanentOfChosenColorChoice`); token count = permanents of that colour on the battlefield (any controller, lands excluded per effective colours). Template `amount` ignored |
| "Search target opponent's library for a card and exile it. Then that player shuffles. Until the beginning of your next upkeep, you may play that card. At the beginning of your next upkeep, if you haven't played it, put it into its owner's graveyard." | `SacrificeSelfCost()` + `SearchTargetLibraryForCardToExileWithPlayPermissionEffect(true)` | activated ability | Grinning Totem (`{2}, {T}, Sacrifice`, opponent-target filter). Same search/exile/play-permission flow as Praetor's Grasp but permission expires at the caster's next upkeep; an unplayed card is put into its owner's graveyard (see the effect's `expiresAtNextUpkeep` note in EFFECTS_INDEX). Pass `false` (or no-arg) for the permanent Praetor's Grasp version |
| "Whenever a [permanent] an opponent controls becomes tapped, you may gain N life" | `TriggeringPermanentConditionalEffect(new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(CardSubtype.X), new MayEffect(new GainLifeEffect(N), prompt))` | ON_OPPONENT_PERMANENT_BECOMES_TAPPED | Thoughtleech (Island, 1). Opponent-scoped counterpart of `ON_ALLY_PERMANENT_BECOMES_TAPPED`; fires on any tap (for mana or forced, e.g. Icy Manipulator), not just taps for mana. Contrast Sanctimony's `GainLifeWhenOpponentTapsLandOfSubtypeEffect` (mana taps only) |
| "{cost}, Sacrifice this creature: Turn all cards exiled with it face up. Counter all spells with those names." | `SacrificeSelfCost()` + `CounterSpellsNamedLikeCardsExiledWithSourceEffect()` | activated ability | Grimoire Thief (`{U}`). Counters every stack spell whose name matches a card exiled with the source; exiled cards are found via the entry's `sourcePermanentId` after the sacrifice |
| "Hideaway N (look at the top N cards, exile one face down, rest on bottom in a random order)" | `ImprintFromTopCardsEffect(N)` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD | Howltooth Hollow, Clone Shell (N=4). Exiles the chosen card face down and imprints it on the source permanent |
| "{cost}: You may play the exiled card without paying its mana cost if <condition>" (Hideaway) | `<cost>` + `ConditionalEffect(<condition>, PlayImprintedCardWithoutPayingManaCostEffect())` | activated ability | Howltooth Hollow (`{B}, {T}`, condition = `NoPlayerHasCardsInHand`), Shelldock Isle (`{U}, {T}`, condition = `AnyLibraryAtMost(20)`), Mosswort Bridge (`{G}, {T}`, condition = `ControlledCreaturesTotalPowerAtLeast(10)`). Offers a may-play of the imprinted card; land → battlefield (counts as the land play), else cast from exile for free. Routed via `MayCastHandlerService.handlePlayImprintedCardChoice` |
| "Skip your draw step." | `SkipDrawStepEffect()` | STATIC | Colfenor's Plans, Necropotence. Controller's draw step skipped in `StepTriggerService.handleDrawStep` |
| "Whenever you discard a card, exile that card from your graveyard." | `ExileDiscardedCardFromGraveyardEffect()` | ON_CONTROLLER_DISCARDS | Necropotence. Fires on the discarding player's own battlefield (`TriggerCollectionService.checkDiscardTriggers` scans it after the existing opponent-discard scan); the just-discarded card is moved from graveyard to exile in `DiscardTriggerCollectorService`. No-op if a replacement effect sent the card elsewhere |
| "Whenever you cycle or discard a card, this creature gets +X/+Y until end of turn." | `BoostSelfEffect(X, Y)` | ON_CONTROLLER_DISCARDS | Hekma Sentinels. Cycling discards the card (CR 702.29e), so this one controller-discard trigger covers both wordings. `DiscardTriggerCollectorService` enqueues it as a `TRIGGERED_ABILITY` carrying the source permanent id so the self-boost lands on "this creature" |
| "Whenever you cycle or discard a card, this creature gets +1/+0 until end of turn and can't be blocked this turn." | `SequenceEffect.of(BoostSelfEffect(1, 0), MakeCreatureUnblockableEffect(true))` | ON_CONTROLLER_DISCARDS | Cunning Survivor. Two self effects in one mandatory trigger → bundle as a single atomic `SequenceEffect` (per-slot dispatch pushes one entry per slot effect). `DiscardTriggerCollectorService.handleSequenceOnDiscard` enqueues the `TRIGGERED_ABILITY` carrying the source permanent id; the spliced steps (`BoostSelfEffect`, self-targeting `MakeCreatureUnblockableEffect`) both read `sourcePermanentId`, landing on "this creature" |
| "Whenever you cycle or discard another card, scry N." | `ScryEffect(N)` | ON_CONTROLLER_DISCARDS | Curator of Mysteries. Cycling discards the card (CR 702.29e), so this one controller-discard trigger covers both wordings. `DiscardTriggerCollectorService` enqueues it as a `TRIGGERED_ABILITY` (uses the stack). The source is on the battlefield while the discarded card comes from hand, so the "another card" clause is inherently satisfied. `AbilityActivationService.activateHandAbility` fires discard triggers **after** the cycling draw is on the stack, so the scry resolves first |
| "Whenever you cycle or discard another card, put a -1/-1 counter on each creature your opponents control." | `PutCounterOnEachMatchingPermanentEffect(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 1, AllOf(IsCreature, Not(ControlledBySourceController)), ALL_PLAYERS)` | ON_CONTROLLER_DISCARDS | Archfiend of Ifnir. Cycling discards the card (CR 702.29e), so this one controller-discard trigger covers both. `DiscardTriggerCollectorService.handlePutCountersOnDiscard` enqueues it as a `TRIGGERED_ABILITY` carrying the source permanent id so the "your opponents" (`Not(PermanentControlledBySourceControllerPredicate)`) predicate resolves against the ability's controller. `PutCounterOnEachMatchingPermanentEffectHandler` now stamps `sourceControllerId` on its `FilterContext` so controller-relative predicates work at resolution |
| "Whenever you cycle or discard a card, target creature gains [keyword] until end of turn." | `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword, GrantScope.TARGET, PermanentIsCreaturePredicate)` | ON_CONTROLLER_DISCARDS | Zenith Seeker (flying). Cycling discards the card (CR 702.29e), so this one controller-discard trigger covers both. Do **not** call `target(...)` — that would demand a target when casting the creature; the effect's `GrantScope.TARGET` filter drives the trigger's target choice. `DiscardTriggerCollectorService.handleGrantKeywordOnDiscard` queues a `PermanentChoiceContext.DiscardControllerTriggerTarget`, serviced by `TriggeredAbilityQueueService.processNextDiscardControllerTriggerTarget` (any-permanent flow, `Options.ATTACK`; the effect's creature predicate narrows it), so the target is chosen before the ability goes on the stack (above the cycling draw) |
| "Whenever you cycle or discard a card, target creature an opponent controls gets -X/-Y until end of turn." | `BoostTargetCreatureEffect(-X, -Y, AllOf(IsCreature, Not(ControlledBySourceController)))` | ON_CONTROLLER_DISCARDS | Ominous Sphinx (-2/-0). Cycling discards the card (CR 702.29e), so this one controller-discard trigger covers both. Do **not** call `target(...)` — the effect's own `filter` (a "creature an opponent controls" predicate, same idiom as Archfiend of Ifnir) drives the trigger's target choice. `DiscardTriggerCollectorService.handleBoostTargetCreatureOnDiscard` queues a `PermanentChoiceContext.DiscardControllerTriggerTarget`, serviced by `processNextDiscardControllerTriggerTarget` (`Options.ATTACK` reads `targetSpec().predicate()` so the opponent-creature filter narrows the legal targets). Trigger is skipped if no opponent creature exists |
| "As long as you have seven or more cards in hand, you may pay {0} rather than pay cycling costs." | `FreeCyclingWhileHandSizeEffect(7)` | STATIC | New Perspectives (pair with `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` `DrawCardEffect(3)`). CR 118.9 alt cost read in `AbilityActivationService.activateHandAbility` via the `FreeCyclingEffect` fact — replaces only the cycling ability's mana cost with {0}; the intrinsic "discard this card" cost still happens. Hand-size check counts the card being cycled (checked before discard). No handler bean, mirroring `AlternativeCostForSpellsEffect` |
| "Pay 1 life: Exile the top card of your library face down. Put that card into your hand at the beginning of your next end step." | `PayLifeCost(1)` + `NecropotenceSetAsideTopCardEffect()` (activated ability) | activated ability | Necropotence. Exiles the top library card and registers a `ReturnExiledCardToHandAtEndStep` delayed action; drained in `StepTriggerService.handleEndStepTriggers` **only at the controller's own end step** (`activePlayerId == ownerId`). Implements `CardDrawingEffect` (1 card) |
| "If you would draw a card during your draw step, instead you may skip that draw. If you do, until your next turn, you can't be attacked except by creatures with flying and/or islandwalk." | `IslandSanctuaryEffect()` | MAY_SKIP_DRAW_STEP_DRAW | Island Sanctuary. Slot presence makes `StepTriggerService.handleDrawStep` offer a `ReplaceSingleDrawEffect(..., DrawReplacementKind.ISLAND_SANCTUARY)` may-ability instead of the draw. On accept, `MayMiscHandlerService.handleSingleDrawReplacementChoice` skips the draw and stamps an `UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN` player-scoped `CreaturesCantAttackControllerUnlessPredicateEffect(PermanentAnyOfPredicate(flying, islandwalk))` floating effect (checked in `CombatAttackService`) |
| "You can't cast more than one spell each turn." (controller only) | `LimitSpellsForControllerEffect(1)` | STATIC | Colfenor's Plans. Controller-only variant of `LimitSpellsPerTurnEffect` (Rule of Law, which is every player) |
| "Each opponent who controls more creatures than you can't cast creature spells. Same for artifacts and enchantments. Each opponent who controls more lands than you can't play lands." | `WardOfBonesEffect()` | STATIC | Ward of Bones. Each permanent type compared independently opponent-vs-controller. Casting side folded into `CastingPermissionService.getRestrictedSpellTypes`; land side via `CastingPermissionService.isLandPlayRestrictedByWardOfBones` (checked in `GameBroadcastService` land-playable gate). Controller never restricted |
| "Cast this spell only during the declare attackers step and only if you've been attacked this step." | `setSpellCastTimingRestriction(SpellCastTimingRestriction.DECLARE_ATTACKERS_IF_ATTACKED)` in the card constructor (not an effect) | — | Defiant Stand. Card-level cast-timing restriction on `Card`; enforced in `CastingPermissionService.canCastWithSpellTimingRestriction` and surfaced by the `GameBroadcastService` playable-card gate. "Attacked" = a creature is attacking you or a planeswalker you control |
| "Cast this spell only during your end step." | `setSpellCastTimingRestriction(SpellCastTimingRestriction.YOUR_END_STEP)` in the card constructor (not an effect) | — | Necrologia. Enforced in `CastingPermissionService.canCastWithSpellTimingRestriction` (`currentStep == END_STEP && caster is active player`) |
| "Cast this spell only during combat before blockers are declared." | `setSpellCastTimingRestriction(SpellCastTimingRestriction.COMBAT_BEFORE_BLOCKERS)` in the card constructor (not an effect) | — | Panic. Enforced in `CastingPermissionService.canCastWithSpellTimingRestriction` (combat phase and step before `DECLARE_BLOCKERS`, i.e. beginning-of-combat or declare-attackers; any player) |
| "Cast this spell only during an opponent's turn, before attackers are declared." | `setSpellCastTimingRestriction(SpellCastTimingRestriction.OPPONENTS_TURN_BEFORE_ATTACKERS)` in the card constructor (not an effect) | — | Siren's Call. Enforced in `CastingPermissionService.canCastWithSpellTimingRestriction` (caster is not the active player and `currentStep.isBeforeAttackersDeclared()`) |
| "Creatures the active player controls attack this turn if able. At the beginning of the next end step, destroy all non-Wall creatures that player controls that didn't attack this turn (ignore each creature they didn't control continuously since the turn began)." | `SirensCallEffect()` | SPELL | Siren's Call. Non-targeted. Resolution sets the transient must-attack flag on every creature the active player controls and queues a `DestroyNonAttackersAtEndStep(activePlayerId)` delayed action drained in `StepTriggerService.handleEndStepTriggers`; the end-step pass destroys the active player's non-Wall creatures with `!attackedThisTurn && !summoningSick`. `summoningSick` == "didn't control continuously since the beginning of the turn" (same signal as `CameUnderControlThisTurn`) |
| "players can't cast spells from graveyards or libraries" | `PlayersCantCastSpellsFromZonesEffect(Set.of(Zone.GRAVEYARD, Zone.LIBRARY))` | STATIC | Grafdigger's Cage. Gated via `GameQueryService.canPlayersCastSpellsFromZone(gd, zone)` (graveyard cast/flashback + `playCardFromLibraryTop`). Only `GRAVEYARD`/`LIBRARY` enforced |
| "You may look at the top card of your library any time. You may cast creature spells from the top of your library. You can spend mana of any type to cast creature spells." | `LookAtTopCardOfOwnLibraryEffect()` + `AllowCastFromTopOfLibraryEffect(Set.of(CardType.CREATURE))` + `SpendAnyManaTypeToCastEffect(Set.of(CardType.CREATURE))`, all `EffectSlot.STATIC` | STATIC | Vizier of the Menagerie. Three independent static markers. The any-type-mana grant (`CastingPermissionService.canSpendAnyManaTypeToCast`) applies to matching spells cast from hand or library top |
| "creature cards in graveyards and libraries can't enter the battlefield" | `CardsCantEnterBattlefieldFromZonesEffect(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), Set.of(Zone.GRAVEYARD, Zone.LIBRARY))` | STATIC | Grafdigger's Cage. Filter selects which cards are blocked (null = all); `zones` selects which source zones are blocked (only `GRAVEYARD`/`LIBRARY` enforced). Blocks reanimation/undying + library-search-to-battlefield; gated via `GameQueryService.isCardBlockedFromEnteringFromZone(gd, card, zone)`. Blocked card stays in its zone |
| "Noncreature spells with mana value N or greater can't be cast." / "Noncreature spells with {X} in their mana costs can't be cast." | `NoncreatureSpellsCantBeCastEffect(N, true)` | STATIC | Gaddock Teeg `(4, true)`. Global/symmetric — restricts all players incl. controller. Enforced via `CastingPermissionService.isNoncreatureSpellCastRestricted` at the hand/exile/library-top playable sites. Pass `restrictXSpells=false` for the mana-value clause alone |
| "Your opponents can't cast spells with mana value N or less." | `OpponentsCantCastSpellsWithManaValueAtMostEffect(N)` | STATIC | Brisela, Voice of Nightmares `(3)`. Opponents-only. Playability leaves `{X}` spells offered (a high enough X is always legal); cast-time includes chosen X in mana value (CR 202.3c). | "Each player who has cast a nonartifact spell this turn can't cast additional nonartifact spells." | `CantCastAdditionalNonartifactSpellsEffect()` | STATIC | Ethersworn Canonist. Global/symmetric — each player's first nonartifact spell and all artifact spells are unrestricted. Enforced via `CastingPermissionService.isAdditionalNonartifactSpellRestricted` (reads `getSpellsCastThisTurn`) at the hand/graveyard/library-top playable sites |

## Library manipulation

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "search your library for a card" (any to hand) | `SearchLibraryEffect()` | SPELL | unified library search; no-arg = unrestricted single card to hand (Diabolic Tutor) |
| "search your library for a white card, a blue card, a black card, a red card, and a green card, reveal those cards, put them into your hand, then shuffle" | `SearchLibraryForOneCardOfEachColorToHandEffect()` | SPELL | Conflux — one different card per colour (WUBRG order), each a separate revealed HAND pick, may fail to find; a colour absent from the library is skipped; library shuffled once after the last colour. Not `SearchLibraryEffect` (that reuses one filter across a multi-count search) |
| "An opponent chooses one — you draw three cards at the beginning of the next turn's upkeep; OR you search your library for a card, put it into your hand, then shuffle" | `LibraryOfLatNamEffect()` | SPELL | Library of Lat-Nam. Opponent picks the mode via the may-ability accept/decline prompt: accept → `DrawCardsAtNextUpkeep` delayed draw-3 (drained in `StepTriggerService.handleUpkeepTriggers`); decline → `SearchLibraryEffect()` tutor to hand. New delayed action added to `DelayedAction` permits |

The `true` is `SpellCastTriggerEffect.onlyDuringOpponentTurn` — gates the trigger to turns where the source's controller is not the active player. For the "may" + target combo, put the target filter on the CARD via `target(new PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(AllOf(PermanentIsCreaturePredicate, PermanentControlledBySourceControllerPredicate), ...))` (the may path reads `sourceCard.getTargetFilter()`, not the trigger's targetFilter) |
| "you may exile target creature card from your graveyard. If you do, create a token that's a copy of that card, except it's a Spirit in addition to its other types. Exile it at the beginning of the next end step" | `EACH_UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` + `MayEffect(ExileTargetCardFromGraveyardAndCreateTokenCopyEffect(CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), true, List.of(SPIRIT), false, true))` | trigger | Séance. `EACH_UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` requires `MayEffect` handling in `StepTriggerService` (queues via `queueMayAbility`) |

## Tokens

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "target player creates a token that's a copy of target creature you control" | `CreateTokenCopyOfTargetCreatureForTargetPlayerEffect()` | SPELL | Two targets (player, then creature); token enters under chosen player |
| "Whenever a nontoken creature you control enters, you may pay {2}. If you do, create a token that's a copy of that creature, except it has haste and 'At the beginning of the end step, sacrifice this permanent.'" | `MayPayManaEffect("{2}", new CreateTokenCopyOfTargetPermanentEffect(true, false, true), prompt)` | `ON_ALLY_NONTOKEN_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Minion Reflector. The slot bakes the entering creature's id (skips tokens); `sacrificeAtEndStep=true` routes the token to the graveyard so its dies-triggers fire (unlike Heat Shimmer's `exileAtEndStep`) |
| "Whenever a nontoken [subtype] you control enters, create a token that's a copy of that creature" | `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect(new CardSubtypePredicate(subtype), new CreateTokenCopyOfTargetPermanentEffect())` | `ON_ALLY_NONTOKEN_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Necroduality (Zombie). Mandatory copy: enter collector bakes the entering permanent id as `targetId` (does not go through EntersTriggerTarget). Tokens skipped by the slot so the copy cannot retrigger |
| "For each creature token you control, create a token that's a copy of that creature" | `CreateTokenCopyOfEachControlledCreatureTokenEffect()` | activated ability / SPELL | Populate-all (Rhys the Redeemed). Snapshots your creature tokens first so new copies aren't copied; respects the token multiplier (Doubling Season). No target |
| "When this enchantment enters, create a token that's a copy of target nontoken creature. When this leaves, exile the token. When the token leaves, sacrifice this." | `target(nontoken creature)` + ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD `CreateTokenCopyAndLinkToSourceEffect()` + ON_SELF_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD `RemoveLinkedPermanentEffect(EXILE)` (+ upkeep `ForcedCostOrElseEffect`) | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD + ON_SELF_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD | Dance of Many. The ETB effect creates the token copy and forges the two-way `chosenPermanentId` bond, attaching the token's own `RemoveLinkedPermanentEffect(SACRIFICE)` leaves-trigger. `RemoveLinkedPermanentEffect` bakes the linked id into the effect (avoids spell-target-filter fizzle) and breaks the bond before removal (no ping-pong) |
| "Whenever a [subtype] you control deals combat damage to a player, you may create ... token" | `AllyCombatDamageTriggerEffect(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(X), MayEffect(CreateTokenEffect(...)))` | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER` | Boggart Mob. Generic wrapper: filters the damage dealer by predicate, then puts any effect (wrap in `MayEffect` for "you may") on the stack for the controller. For "... put a +1/+1 counter on it" (effect applies to the dealer, e.g. Rakish Heir) pass `PutCountersOnSourceEffect` with `bindSourceToDealer=true`. For "... that player discards a card" (effect applies to the damaged player) pass `DiscardEffect(1, DiscardRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)` — the damaged player is bound as the trigger's target (Oona's Blackguard, dealer predicate `PermanentHasCountersPredicate(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE)`) |
| "create N 1/1 white Spirit creature tokens with flying" | `CreateTokenEffect.whiteSpirit(N)` | SPELL/trigger | Static factory |
| "Whenever another non-[Subtype] creature you control dies, create ..." | `EffectSlot.ON_ALLY_CREATURE_DIES` + `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect(new CardNotPredicate(new CardSubtypePredicate(subtype)), CreateTokenEffect...)` | trigger | Requiem Angel-style; use ally creature death, not nontoken, because token non-Spirits count |
| "Whenever a creature dies, that creature's controller may draw a card" | `DyingCreatureControllerMayDrawCardEffect()` | `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES` | Fecundity. Routes the optional draw to the DYING creature's controller (may be an opponent), not the source's controller — do NOT use `MayEffect(DrawCardEffect())`, which offers it to the source's controller |
| "Whenever this creature attacks, defending player may draw a card" | `DefendingPlayerMayDrawCardEffect()` | `ON_ATTACK` | Sibilant Spirit. `CombatAttackService` routes the optional draw to the defending player (or the attacked planeswalker's controller), not the attacking creature's controller — do NOT use `MayEffect(DrawCardEffect())`, which offers it to the source's controller |
| "Whenever a green creature dies, its controller discards a card" | `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect(new CardColorPredicate(GREEN), new DyingCreatureControllerDiscardsCardEffect())` | `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES` | Bereavement. Mandatory discard routed to the DYING creature's controller (may be an opponent). The `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect` restricts to green creatures |
| "Whenever another creature dies, you may put a +1/+1 counter on this creature" | `MayEffect(new PutCountersOnSourceEffect(1, 1, 1), "...")` | `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES` | Scavenger Drake. The ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES MayEffect collector carries the source permanent id, so the wrapped `PutCountersOnSourceEffect` resolves onto the trigger source (mandatory variant = bare `PutCountersOnSourceEffect`, e.g. Lumberknot / Village Cannibals) |
| "Whenever a player sacrifices a creature, you may put a +1/+1 counter on this creature" | `MayEffect(new PutCountersOnSourceEffect(1, 1, 1), "...")` | `ON_ANY_CREATURE_SACRIFICED` | Thraximundar. Global sacrifice watcher (any player, including you); the collector carries the source permanent id so the wrapped `PutCountersOnSourceEffect` resolves onto the trigger source and the "you may" goes to the source's controller. Fired from both sacrifice choke points (edict/chosen via `sacrificeAndLog`; sacrifice-self / sacrifice-as-cost via `checkAllyPermanentSacrificedTriggers`) |
| "Whenever another creature dies, you may put X +1/+1 counters on this creature, where X is that creature's power" | `PutCountersOnSourceEqualToDyingPowerEffect(1, 1, true)` | `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES` | Kresh the Bloodbraided. Dying creature's last-known effective power read at trigger time; `optional=true` = "you may". Death sibling of Hamletback Goliath's `PutCountersOnSourceEqualToEnteringPowerEffect` |
| "Whenever another creature dies, untap this creature" | `UntapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.SELF)` | `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES` | Galvanic Juggernaut. The dedicated `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES` untap collector carries the source permanent id so the SELF-scope untap resolves onto the trigger source (the `CardEffect` default collector does NOT set the source id — a bare source-referencing effect there would no-op). Pair with `DoesntUntapEffect.self()` + `MustAttackEffect` for the full Juggernaut |
| "Whenever another [Subtype] you control is put into a graveyard from the battlefield, you may have this deal 1 damage to target player or planeswalker" | `EffectSlot.ON_ALLY_CREATURE_DIES` + `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect(new CardSubtypePredicate(subtype), new MayEffect(new DealDamageToTargetPlayerOrPlaneswalkerEffect(1), "..."))` | trigger | Boggart Shenanigans. Non-creature source satisfies "another" automatically; MayEffect-wrapped targeted effect picks its target during may-resolution |
| "Whenever a creature dies, if it had a -1/-1 counter on it, put a -1/-1 counter on target creature" | `EffectSlot.ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES` + `TriggeringPermanentConditionalEffect(new PermanentHasCountersPredicate(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE), new PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 1))` | trigger | Blowfly Infestation. `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES` now unwraps `TriggeringPermanentConditionalEffect` against the **dying permanent** (its counters at death), so the intervening-if reads the dying creature's -1/-1 counter. The death-trigger target pipeline restricts the target to creatures automatically |
| "Whenever a creature an opponent controls with a -1/-1 counter on it dies, you may return that card to the battlefield under your control" | `EffectSlot.ON_OPPONENT_CREATURE_DIES` + `TriggeringPermanentConditionalEffect(new PermanentHasCountersPredicate(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE), new ReturnDyingOpponentCreatureUnderYourControlEffect())` | trigger | Necroskitter. `ON_OPPONENT_CREATURE_DIES` now carries the dying card + unwraps `TriggeringPermanentConditionalEffect` against the dying permanent. | "Increment (Whenever you cast a spell, if the mana you spent is greater than this creature's power or toughness, put a +1/+1 counter on it)" | *(none — keyword-driven)* | — | Increment keyword (SOS). Auto-loaded from Scryfall as `Keyword.INCREMENT`; behavior is driven by the keyword in `TriggerCollectionService.collectIncrementTriggers` (like Undying). Add **nothing** to the card (e.g. Ambitious Augmenter) |
| "Whenever you clash, [effect]. If you won, [win-only effect]." | `addEffect(ON_CONTROLLER_CLASHES, effect)` + `addEffect(ON_CONTROLLER_CLASHES, new IfWonClashEffect(winOnlyEffect))` | `ON_CONTROLLER_CLASHES` | Clash (LRW, rule 701.29). Fired by `TriggerCollectionService.fireClashTriggers` after the clash ends; targeting triggers route through `ClashTriggerTarget` (target creature an opponent controls). `IfWonClashEffect` clause applied only on a won clash (winner = strictly higher revealed mana value; 2-player). Inert until some card *initiates* a clash (see `ClashEffect`). E.g. Entangling Trap: `TapPermanentsEffect(TARGET)` + `IfWonClashEffect(SkipNextUntapEffect(TARGET))` |
| "Whenever you clash, you may pay {C}. If you do, [effect]. If you won, [outcome-dependent detail]." | `addEffect(ON_CONTROLLER_CLASHES, new IfWonClashEffect(new MayPayManaEffect("{C}", wonVariant, prompt)))` + `addEffect(ON_CONTROLLER_CLASHES, new IfLostClashEffect(new MayPayManaEffect("{C}", lostVariant, prompt)))` | `ON_CONTROLLER_CLASHES` | Clash trigger whose base effect happens either way but a detail differs by outcome. Split into won/lost variants so exactly one branch fires. Non-targeting → the trigger goes straight onto the stack (no `ClashTriggerTarget`). E.g. Rebellion of the Flamekin: create a 3/1 red Elemental Shaman token that gains `HASTE` (`grantedKeywordsUntilEndOfTurn`) only on the won branch |
| "When this enters/[event], clash with an opponent. If you win, [win-only effect]." | `addEffect(ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD, new ClashEffect(winOnlyEffect))` | any stack slot (usually `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD`) | Clash-*source* (LRW, rule 701.29). Resolves by calling `performClash` for the controller; on a win dispatches the wrapped effect against the same entry (acts on the source). Pass `null` for a bare "clash with an opponent" with no reward. E.g. Oaken Brawler: `ClashEffect(new PutCountersOnSourceEffect(1, 1, 1))` |
| "[body], then clash with an opponent. If you win, repeat this process." | `addEffect(SPELL, new ClashEffect(List.of(bodyEffects...), null, true))` | SPELL | Clash-*source* loop (LRW). Runs the `beforeClash` body first, then clashes; `repeatWhileWinning=true` repeats the whole sequence while the controller keeps winning `performClash`, stopping on the first loss. E.g. Hoarder's Greed: `ClashEffect(List.of(new LoseLifeEffect(2), new DrawCardEffect(2)), null, true)` |
| "Whenever this creature attacks, clash with an opponent. If you win, target creature gains [keyword] until end of turn." | `target(new PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), ...))` + `addEffect(ON_ATTACK, new ClashEffect(new GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.X, GrantScope.TARGET)))` | `ON_ATTACK` | Clash-*source* with a **targeted** win reward. `ClashEffect` delegates targeting to `wrapped`, so the attack pipeline collects the target when the trigger goes on the stack; the clash resolves and the keyword is granted only on a win. E.g. Springjack Knight (double strike) |
| "When this dies, if it had one or more counters on it, create a 0/0 [color] [Subtype] token, then put this creature's counters on that token" | `CreateTokenWithDyingSourceCountersEffect(new CreateTokenEffect("name", 0, 0, color, Set.of(colors), List.of(subtype)))` | `ON_DEATH` | Snapshots dying creature's +1/+1 counters onto the new token (e.g. Ambitious Augmenter's Fractal) |
| "When this dies, if it had counters on it, put those counters on up to one target creature" | `MoveDyingSourceCountersToTargetCreatureEffect()` | `ON_DEATH` | Snapshots every counter type on the dying creature and moves them to a chosen creature (e.g. Scolding Administrator) |
| "When this creature dies, draw a card for each -1/-1 counter on it" | `DrawCardForEachDyingSourceCounterEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE)` | `ON_DEATH` | Snapshots the dying creature's counter count of that type at death and draws that many (e.g. Dusk Urchins). Pair with `ON_ATTACK`/`ON_BLOCK` `PutCountersOnSourceEffect(-1,-1,1)` for "whenever it attacks or blocks, put a -1/-1 counter on it" |
| "Whenever this creature attacks, remove a -1/-1 counter from target creature you control and put a -1/-1 counter on up to one target creature defending player controls" | `RemoveAndPutCounterOnAttackEffect()` | `ON_ATTACK` | Decimator Beetle. **Two targets** — the single-target attack pipeline can't collect them, so the effect implements marker `AttackCounterMoveEffect` and `CombatAttackService` routes it to the two-step `AttackCounterMoveFirstTarget` (creature you control) → `AttackCounterMoveSecondTarget` (up to one defending-player creature) flow. Independent halves (CR-accurate): puts even with nothing to remove; if one target becomes illegal the other still resolves |
| "When this creature dies, put a -1/-1 counter on target creature for each -1/-1 counter on it" | `PutCounterOnTargetForEachDyingSourceCounterEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE)` | `ON_DEATH` | Snapshots the dying creature's counter count of that type at death and puts that many on a targeted creature (mandatory target, any creature). Pair with `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` `EnterWithCountersEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, new Fixed(N))` for "enters with N -1/-1 counters" (e.g. Grief Tyrant). Unlike `MoveDyingSourceCountersToTargetCreatureEffect`, counts only the one counter type and always triggers |
| "When this creature dies, you **may** put a -1/-1 counter on target creature for each -1/-1 counter on it" | `PutCounterOnTargetForEachDyingSourceCounterEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, true)` | `ON_DEATH` | The `true` = optional "you may" form (Soulstinger): target still chosen as the trigger stacks (any creature), may decline placing the counters at resolution. Pairs with an `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` `target(new ControlledPermanentPredicateTargetFilter(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), …)).addEffect(…, PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 2))` for "put two -1/-1 counters on target creature you control" — the ETB's "you control" cast-time filter does **not** leak into this death trigger (the death trigger targets any creature) |
| "{cost}, {Q}: Move a counter from target creature onto a second target creature" | `MoveCounterFromTargetCreatureToTargetCreatureEffect()` | activated ability | Multi-target `ActivatedAbility` (two creature filters, min/max 2) + `.withRequiresUntap()` for `{Q}`. Moves one counter (first kind present) from target 0 to target 1; no-op if the first has no counters. Leech Bonder (`{U}, {Q}`) |
| "{cost}, {Q}: Double the number of each kind of counter on target permanent" | `DoubleCountersOnTargetPermanentEffect()` | activated ability | Single-target `ActivatedAbility` + `PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(new PermanentTruePredicate(), ...)` + `.withRequiresUntap()` for `{Q}`. Doubles every counter kind present on the target; no-op if none. Gilder Bairn (`{2}{G/U}, {Q}`) |
| "for each kind of counter on target permanent, put another counter of that kind on it or remove one from it" | `AdjustEachCounterKindOnTargetEffect()` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD (also SPELL/trigger) | Quarry Hauler. `target(new PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(new PermanentTruePredicate(), ...))` + this effect. Snapshots every counter kind present at resolution and asks the controller ADD/REMOVE once per kind (generic list-choice); no-op if the target has none. ADD routes through `PermanentCounterSupport.placeCounterOnPermanent` (preserves +1/+1/-1/-1 triggers, saga chapters) |
| "Move all counters from target creature onto another target creature" | `MoveCounterFromTargetCreatureToTargetCreatureEffect(true)` | SPELL | Two `target(creatureFilter)` groups, effect on the first (position 0 = source, 1 = destination). Moves every counter of every kind; distinct targets by default ("another"). Fate Transfer |
| "When this dies, create a N/N [color] [Subtype] creature token for each counter on it" | `CreateTokensForEachDyingSourceCounterEffect(new CreateTokenEffect("name", n, n, color, List.of(subtypes), Set.of(), Set.of()))` | `ON_DEATH` | Snapshots the dying creature's total counter count and creates that many tokens (e.g. Kinsbaile Borderguard). Distinct from `CreateTokenWithDyingSourceCountersEffect`, which makes one token carrying the counters |
| "create a N/N [color] [Subtype] creature token with [keyword]" | `CreateTokenEffect("name", N, N, color, subtype, keyword)` | SPELL/trigger | With keyword |
| "create a … token for each [thing]" / "create X … tokens, where X is …" | `CreateTokenEffect(DynamicAmount, "name", N, N, color, subtypes, keywords, additionalTypes)` | SPELL/trigger/ability | Any dynamic token count = `CreateTokenEffect` + a `DynamicAmount` (see EFFECTS_INDEX "Dynamic amounts") — never a new effect class. "for each charge counter on ~" = `CountersOnSource(CHARGE)`; "create X" = `XValue()`; "for each Equipment/Aura attached to ~" = `AttachmentsOnSource`; "for each creature you control" = `PermanentCount(IsCreature, CONTROLLER)`; "for each creature card in your graveyard" = `CardsInGraveyard(CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), CONTROLLER)`; "for each Forest you control" = `PermanentCount(HasSubtype(FOREST), CONTROLLER)`; "for each creature put into your graveyard this turn" = `CreatureDeathsThisTurn(CONTROLLER)`; "half the number of …, rounded down" = `Divided(count, 2)`. Non-default token flags (tappedAndAttacking, exileAtEndStep) use the canonical ctor |
| "create N tokens. If this spell was cast from a graveyard, create M of those tokens instead" | `CreateTokenEffect(N, ...)` + `ConditionalEffect(new CastFromZone(Zone.GRAVEYARD), new CreateTokenEffect(M - N, ...))` | SPELL | Add the base amount first, then the conditional extra amount; add `FlashbackCast` separately when appropriate |
| "Then if this spell was cast from anywhere other than your hand, [effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new CastNotFromHand(), ...)` | SPELL | Broader than graveyard-only; covers flashback and any future non-hand cast paths. E.g. Antiquities on the Loose |

## Graveyard return

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "return target [type] card from your graveyard to your hand" | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(predicate).targetGraveyard(true).build()` | SPELL | |
| "whenever a [subtype] you control enters, you may pay {cost}. If you do, return this card from your graveyard to your hand" | `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect(CardSubtypePredicate(...), MayPayManaEffect("{cost}", ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(CardIsSelfPredicate).returnAll(true).build(), prompt))` | `GRAVEYARD_ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Unconventional Tactics ({W}, Zombie). Fires from the controller's graveyard; the `MayPayManaEffect` goes on the stack and prompts payment on resolution |
| "return target creature card from your graveyard to the battlefield" | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).targetGraveyard(true).build()` | SPELL | |
| "return up to two target creature cards with power 2 or less from your graveyard to the battlefield" | `ReturnCardsFromControllerGraveyardToBattlefieldEffect(CardAllOfPredicate(List.of(CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), CardPowerAtMostPredicate(2))), 2)` | any slot (Reveillark: `ON_SELF_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD`) | Up-to-N return from controller's own graveyard; choice made at resolution (non-targeting), so it works from trigger slots with no graveyard-targeting pipeline |
| "return up to N target [type] cards from your graveyard to your hand" | `ReturnTargetCardsFromGraveyardToHandEffect(predicate, N)` | SPELL or `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` | Multi-target graveyard return-to-hand. SPELL: targets chosen at cast time (Morbid Plunder). ETB: `GraveyardTargetingService.handleReturnToHandETBTargeting` prompts a multi-graveyard choice (0..N) as the trigger goes on the stack; "up to N" covers the "you may" (Tilling Treefolk). |
| "you may shuffle up to N target cards from your graveyard into your library" | `ShuffleTargetCardsFromControllerGraveyardIntoLibraryEffect(null, N)` | `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` | Multi-target own-graveyard shuffle. Distinct from Memory's Journey's player-targeted `ShuffleTargetCardsFromGraveyardIntoLibraryEffect` and Put Away's resolution-time single-card `ShuffleCardFromControllerGraveyardIntoLibraryEffect` |
| "return target creature card ... to the battlefield with a mannequin counter on it. | "put target creature card from an opponent's graveyard onto the battlefield under your control" (permanent, no haste/exile) | `PutCardFromOpponentGraveyardOntoBattlefieldEffect(false, new CardTypePredicate(CardType.CREATURE), false)` | SPELL (Ashen Powder) | Registered in `stolenCreatures`, so it returns to its owner's graveyard on death. `requireManaValueEqualsX=false` ⇒ any MV and no mill (the Geth-style MV==X + mill-X path uses the `(boolean tapped)`/`()` constructors) |
| "Target opponent reveals cards from the top of their library until they reveal a creature card. | "Undying" (keyword) | none — loaded from Scryfall as `Keyword.UNDYING` | — | Engine handles the return-with-counter in `PermanentRemovalService.collectUndyingTrigger` + `UndyingReturnEffect`. Just register the printing. |

| "When this creature enters, return to your hand all cards in your graveyard that were put there from the battlefield this turn" | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).returnAll(true).fromBattlefieldThisTurn(true).build()` | `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` | Twilight Shepherd. `fromBattlefieldThisTurn` returns all card types (vs `thisTurnOnly` which is creatures only). |
| "Return to your hand all cards in your graveyard that you cycled or discarded this turn" | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).returnAll(true).discardedOrCycledThisTurn(true).build()` | SPELL | Shadow of the Grave. `discardedOrCycledThisTurn` reads `GameData.cardsDiscardedOrCycledThisTurn`, populated in the central discard hook `TriggerCollectionService.checkDiscardTriggers` (cycling is a discard, so a single tracking set covers both). Cards that reached the graveyard by other means (milled, destroyed, sacrificed) are not returned. |
| "Whenever this creature or another creature enters from your graveyard, that creature deals damage equal to its power to any target" | `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect(new SourcePower())` | `ON_CREATURE_ENTERS_FROM_GRAVEYARD` | Flayer of the Hatebound. The entering creature is the damage source (its power is read at resolution); any-target choice is handled by the `EntersFromGraveyardTriggerTarget` pipeline. |
| "Whenever this creature or another permanent enters from a graveyard, draw a card" | `DrawCardEffect()` | `ON_PERMANENT_ENTERS_FROM_GRAVEYARD` | River Kelpie. Distinct from `ON_CREATURE_ENTERS_FROM_GRAVEYARD` (Flayer of the Hatebound), which is creatures-only, controller's-graveyard-only, and any-target. |
| "Whenever a player casts a spell from a graveyard, draw a card" | `SpellCastTriggerEffect(null, List.of(new DrawCardEffect()), new StackEntryCastFromZonePredicate(Zone.GRAVEYARD))` | `ON_ANY_PLAYER_CASTS_SPELL` | River Kelpie. `castSpellTargetCondition` gates on the cast spell's `sourceZone == GRAVEYARD` (flashback etc.), excluding exile casts. |
| "Whenever a [subtype] creature enters, you may attach this Equipment to it" | `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect(new CardSubtypePredicate(subtype), new AttachSourceEquipmentToEnteringCreatureEffect())` | `ON_ANY_OTHER_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Cloak and Dagger (Rogue). Non-targeting "may attach" to the entering creature (any player's), materialised by the enter collector as `MayEffect(AttachSourceEquipmentToTargetCreatureEffect)`. |
| "Whenever another [subtype] you control enters, destroy target permanent" | `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect(new CardSubtypePredicate(subtype), new DestroyTargetPermanentEffect(false))` | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Reaper King (Scarecrow). "Another" is implicit (the entering creature never triggers its own controller's copy). Mandatory targeted enter trigger: a permanent-targeting effect in this slot is routed to the `EntersTriggerTarget` pipeline (controller picks any permanent) instead of a straight non-targeting stack entry. Pair with the STATIC subtype lord. |
| "Whenever a creature an opponent controls enters, you may attach this Aura to that creature" | `AttachSourceAuraToEnteringCreatureEffect()` | `ON_OPPONENT_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Prison Term (Aura). Non-targeting "may attach" moving the Aura onto the entering opponent creature; materialised by the enter collector as `MayEffect(AttachSourceAuraToTargetCreatureEffect)`. | "Sacrifice another permanent: Attach this Aura to target creature. | "When a [subtype] you control enters, return this enchantment to its owner's hand" | `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect(new CardSubtypePredicate(subtype), ReturnToHandEffect.self())` | `ON_ALLY_ENCHANTMENT_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Trial of Solidarity (CARTOUCHE).
