| "{cost}: Attach target Aura attached to a creature to another creature" | `AttachTargetAuraToTargetCreatureEffect()` | activated ability (multi-target) | Crown of the Ages. Two target filters: `PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(new PermanentIsAuraAttachedToCreaturePredicate(), ...)` for the Aura, `PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), ...)` for the destination creature; `minTargets=maxTargets=2`. Reads targetIds[0] = Aura, [1] = creature. |
| "Whenever a creature enters, its controller sacrifices a creature or land of their choice" | `SacrificePermanentsEffect(1, new PermanentAnyOfPredicate(List.of(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), new PermanentIsLandPredicate())), SacrificeRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)` | `ON_ANY_OTHER_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Tainted Aether. | "Whenever a creature enters, this enchantment deals N damage to it" | `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(N)` | `ON_ANY_OTHER_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Aether Flash. ## Counters

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "Whenever another creature enters, you may put X +1/+1 counters on this creature, where X is that creature's power" | `PutCountersOnSourceEqualToEnteringPowerEffect(1, 1, true)` | `ON_ANY_OTHER_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Hamletback Goliath. Entering creature's power read at trigger time; `optional=true` = "you may". Set `optional=false` for a mandatory variant. |
| "Whenever a creature you control with power N or greater enters, you may put M +1/+1 counters on it" | `EnteringCreatureMinPowerConditionalEffect(N, new PutCountersOnEnteringCreatureEffect(M))` | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Mighty Emergence (N=5, M=2). Counters go on the entering creature ("it"), not the source; the collector bakes the entering permanent id and materialises a `MayEffect(PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, M))`. Drop the min-power wrapper for an unconditional "whenever a creature you control enters" variant. |
| "Whenever a creature you control with power N or greater enters, you may put a +1/+1 counter on THIS creature" | `EnteringCreatureMinPowerConditionalEffect(N, new MayEffect(new PutCountersOnSourceEffect(1, 1, 1), "…"))` | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Godtracker of Jund (N=5). Counter goes on the source, not the entering creature. `handleEnterMay` binds the source permanent even for ally scans (no default target player), so the wrapped `PutCountersOnSourceEffect` resolves against the source. |
| "Whenever a creature you control enters, if that creature is X/Y, put M +1/+1 counters on it" | `EnteringCreatureExactStatsConditionalEffect(X, Y, new PutCountersOnEnteringCreatureEffect(M, false))` | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` | Sigil Captain (X=1, Y=1, M=2). Intervening-if "is 1/1" gate = exact printed power AND toughness; `optional=false` makes the counter placement mandatory (baked directly onto the stack, no "you may" prompt), unlike Mighty Emergence's may variant. |
| "CARDNAME enters the battlefield with N [type] counters on it" | `EnterWithCountersEffect(CounterType.X, new Fixed(N))` | `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` | As-enters replacement effect (CR 614.1c), applied during battlefield entry before ETB triggers/statics see the permanent. Trigons/Tumble Magnet (CHARGE), Djinn of Wishes (WISH) |
| "CARDNAME enters the battlefield with X [type] counters on it" (X-cost spell) | `EnterWithCountersEffect(CounterType.X, new XValue())` | `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` | X read from the resolving spell's stack entry; 0 when the permanent wasn't cast (tokens, reanimation). Chimeric Mass, Protean Hydra, Mikaeus the Lunarch |
| "enters with a +1/+1 counter on it for each [thing]" | `EnterWithCountersEffect(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, <DynamicAmount>)` | `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` | Any "enters with … for each …" wording = this effect + an amount, never a new class. "each creature that died this turn" = `CreatureDeathsThisTurn(ANY_PLAYER)` (Bloodcrazed Paladin); "each other Zombie you control and each Zombie card in your graveyard" = `Sum(PermanentCount(HasSubtype(ZOMBIE), CONTROLLER), CardsInGraveyard(CardSubtypePredicate(ZOMBIE), CONTROLLER))` (Unbreathing Horde) |
| "If CARDNAME was kicked, it enters the battlefield with N +1/+1 counters on it" | `ConditionalEffect(new Kicked(), new EnterWithCountersEffect(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, new Fixed(N)))` | `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` | Pair with `KickerEffect` on STATIC. Academy Drake, Baloth Gorger, Grunn the Lonely King |
| "Raid — CARDNAME enters the battlefield with a +1/+1 counter on it if you attacked this turn" | `ConditionalEffect(new Raid(), new EnterWithCountersEffect(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, new Fixed(1)))` | `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` | Rigging Runner, Storm Fleet Aerialist |
| "Each other [subtype] creature you control enters with an additional +1/+1 counter on it" | `ControlledCreaturesEnterWithAdditionalCountersEffect(CardSubtype.X, N)` | `STATIC` | Battlefield static replacement (CR 614.1c) on the source; "other" is implicit. Sage of Fables (WIZARD). Graveyard-active twin ("As long as CARDNAME is in your graveyard…") = `GraveyardEnterWithAdditionalCountersEffect` (Dearly Departed) |
| "Devour N (As this creature enters, you may sacrifice any number of creatures. It enters with N times that many +1/+1 counters on it.)" | `DevourEffect(N)` | `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` | As-enters replacement (CR 702.82); controller sacrifices any number of their *other* creatures via a multi-permanent choice, enters with `N ×` that many +1/+1 counters, records the devoured count. No other creatures ⇒ no prompt. Tar Fiend |
| "Exploit (When this creature enters, you may sacrifice a creature.)" | `MayEffect(new ExploitEffect(), "Sacrifice a creature?")` | `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` | CR 702.110. May sacrifice any controlled creature including self. Successful sacrifice while source was on battlefield at resolution start fires `ON_EXPLOIT`. Overcharged Amalgam |

| "{T}: Target land becomes a Forest until this creature leaves the battlefield" | `TargetLandBecomesForestUntilSourceLeavesEffect()` (ability, benign LAND target) + `TrackedLandsBecomeForestEffect()` in the STATIC slot | ability + STATIC | Gaea's Liege. The ability records the target land's id on the source permanent's `forestedLandIds`; the STATIC companion (layer 4, `applyL4Instance`) makes every recorded land a Forest (type-**replacing**, rule 305.7). The grant lives on the source permanent, so it ends automatically when the source leaves — no cleanup pass and no new duration. Because it enters the layered characteristic state it also feeds Forest-counting CDAs (Gaea's own P/T) |

Lands lacking A unaffected. Contrast Blood Moon (nonbasic-only). Conversion = `(MOUNTAIN, PLAINS)` |

| "Until your next upkeep, target noncreature artifact becomes an artifact creature with power and toughness each equal to its mana value" | `AnimatePermanentsEffect(new TargetManaValue(), new TargetManaValue(), List.of(), Set.of(), null, Set.of(), GrantScope.TARGET, EffectDuration.UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN, null)` | activated `{T}` | Xenic Poltergeist. | "Whenever one or more +1/+1 counters are put on CARDNAME" | `AwardAnyColorManaEffect()` (or other effects) | `ON_SELF_PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE_COUNTERS_PUT` | Fired from `PermanentCounterSupport` after each +1/+1 placement event (once per event). Used by Berta, Wise Extrapolator |
| "Whenever a -1/-1 counter is put on a creature, you may …" | any effect (e.g. `MayEffect(CreateTokenEffect(...))`) | `ON_MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE_COUNTER_PUT_ON_CREATURE` | Global watcher — fires for a -1/-1 counter put on ANY creature on any battlefield, from any source (placement, infect/wither damage, proliferate, or entering with counters incl. persist). Trigger controller = the source permanent's controller. Used by Flourishing Defenses |
| "Whenever **you** put one or more -1/-1 counters on a creature, …" | any effect (e.g. `CreateTokenEffect(...)` — one token per counter yields "that many") | `ON_YOU_PUT_MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE_COUNTER_ON_CREATURE` | Controller-restricted variant of the above — fires **only** for counters this card's controller puts (Gatherer ruling: an opponent's wither/infect creature or spell putting the counters does NOT trigger it). Same per-counter firing. Placing player = `gameData.currentlyResolvingControllerId` for spell/ability resolution, damage source's controller for wither/infect. Used by Nest of Scarabs |
| "Whenever **you** put one or more -1/-1 counters on **this creature**, [targeted effect]" | the targeted effect (e.g. `RemoveCounterFromTargetPermanentEffect(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, anotherCreatureYouControl)`) | `ON_SELF_MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE_COUNTERS_PUT` | Self-scoped -1/-1 mirror of `ON_SELF_PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE_COUNTERS_PUT`. Fires **once per placement event** (regardless of counter count), only when the placing player is this permanent's controller. A targeted effect chooses its target as the ability goes on the stack (reuses the `SpellTargetTriggerAnyTarget` interaction; the effect's `targetSpec()` predicate governs legal targets). Fired from `PermanentCounterSupport.fireSelfMinusOneMinusOneCountersPutTriggers`. Used by Defiant Greatmaw |
| "put N +1/+1 counters on target creature" | `PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect(CounterType.PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, N)` | SPELL/trigger | `(…, new XValue())` for "X +1/+1 counters" |
| "put a +1/+1 counter on each creature you control" | `PutCounterOnEachControlledPermanentEffect(CounterType.PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, 1, new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate())` | SPELL/trigger | |
| "remove a -1/-1 counter from each creature you control" | `RemoveCounterFromEachControlledPermanentEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 1, new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate())` | UPKEEP_TRIGGERED/SPELL/trigger | Heartmender. Mirror of `PutCounterOnEachControlledPermanentEffect`; removes up to N counters from each matching controlled permanent, clamped at zero (a permanent with none is unaffected) |
| "you may remove a counter from target permanent" | `MayEffect(RemoveCounterFromTargetPermanentEffect(), prompt)` on `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` + `target(PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(PermanentTruePredicate(), …))` | ETB trigger | Medicine Runner. Removes one counter of any kind (first present type when several); no-op if the target has none |
| "you may remove any number of +1/+1 counters from this creature. If you do, create that many 1/1 colorless Tetravite artifact creature tokens…" | `RemoveCountersToCreateTetraviteTokensEffect(tokenTemplate)` | UPKEEP_TRIGGERED | Tetravus. 0..N number choice (0 = decline); removes that many +1/+1 counters and creates that many tokens, tracked in `GameData.tetravusCreatedTokens`. No `MayEffect` wrapper — the 0 option is the decline |
| "you may exile any number of tokens created with this creature. If you do, put that many +1/+1 counters on this creature." | `ExileTetraviteTokensToPutCountersOnSelfEffect()` | UPKEEP_TRIGGERED | Tetravus. Multi-permanent choice over the source's tracked, still-alive tokens (any controller); exiles the chosen ones and puts that many +1/+1 counters on the source |
| "put a +1/+1 counter on each creature target player controls" | `PutPlusOnePlusOneCounterOnEachCreatureTargetPlayerControlsEffect()` bound to the player group via `target(...).addEffect(...)` | SPELL | Multi-target group binding. Practiced Offense |
| "target creature gains your choice of [keyword] or [keyword] until end of turn" | `GrantChosenKeywordToTargetEffect(List.of(Keyword.X, Keyword.Y))` bound to the creature group via `target(...).addEffect(...)` | SPELL | Multi-target group binding. Practiced Offense |
| "this creature gains your choice of [keyword]... until end of turn" (self, no target) | `GrantChosenKeywordToSelfEffect(List.of(Keyword.X, Keyword.Y))` | activated ability effects list | Self grant, no target. Pair with `BoostSelfEffect(-1,-1)` for the -1/-1. Urza's Avenger |
| "damage to target creature equal to the amount of mana spent to cast this spell" | `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(new ManaSpentToCast())` | SPELL | Total mana spent snapshotted at cast time (`SpellCastingService` keys on the `ManaSpentToCast` amount). Molten Note |
| "put a -1/-1 counter on target creature" | `PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 1)` | SPELL/trigger | `(…, count, true)` regenerates if it survives (Gore Vassal) |
| "distribute two -1/-1 counters among one or two target creatures" | `target(creatureFilter, 1, 2).addEffect(SPELL, new DistributeCountersAmongTargetsEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 2))` | SPELL/trigger | Splendid Agony. Even split of the total across the chosen target group (1 target → 2 counters; 2 targets → 1 each), which is the forced CR 601.2d distribution for two counters among ≤2 targets. Counter-type generic — Common Bond is the `PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE` twin. Do NOT use for a real three-way choose-your-division |
| "put a -1/-1 counter on each attacking creature / each other creature / each creature (X)" | `PutCounterOnEachMatchingPermanentEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, amount, predicate, EachPermanentScope.ALL_PLAYERS)` | SPELL/trigger | predicate = `AllOf(IsCreature, IsAttacking)` / `AllOf(IsCreature, Not(IsSourceCard))` / `IsCreature` (with `XValue()`). Choking Fumes, Carnifex Demon, Black Sun's Zenith |
| "deals N damage to each attacking or blocking creature target player controls" | `DealDamageToEachMatchingPermanentEffect(N, AllOf(IsCreature, AnyOf(IsAttacking, IsBlocking)), EachPermanentScope.TARGET_PLAYER)` | ACTIVATED_ABILITY | Brigid, Hero of Kinsbaile |
| "put a +1/+1 counter on CARDNAME. If this is the Nth time this ability has resolved this turn, remove all +1/+1 counters and it deals that much damage to each creature and each player" | `PutCountersOnSelfEffect(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE)` + `ConditionalEffect(new NthAbilityResolutionThisTurn(N), new RemoveAllCountersFromSelfEffect(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE))` + `ConditionalEffect(new NthAbilityResolutionThisTurn(N), new MassDamageEffect(new EventValue(), true))` | ACTIVATED_ABILITY | Resolutions counted per source permanent this turn (engine-side, in `StackResolutionService`); the condition fires only on the exact Nth. The removal snapshots the removed count as the entry's event value; the mass damage reads it back as "that much". Ashling the Pilgrim (N=3) |
| "creatures you control get +1/+0 until end of turn. If this is the third time this ability has resolved this turn, creatures you control gain first strike until end of turn" | `BoostAllOwnCreaturesEffect(1, 0)` + `InnerFlameIgniterEffect()` | ACTIVATED_ABILITY | Pump is unconditional; card-specific effect counts resolutions per source permanent and grants first strike only on the exact third. Inner-Flame Igniter |
| "target creature gains trample until end of turn. If this is the third time this ability has resolved this turn, you may add {R}{R}{R}{R}{R}{R}{R}{R}" | `GrantKeywordEffect(TRAMPLE, TARGET)` + `SoulbrightFlamekinEffect()` | ACTIVATED_ABILITY | Trample grant is unconditional; card-specific effect counts resolutions per source permanent and adds 8 red mana only on the exact third. "You may" is a no-op (no mana burn). Soulbright Flamekin |
| "put a -1/-1 counter on each creature target player controls" | `PutCounterOnEachMatchingPermanentEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 1, IsCreature, EachPermanentScope.TARGET_PLAYER)` | SPELL/trigger | targets a player. Contagion Engine |
| "proliferate" | `ProliferateEffect()` | SPELL/trigger | |
| "put N <named> counters on CARDNAME" | `PutCountersOnSelfEffect(CounterType.X, N)` | trigger/ability | for a non-P/T named counter type on the source (e.g. Jar of Eyeballs: `CounterType.EYEBALL, 2`) |
| "Remove all <named> counters from CARDNAME: Look at the top X cards…" | `RemoveAllCountersAsCostEffect(CounterType.X)` + `LookAtTopCardsEffect.chooseOneToHandRestOnBottom(new XValue())` | ability | X = counters removed, snapshotted into xValue (Jar of Eyeballs: `CounterType.EYEBALL`). The look effect reads xValue, so it works for any counter-removal cost that snapshots X |

## Tap / untap

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "tap enchanted creature" | `TapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.ENCHANTED)` | ability | aura's own activated ability; no targeting |
| "untap enchanted creature" | `UntapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.ENCHANTED)` | ability | aura's own activated ability; no targeting. Instill Energy pairs it with a `{0}` cost, `ONLY_DURING_YOUR_TURN` timing and `maxActivationsPerTurn=1` |
| "whenever this creature is dealt damage, it deals that much damage to any target" | `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect(new XValue())` | `ON_DEALT_DAMAGE` | Spitemare — the ON_DEALT_DAMAGE trigger paths (combat + non-combat) snapshot the damage dealt into xValue and queue an any-target choice |
| "whenever enchanted creature is dealt damage, it deals that much damage to its controller" | `EnchantedCreatureDealsDamageEqualToDealtDamageToControllerEffect()` | `ON_ENCHANTED_CREATURE_DEALT_DAMAGE` | Spiteful Shadows |
| "whenever enchanted creature deals damage to you, this Aura deals that much damage to that creature's controller" | `EnchantedCreatureDealsDamageEqualToDealtDamageToControllerEffect()` | `ON_ENCHANTED_CREATURE_DEALS_DAMAGE_TO_YOU` | Backfire |
| "whenever enchanted creature attacks and isn't blocked, you may have it assign no combat damage this turn. If you do, defending player discards a card at random" | `MayEffect(new AssignNoCombatDamageAndDefendingPlayerDiscardsEffect(), ...)` | `ON_ENCHANTED_CREATURE_ATTACKS_UNBLOCKED` | Cloak of Confusion. Aura enchants a creature you control; the enchanted attacker is baked as the trigger's non-targeting `sourcePermanentId` and the defending player as `targetId`. On accept the attacker is added to `creaturesPreventedFromDealingCombatDamage` (deals no combat damage this turn) and the defender discards at random. Collected in `CombatBlockService.collectUnblockedAttackTriggers` |
| "whenever a creature is dealt damage, destroy it. It can't be regenerated" | `DestroyTargetPermanentEffect(true)` | `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DEALT_DAMAGE` | Death Pits of Rath — queued entry auto-targets the damaged creature |
| "whenever a creature dealt damage by this creature this turn dies, put that card onto the battlefield under your control at the beginning of the next end step. Sacrifice it when you lose control of this creature" | `RegisterDelayedReturnDamagedCreatureUnderControlEffect()` | `ON_DAMAGED_CREATURE_DIES` | Seraph. Trigger stamps the dying card id onto `StackEntry.triggeringCardId`; the return (delayed to next end step) puts the card under your control with a PERMANENT control effect + `stolenCreatures` owner record; `StateBasedActionService` sacrifices linked creatures on Seraph control-loss (`GameData.seraphReturnedCreatures`) |
| "whenever a creature dealt damage by equipped creature this turn dies, you may exile that card. If you do, create a 2/2 black Zombie creature token" | `MayEffect(new ExileDyingCreatureCardAndCreateTokenEffect(CreateTokenEffect.blackZombie(1)), "…")` | `ON_DAMAGED_CREATURE_DIES` | Unscythe, Killer of Kings (Equipment). On an Equipment the slot fires for the **currently-equipped** creature's damage — `GraveyardService.triggerDamagedCreatureDiesAbilities` scans Equipment attached to the damaging creature (rulings: only the currently-equipped creature is checked, even if the Equipment wasn't attached when the damage was dealt; any damage counts, not just combat). The effect implements `DyingCreatureCardAwareEffect` so the collector binds the dying card id; exile (and thus the token) only happens if the card is still in a graveyard |
| "whenever a [subtype] you control deals damage to a creature, that [subtype] deals that much damage to that creature's controller" | `ReflectAllyDamageToDamagedCreatureControllerEffect(new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(subtype))` | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_DEALS_DAMAGE_TO_CREATURE` | Greatbow Doyen — fires for combat and non-combat damage; the source creature (not the watcher) deals the reflected damage |
| "whenever this creature deals damage to a creature, this creature deals N damage to that creature's controller and M damage to you" | `DamageDamagedCreatureControllerAndSelfEffect(N, M)` | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_DEALS_DAMAGE_TO_CREATURE` | Bellowing Fiend — self-scoped (only when this creature dealt the damage); fires for combat and non-combat damage; expands into `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(N, TARGET_PLAYER)` + `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(M, CONTROLLER)` on one stack entry |
| "whenever a red creature or spell deals damage, this enchantment deals that much damage to that creature's or spell's controller" | `ReflectSourceDamageToItsControllerEffect(CardColor.RED)` | `ON_ANY_SOURCE_DEALS_DAMAGE` | Justice — global watcher across combat and non-combat; all damage one source deals at once is summed into a single reflection (CR ruling), dealt by the watcher to the source's controller. Parameterize the color for any "whenever a [color] source deals damage" card |
| "tap target [permanent]" | `TapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.TARGET)` | SPELL/ability | target filter from the ability/spell target spec |
| "tap target creature unless its controller pays N life" | `TapTargetCreatureUnlessControllerPaysLifeEffect(N)` | ability | Vectis Dominator (`{T}:`, 2 life). Punisher tap — the **target creature's controller** (not the ability controller) chooses pay-life vs. tap; can't-pay auto-taps. Pair the ability with `target(new PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), …))`. Reuses the normal tap path (fires "becomes tapped" triggers); choice in `MayPenaltyChoiceHandlerService.handleTapTargetCreatureUnlessControllerPaysLifeChoice` |
| "untap target [permanent]" | `UntapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.TARGET[, predicate])` | SPELL/ability | predicate restricts valid targets |
| "Untap target creature. | "Whenever ~ deals combat damage to a player, untap target creature or land." | `UntapChosenPermanentEffect(PermanentAnyOfPredicate(PermanentIsCreaturePredicate, PermanentIsLandPredicate))` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Initiate's Companion. Combat-damage slots have no targeting pipeline, so the "target" is a **resolution-time choice**: pushed non-targeting, then the controller picks one matching permanent across every battlefield to untap (`MultiPermanentChoiceContext.UntapChosenPermanent`). Use this pattern for any no-target-pipeline trigger that untaps a chosen permanent |
| "tap all [permanents] target player controls" | `TapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.TARGET_PLAYERS_PERMANENTS, predicate)` | SPELL/ability | targets a player (Sleep, Tempest Caller) |

## Control / steal

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "if a player has more life than each other player, the player with the most life gains control of this creature" | `PlayerWithMostLifeGainsControlOfSourceCreatureEffect()` | UPKEEP_TRIGGERED | Ghazbán Ogre — no-op on a tie for most life (intervening-if) |
| "gain control of target [permanent]" | `GainControlOfTargetEffect(ControlDuration.PERMANENT)` | SPELL | Permanent |
| "gain control of target creature with power <= creature count" | `GainControlOfTargetEffect(ControlDuration.PERMANENT)` + `PermanentPowerAtMostControlledCreatureCountPredicate` filter | ability | Dynamic power check vs creature count |
| "gain control of target creature until end of turn" | `GainControlOfTargetEffect(ControlDuration.END_OF_TURN)` | SPELL | Threaten |
| "gain control of target [permanent] until end of turn. Untap it and it gains haste" | flat `GainControlOfTargetEffect(END_OF_TURN)` + `UntapPermanentsEffect(TARGET)` + `GrantKeywordEffect(HASTE, TARGET)` (Threaten) | any | Add the three as separate `SPELL` effects on one target (Act of Treason). When the whole rider must sit inside one `MayEffect`, wrap them in a `SequenceEffect` (next row) |
| "At the beginning of your upkeep, you may gain control of target permanent until end of turn. If you do, untap it and it gains haste" | `MayEffect(SequenceEffect.of(GainControlOfTargetEffect(END_OF_TURN), UntapPermanentsEffect(TARGET), GrantKeywordEffect(HASTE, TARGET)), prompt)` on `UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` + `PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(PermanentTruePredicate(), ...)` | UPKEEP_TRIGGERED | Dominus of Fealty — `MayEffect` wraps exactly one effect, so `SequenceEffect` bundles the three primitives as one unit. Accepting the may makes gain-control happen, so untap+haste are unconditional (plain, non-contingent sequence is rules-correct). Target chosen at resolution after the may is accepted (engine's targeted-may flow), any permanent |
| "gain control of target [permanent] for as long as you control [source]" | `GainControlOfTargetEffect(ControlDuration.WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD)` | ability | Olivia Voldaren |
| "you and target player exchange control of the creature you each control with the greatest mana value, then artifacts the same way" | `JuxtaposeEffect()` | SPELL | Juxtapose — targets a player (player-targeting spec). Creatures exchanged first, then artifacts on the updated board (artifact creatures can move in both steps); ties prompt the controlling player; a side with no permanent of that type skips that exchange |
| "gain control of all lands target player controls" | `GainControlOfAllLandsTargetPlayerControlsEffect()` | ability | Gilt-Leaf Archdruid — targets a player (player-targeting spec), permanent control of every land they control at resolution. Cost "tap seven untapped Druids you control" = `TapMultiplePermanentsCost(7, PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(DRUID))` |
| "gain control of target creature … for as long as you control [source] and [source] remains tapped" | `GainControlOfTargetEffect(ControlDuration.WHILE_SOURCE_TAPPED)` | ability | Seasinger — `{T}` cost keeps the source tapped; pair with `MayNotUntapDuringUntapStepEffect` static + a `PermanentControllerControlsPermanentPredicate` target filter (creature whose controller controls an Island). Control ends the instant the source untaps or leaves |
| "Untap target artifact an opponent controls and gain control of it until end of turn. It gains haste until end of turn. When you lose control of the artifact, tap it." | `GainControlOfTargetEffect(ControlDuration.END_OF_TURN, true)` + `UntapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.TARGET)` + `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.HASTE, GrantScope.TARGET)` | activated ability (`{1}{U}, {T}`) | Magus of the Unseen. The `tapWhenControlLost=true` flag on the gain-control effect taps the artifact when the until-end-of-turn control effect expires at cleanup (via `GameData.permanentsToTapWhenControlLost`, tapped in `TurnCleanupService`). Target filter = artifact + `PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentControlledBySourceControllerPredicate())` |
| "you and target player exchange control of the creature you each control with the greatest mana value, then artifacts the same way" | `JuxtaposeEffect()` | SPELL | Juxtapose — targets a player (`canTargetPlayer`). Creatures exchanged first, then artifacts on the updated board (artifact creatures can move in both steps); ties prompt the controlling player; a side with no permanent of that type skips that exchange |
| "{cost}, Sacrifice this artifact: Exchange control of target artifact, creature, or land you control and target permanent an opponent controls that shares one of those types with it. If those permanents are exchanged this way, destroy all Auras attached to them." | multi-target `ActivatedAbility` (`SacrificeSelfCost` + `ExchangeControlOfSharedTypeTargetsAndDestroyAurasEffect()`), positions `ControlledPermanentPredicateTargetFilter(artifact/creature/land)` + `PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(opponent-controlled artifact/creature/land)`, `.withMultiTargetConstraint(MultiTargetConstraint.SHARE_ARTIFACT_CREATURE_OR_LAND_TYPE)` | activated | Gauntlets of Chaos — cross-target "shares one of those types" enforced at announcement by the constraint; handler swaps controllers permanently then destroys Auras attached to either permanent |
| "gain control of all lands target player controls" | `GainControlOfAllLandsTargetPlayerControlsEffect()` | ability | Gilt-Leaf Archdruid — targets a player (`canTargetPlayer`), permanent control of every land they control at resolution. Cost "tap seven untapped Druids you control" = `TapMultiplePermanentsCost(7, PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(DRUID))` |
| "Whenever this creature attacks and isn't blocked, you may gain control of target land defending player controls for as long as you control this creature. If you do, this creature assigns no combat damage this turn" | `MayEffect(new GainControlOfLandDefendingPlayerControlsAndAssignNoCombatDamageEffect())` | ON_ATTACKS_UNBLOCKED | Orcish Squatters. Non-targeting trigger (`targetId`=defender, `sourcePermanentId`=attacker); at resolution a max-1 choice among the defender's lands. Taking one gains control `WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD` and adds the attacker to `creaturesPreventedFromDealingCombatDamage`. Completion in `MultiPermanentChoiceHandlerService` |
| "At end of combat, gain control of all creatures blocking this creature for as long as you control this creature" | `GainControlOfCombatOpponentAtEndOfCombatEffect()` | ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED (`TriggerMode.PER_BLOCKER`) | The Wretched. One trigger per blocker; each queues a `GainControlOfPermanentAtEndOfCombat` delayed action drained in `CombatService.processEndOfCombatControlGains()`, applying `WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD` control keyed to the source. Add only to `ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED` (blockers only, not creatures this blocks) |
| "When this enters, gain control of all [subtype]s, then untap all [subtype]s" | `GainControlOfAllPermanentsMatchingEffect(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(X))` + `UntapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.ALL_CREATURES, PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(X))` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD | Karrthus, Tyrant of Jund (X=DRAGON). Pair with STATIC `GrantKeywordEffect(HASTE, OWN_CREATURES, PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(X))` for "Other [subtype] creatures you control have haste" |
| "{cost}, {T}, Tap two untapped red creatures you control: deals 3 damage to any target" + "{cost}, {Q}, Untap two tapped blue creatures you control: Return target creature to its owner's hand" | two `ActivatedAbility`s: `TapMultiplePermanentsCost(2, PermanentAllOfPredicate(creature+red))` + `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect(3, false)`; and `UntapMultiplePermanentsCost(2, PermanentAllOfPredicate(creature+blue))` + `ReturnToHandEffect.target()` `.withRequiresUntap()` | activated abilities | Crackleburr. `UntapMultiplePermanentsCost` is the `{Q}` untap-symbol mirror of `TapMultiplePermanentsCost` (untaps N *tapped* matching permanents as cost) |
| "you control enchanted creature" (aura STATIC) | `ControlEnchantedCreatureEffect()` | STATIC | Mind Control, Persuasion, Volition Reins — the STATIC control-magic aura effect (`StackResolutionService` wires it on aura resolution). Pair "untap enchanted creature as it enters" with `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` + `UntapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.TARGET)` (reuses the aura's target). NOTE: `GainControlOfEnchantedTargetEffect()` is the *activated-ability* variant (Rootwater Matriarch), not the aura STATIC one |
| "When enchanted creature dies, return that card to the battlefield under its owner's control" | `ReturnEnchantedCreatureToBattlefieldUnderOwnersControlOnDeathEffect()` | ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD | Abduction. | "When enchanted creature dies, that creature's controller loses life equal to its toughness" | `EnchantedCreatureControllerLosesLifeEffect(0)` | ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD | Banewasp Affliction. Card-def amount is a placeholder — the death collector bakes in the dying creature's last-known toughness (clamped to ≥0) and its controller. | "When enchanted creature dies, this Aura deals damage equal to that creature's toughness to the creature's controller" | `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(0, DamageRecipient.ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER)` | ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD | Creature Bond. | "gain control of target creature (Rootwater Matriarch activated ability)" | `GainControlOfEnchantedTargetEffect()` | activated | Control persists for as long as the target remains enchanted |
| "At the beginning of your end step, clash with an opponent. If you win, gain control of enchanted creature. ## Mana

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "add {C}" / "add one mana of [color]" | `AwardManaEffect(ManaColor.X, 1)` | ON_TAP/ability | |
| "add {B} or {R}" (or any fixed set of colors) | `AwardManaOfColorsEffect(List.of(ManaColor.BLACK, ManaColor.RED))` | ability/ON_TAP | Manaforge Cinder — one ability, player chooses among the listed colors. Use this (not one ability per color) when the printed ability has a shared per-turn cap like "activate no more than three times each turn" (`maxActivationsPerTurn` on the single `ActivatedAbility`) |
| "add [color] for each [X] you control" | `AwardManaEffect(ManaColor.X, new PermanentCount(filter, CountScope.CONTROLLER))` | ability | Elvish Archdruid, Cabal Stronghold, Itlimoc, Koth −2, Powerstone Shard |
| "add {C} for each charge counter on it" | `AwardManaEffect(ManaColor.COLORLESS, new CountersOnSource(CounterType.CHARGE))` | ability | Shrine of Boundless Growth |
| "add [color] equal to its power" | `AwardManaEffect(ManaColor.X, new SourcePower())` | ability/trigger | Marwyn, the Nurturer; Molten-Core Maestro |
| "add {R} for each 1 life your opponents have lost this turn" | `AwardManaEffect(ManaColor.RED, new LifeLostThisTurn(CountScope.OPPONENTS))` | `POSTCOMBAT_MAIN_TRIGGERED` | Neheb, the Eternal — see life-loss row above |
| "At the beginning of your first main phase, remove all flood counters from this. If none removed, put a flood counter on it and draw a card. Not a mana ability — beginning-of-step trigger uses the stack |
| "{T}: Reveal any number of creature cards with power 5 or greater from your hand. Add {G} for each card revealed this way" | `AwardManaEffect(ManaColor.GREEN, new MatchingCardsInHand(CountScope.CONTROLLER, new CardAllOfPredicate(List.of(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), new CardPowerAtLeastPredicate(5)))))` | mana ability | Sacellum Godspeaker. Revealing has no downside, so "any number" is modelled as the whole set of qualifying hand cards (cf. Phosphorescent Feast). `MatchingCardsInHand` = predicate-filtered `CardsInHand` |

## Prevention

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "This turn, whenever an attacking creature deals combat damage to you, it deals that much damage to its controller" | `RegisterCombatDamageReflectionEffect()` | SPELL | Harsh Justice. Registers a `DelayedCombatDamageReflection(controllerId)` delayed action for the rest of the turn; `CombatDamageService.processCombatDamageReflectionTriggers` fires one trigger per attacking creature that dealt combat damage to the protected player, dealing that much back to its controller with the attacking creature as the damage source. Cleared at turn cleanup. Usually paired with `setSpellCastTimingRestriction(DECLARE_ATTACKERS_IF_ATTACKED)` |
| "prevent all combat damage that would be dealt this turn" | `PreventDamageEffect.allCombat()` | SPELL | |
| "Prevent all combat damage target creature would deal this turn" | `PreventDamageEffect.allCombatByTargetCreatures()` | SPELL/ability | Resistance Fighter (`Sacrifice this creature:`). Combat-only variant — adds the target to `creaturesPreventedFromDealingCombatDamage`, gating attacker participation in `CombatDamageService`. Use `PreventDamageEffect.allByTargetCreatures()` for "prevent all damage target creature would deal" (Soul Parry, Inquisitor's Snare) |
| "Prevent all damage that would be dealt to you this turn by attacking creatures" | `PreventDamageEffect.allToControllerFromAttackers()` | SPELL | Deep Wood. Protects only the caster (not their creatures) and only from attacking creatures. Pair with `setSpellCastTimingRestriction(DECLARE_ATTACKERS_IF_ATTACKED)` |
| "Prevent all combat damage that would be dealt to attacking creatures you control" | `PreventCombatDamageToAttackingCreaturesYouControlEffect()` | STATIC | Dolmen Gate. Only combat damage to *attacking* creatures the controller controls; noncombat unaffected. Hooked in `DamagePreventionService.applyCreaturePreventionShield` |
| "Prevent all noncombat damage that would be dealt to creatures you control" | `PreventNoncombatDamageToCreaturesYouControlEffect()` | STATIC | Mark of Asylum. Every creature the controller controls (re-evaluated per damage event, so it covers creatures gained later); combat damage unaffected; also stops wither/infect noncombat damage (the damage is prevented, so no -1/-1 counters). Hooked in `DamagePreventionService.applyCreaturePreventionShield` (the `!isCombatDamage` branch) |
| "prevent the next N damage that would be dealt to target" | `PreventDamageEffect.nextToTarget(N)` | SPELL | |
| "Prevent the next N damage that would be dealt to you this turn" | `PreventDamageEffect.nextToController(N)` | activated ability (no target) | Esper Battlemage (`{W},{T}`). | "Prevent the next N damage that would be dealt this turn to any number of targets, divided as you choose" | `PreventDividedDamageEffect(N)` | SPELL (no `target()` call) | Remedy. Reverse of divided damage: per-target shield amounts come from the cast-time `damageAssignments` map (harness `castInstant(player, idx, Map)`), summing to N; each target (creature and/or player) gets a "next X damage" shield. N caps the target count. Triggers the damage-distribution cast flow (`EffectResolution.needsDamageDistribution`). Shields expire at end of turn |
| "COST: Prevent the next N damage that would be dealt to this creature this turn" | `PreventDamageEffect.nextToSelf(N)` | activated ability (no target) | Ethereal Champion. Shields the ability's own source permanent (no target) via the permanent's `damagePreventionShield`; next N damage from any source (combat or noncombat), then consumed. | "prevent all damage that would be dealt to target creature this turn" | `PreventDamageEffect.allToTargetCreatures()` | SPELL/ability | Target creature only. Wellgabber Apothecary — combine with a `PermanentPredicateTargetFilter` for subtype/tapped restrictions. Multi-target aware: for "up to two target creatures" use `target(filter, 0, 2).addEffect(SPELL, ...)` (Redeem) — the handler shields each target in the group |
| "Prevent all damage that would be dealt to ~ this turn" (the source itself) | `PreventDamageEffect.allToSelf()` | ability | No target — shields `entry.getSourcePermanentId()` via `creaturesWithAllDamagePrevented`. | "Prevent all combat damage that would be dealt to it this turn" (the source itself) | `PreventDamageEffect.allCombatToSelf()` | ability/trigger | No target — combat-only variant of `allToSelf()`; shields `entry.getSourcePermanentId()` via `creaturesWithCombatDamagePrevented` (noncombat damage unaffected). | "{T}, Exert this creature: [effect]" (exert as an **activated-ability cost**) | `new SkipNextUntapEffect(TapUntapScope.SELF)` first in the ability's effects list, before the actual effect | activated ability (`requiresTap=true`, empty mana cost for tap-only) | Steward of Solidarity. Exert ("won't untap during your next untap step") has no dedicated cost record; model it as the skip-untap effect on the source. The `{T}` is the ability's tap cost (first ctor arg). Distinct from exert-**as-attack-trigger** (Battlefield Scavenger / Oketra's Avenger), which wraps it in a `MayEffect` on `ON_ATTACK`. When the payoff produces mana (Oasis Ritualist: `AwardAnyColorManaEffect(2)`), the whole ability is a mana ability — `SkipNextUntapEffect(SELF)` is applied inline in `ActivatedAbilityExecutionService.doResolveManaAbility` (same rider pattern as Pyramid's `PutCountersOnSelfEffect`) |

| "prevent all damage that would be dealt to artifact creatures this turn" | `PreventDamageEffect.allToMatchingPermanents(predicate)` | trigger/SPELL (no target) | Ethersworn Shieldmage.
