Combat prevented in `DamagePreventionService.applyCreaturePreventionShield` (combat source is always a creature); noncombat via `GameQueryService.isCreatureSourceDamageToSelfPrevented` hooked in `DamageSupport.dealCreatureDamage` |
| "If a source would deal damage to this creature, prevent that damage. The source's controller draws cards equal to the damage prevented this way" | `PreventDamageToSelfAndSourceControllerDrawsEffect()` | STATIC | Swans of Bryn Argoll. Prevents all damage (combat + noncombat, any source) to itself; the source's controller draws one card per point prevented. Via `DamagePreventionService.applySwansSourceControllerDraw`, hooked in `DamageSupport.dealCreatureDamage` + `CombatDamageService.applyCombatCreatureDamage` |
| "The next time a [color / artifact] source of your choice would deal damage to you this turn, prevent that damage" | `PreventDamageFromChosenSourceEffect.nextDamageToYou(predicate, label)` (e.g. `new PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(CardColor.RED)), "red"` or `new PermanentIsArtifactPredicate(), "artifact"`) | activated ability | Circle of Protection cycle. One-shot: only the *next* damage event from the chosen source is prevented (double strike's second hit still lands). Not the `ALL_DAMAGE_THIS_TURN` scope (`allDamage`/`allDamageToYou` factories), which prevents all damage that turn |
| "The next time a source of your choice would deal damage to you this turn, prevent that damage. You gain life equal to the damage prevented this way" | `PreventDamageFromChosenSourceEffect.nextDamageToYouAndGainLife()` | SPELL | Reverse Damage. Like the Circle of Protection effect but no color restriction (any permanent is a valid source) and the controller gains life equal to the damage prevented. One-shot: only the *next* damage event from the chosen source is prevented (combat or noncombat) |
| "The next time a source of your choice would deal damage to you this turn, prevent that damage" (no life gain) | `PreventDamageFromChosenSourceEffect.nextDamageToYou()` | activated ability | Pentagram of the Ages (`{4},{T}`). Same as Reverse Damage's effect but no life gain; any permanent is a valid source |
| "The next time a source of your choice would deal damage to any target this turn, prevent that damage" | `PreventDamageFromChosenSourceEffect.nextDamageToAnyTarget()` | activated ability (usually with `SacrificeSelfCost`) | Sanctum Guardian. Like Reverse Damage but protects **any** target (player, planeswalker, or creature), not just the controller, and grants no life. One-shot: only the *next* damage event from the chosen source is prevented (combat or noncombat). Shield keyed by source ID in `GameData.sourceNextDamageToAnyTargetShields`, consumed by `DamagePreventionService.applyChosenSourceNextDamageToAnyTargetShield` (hooked in every player/creature/planeswalker damage path) |
| "The next time a source of your choice would deal damage to you this turn, instead that source deals that much damage to you and ~ deals that much damage to that source's controller" | `EyeForAnEyeEffect()` | SPELL | Eye for an Eye. Reflection (not prevention): you still take the damage, and an equal reflected damage event is dealt back at the chosen source's controller by Eye for an Eye. One-shot: only the *next* damage event from the chosen source (combat or noncombat). Shield in `GameData.eyeForAnEyeShields`, applied by `DamagePreventionService.applyEyeForAnEyeReflection` (hooked in `DamageSupport.dealDamageToPlayer` + `CombatDamageService.accumulatePlayerDamage`), reflected damage processed via `pendingEyeForAnEyeReflections` |
| "Protection from everything" | `ProtectionFromEverythingEffect()` | `STATIC` | Progenitus. Protection from every source (any colour/type/subtype/mana value) — can't be blocked, targeted, dealt damage, or enchanted/equipped by anything. Consulted in `GameQueryService.hasProtectionFromSourceCardTypes` (every source has a card type) |
| "If ~ would be put into a graveyard from anywhere, exile it instead" | `ExileInsteadOfGraveyardReplacementEffect()` | STATIC | Disturb back faces (Luminous Phantom). Checked in `GraveyardService` and when a transformed permanent's current face has this effect (`PermanentRemovalService`). Sibling of `ShuffleIntoLibraryReplacementEffect` |
| "Disturb {cost}" | `addCastingOption(new DisturbCast("{cost}"))` + back face via `setBackFaceCard` | casting option | Cast from graveyard transformed (CR 702.146). Wire through the flashback graveyard-cast path (`playFlashbackSpell` / frontend `flashback` flag). Permanent enters back-face up (`StackEntry.castWithDisturb`). Aura backs (Twinblade Invocation): put `target(...)` + STATIC effects on the **back face** class; cast validates/targets using back-face characteristics; `CardViewFactory.createForGraveyard` ORs back-face `needsTarget` for UI |
| "Miracle {cost}" | `addCastingOption(new MiracleCast("{cost}"))` | casting option | Temporal Mastery. Cost declared on the card (not Scryfall-parsed). DrawService offers reveal on first draw of the turn; accepting pushes a miracle trigger whose resolution offers cast-for-miracle-cost (ignores type timing). Keyword.MIRACLE mapped from Scryfall |
| "Whenever another creature you control leaves the battlefield, you gain N life" | `GainLifeEffect(N)` | `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD` | Luminous Phantom. Controller-scoped leave watcher |
| "If ~ would die, put it on top of its owner's library instead" | `PutOnTopOfLibraryInsteadOfDyingEffect()` | `STATIC` | Gravebane Zombie. Replacement effect — only fires on a "die" (battlefield → graveyard); the card goes to library top instead of the graveyard. Checked in `GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard` |
| "If a creature would enter the battlefield under an opponent's control this turn, it enters under your control instead" | `GatherSpecimensEffect()` | `SPELL` | Gather Specimens. Turn-scoped control-changing replacement (CR 614.1); adds the controller to `GameData.playersGatheringSpecimensThisTurn`. Applied by `BattlefieldEntryService.resolveEnteringController` (called in `putPermanentOntoBattlefield` for placement and in the `StackResolutionService` creature/artifact spell paths for ETB/log/legend attribution). Cleared at turn cleanup |
| "As this artifact enters, choose an opponent. The chosen player's maximum hand size is N" | `SetOpponentMaximumHandSizeEffect(N)` | `STATIC` | Cursed Rack (N=4). The "choose an opponent" is implicit (the controller's opponent(s), matching Booby Trap's single-opponent model) — no ETB effect needed. `TurnCleanupService.getMaxHandSize` folds it with reductions in timestamp order (CR 402.2); `NoMaximumHandSizeEffect` still wins |
| "You have no maximum hand size. If an effect causes you to discard a card, discard it, but you may put it on top of your library instead" | `NoMaximumHandSizeEffect()` + `DiscardToTopOfLibraryInsteadEffect()` | `STATIC` | Library of Leng. The discard replacement affects only the controller's own effect-caused discards; checked in `GraveyardService.discardCard` (the choke point all discard sites route through). Modeled as always keeping the card — it still counts as a discard, so discard triggers still fire |
| "When ~ is put into a graveyard from the battlefield, return it to its owner's hand" | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardIsSelfPredicate()).returnAll(true).build()` | `ON_SELF_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD_FROM_BATTLEFIELD` | Spreading Algae. **Battlefield-only** slot (fires only when the source zone is `BATTLEFIELD`, i.e. the permanent "dies") — do NOT use `ON_SELF_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD_FROM_ANYWHERE`, which would wrongly fire on mill/discard/counter |
| "Enchant player. If a card would be put into enchanted player's graveyard from anywhere, instead reveal it and put it on the bottom of that player's library" | `setEnchantPlayer(true)` + `addEffect(STATIC, new RevealAndPutOnBottomOfLibraryInsteadOfGraveyardEffect())` | `STATIC` | Wheel of Sun and Moon (SHM). Non-Curse "Enchant player" aura — call `setEnchantPlayer(true)` so it targets/attaches to a player (Curses are auto-detected; plain player auras are not). Replacement applied in `GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard` by scanning for a permanent with the effect attached to the graveyard's owner; tokens are unaffected |
| "Whenever a land is put into a graveyard from the battlefield, this artifact deals 2 damage to that land's controller" | `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(2, DamageRecipient.TRIGGERING_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER)` | `ON_ANY_LAND_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD_FROM_BATTLEFIELD` | Dingus Egg. Fires for any player's land (destroy, sacrifice, etc.); the collector pre-sets the damage target to the land's controller at trigger time. Parallels Magnetic Mine's artifact version |
| "Whenever a black card is put into an opponent's graveyard from anywhere, you may draw a card" | `MayEffect(new DrawCardEffect(), "Draw a card?")` | `ON_BLACK_CARD_PUT_INTO_OPPONENT_GRAVEYARD_FROM_ANYWHERE` | Compost. Fires from any zone (battlefield/hand/library/stack) via `GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard`; only on permanents controlled by an opponent of the graveyard owner |
| "Whenever a permanent an opponent controls is put into a graveyard, put that card onto the battlefield under your control unless that opponent pays 3 life" | `StealDyingOpponentPermanentUnlessPaysLifeEffect(3)` | `ON_OPPONENT_PERMANENT_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD_FROM_BATTLEFIELD` | Prince of Thralls. Fires for any permanent type from the battlefield; "that opponent" (the dying permanent's controller) chooses pay-life vs. lose-the-permanent (can't-pay ⇒ auto-steal). Stolen via `trackStolenCreature`, so it returns to its owner on death |
| "If a card would be put into an opponent's graveyard from anywhere, exile it instead" | `ExileOpponentCardsInsteadOfGraveyardEffect()` | `STATIC` | Leyline of the Void. Replacement effect checked in `GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard` |
| "If a card would be put into your graveyard from anywhere, exile that card instead" | `ExileOwnCardsInsteadOfGraveyardEffect()` | `STATIC` | Forbidden Crypt (controller-side; only your own graveyard). Replacement checked in `GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard` |
| "You may cast spells that have a cycling ability from your graveyard" / "If a card that has a cycling ability would be put into your graveyard from anywhere and it wasn't cycled, exile it instead" | `CastSpellsWithCyclingFromGraveyardEffect()` + `ExileOwnCyclingCardsUnlessCycledEffect()` | `STATIC` | Abandoned Sarcophagus. Cast permission via `CastSpellsFromGraveyardPermission`; exile replacement via `OwnGraveyardExileReplacement` (cycling discard sets `GameData.cardEnteringGraveyardByCycling`) |
| "If you would draw a card, return a card from your graveyard to your hand instead. If you can't, you lose the game." | `ReturnFromGraveyardInsteadOfDrawEffect()` | `STATIC` | Forbidden Crypt. Forced `GraveyardChoice` (HAND) on each draw; empty graveyard → the drawer loses. Detected in `DrawService.resolveDrawCard` |
| "If you would lose the game, instead shuffle your hand, your graveyard, and all permanents you own into your library, then draw seven cards and your life total becomes 20." | `ReplaceControllerLossWithGameResetEffect()` | `STATIC` | Lich's Mirror. Loss-replacement consulted at every rules-loss source (`GameOutcomeService.replaceLossWithGameReset`), executed by `LichsMirrorResetService`. One-shot (the Mirror shuffles itself away); poison is NOT reset |
| "When enchanted [land] becomes tapped, destroy it" | `DestroyEnchantedPermanentEffect()` | `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_TAPPED` | Spreading Algae. Destroys the permanent the source Aura is attached to (re-derived at resolution via the Aura's `attachedTo`). Pair the Aura's `target(...)` with the enchant filter (e.g. `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(SWAMP)`) |
| "When a creature dies, destroy enchanted creature" | `DestroyEnchantedPermanentEffect()` | `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES` | Yoke of the Damned. Fires whenever any creature dies (including the enchanted one — then the orphaned Aura is already in the graveyard, so it fizzles). The collector bakes the Aura's source-permanent id so the enchanted creature is re-derived at resolution |
| "Whenever enchanted land becomes tapped, this Aura deals N damage to that land's controller" | `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(N, DamageRecipient.TRIGGERING_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER)` | `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_TAPPED` | Psychic Venom. The `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_TAPPED` collector bakes the damage target to the tapped permanent's controller. Pair the Aura's `target(...)` with `PermanentIsLandPredicate` |
| "Whenever enchanted land becomes tapped, its controller loses N life" | `LoseLifeEffect(N, LoseLifeRecipient.TARGET_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER)` | `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_TAPPED` | Corrupted Roots. Life loss, **not** damage (CR 118.2) — fires "loses life" triggers and can't be prevented. The collector bakes the tapped land into the entry's `targetId` so `TARGET_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER` re-derives its controller. Pair the Aura's `target(...)` with the enchant filter (`PermanentHasAnySubtypePredicate(Set.of(FOREST, PLAINS))`) |
| "Whenever enchanted creature becomes tapped, put a -0/-2 counter on it" | `PutCounterOnEnchantedCreatureEffect(CounterType.MINUS_ZERO_MINUS_TWO)` | `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_TAPPED` | Spirit Shackle. The effect re-derives the enchanted creature from the source Aura's `attachedTo` at resolution. Pair the Aura's `target(...)` with `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate` |
| "At the beginning of the upkeep of enchanted [land]'s controller, destroy that [land] unless that player pays {M} or N life" | `DestroyEnchantedPermanentUnlessPaysManaOrLifeEffect("{M}", N)` | `ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER_UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` | Erosion (`"{1}", 1`). Punisher: the enchanted permanent's controller may pay mana **or** life to save it, else it's destroyed. Pair the Aura's `target(...)` with `PermanentIsLandPredicate` |
| "{T}: All damage that would be dealt to target creature this turn by a source of your choice is dealt to this creature instead" | `RedirectTargetCreatureDamageFromChosenSourceToSelfEffect()` | activated ability (target creature, `requiresTap`) | Oracle's Attendants. Ability targets the protected creature; the source is chosen on resolution. Redirects to the source permanent (self). Works in both combat and noncombat creature-damage paths. Not Harm's Way (`PreventDamageFromChosenSourceAndRedirectToAnyTargetEffect`), which protects a player's permanents with a capped amount |
| "{1}: The next time a source of your choice would deal damage to target creature this turn, that source deals that damage to you instead" | `RedirectTargetCreatureNextDamageFromChosenSourceToControllerEffect()` | activated ability (target creature) | Jade Monolith. Ability targets the protected creature; the source is chosen on resolution. Redirects the next single damage event in full to the controller (you), then consumes the shield. Works in both combat and noncombat creature-damage paths. Like Oracle's Attendants but redirect target is a player and it is one-shot (`CreatureDamageRedirectShield.NEXT_EVENT`) |
| "COST: The next N damage that would be dealt to this creature this turn is dealt to target creature instead" | `RedirectNextDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(N)` | activated ability (target creature) | Zealous Inquisitor. Ability targets the redirect-destination creature; the protected creature is this ability's own source. Any source, amount-limited to the next N; consumed once used. Works in both combat and noncombat creature-damage paths |
| "COST: The next N damage that would be dealt to this creature this turn is dealt to its owner instead" | `RedirectNextDamageToSelfToOwnerEffect(N)` | activated ability (no target) | Personal Incarnation. No target: the protected creature is the ability's own source; redirect destination is the source's controller (its owner, a player). Any source, amount-limited to the next N; consumed once used. Same `CreatureDamageRedirectShield` machinery as Zealous Inquisitor but destined for a player |
| "When this Aura enters, all damage that would be dealt this turn to you and permanents you control is dealt to enchanted creature instead" | `RedirectYourDamageToEnchantedCreatureThisTurnEffect()` | `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` (no target) | Saving Grace. Installs a turn-scoped `TurnDamageRedirectToCreatureShield(auraController, enchantedCreatureId)`; the destination creature is locked in at resolution (persists even if the Aura leaves). Redirects at all four damage paths (any source, unlimited) via `DamagePreventionService.applyTurnDamageRedirectToCreature`; skipped while the destination is no longer a creature on the battlefield, and for damage to that creature itself. Enchant creature you control via `ControlledPermanentPredicateTargetFilter`; pair with `StaticBoostEffect(0, 3, ENCHANTED_CREATURE)` |

## Alternate casting costs / keywords

| Oracle text phrase | How | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| "Evoke {cost}" (cast for alternate cost; sacrificed when it enters) | `addCastingOption(new AlternateHandCast(List.of(new ManaCastingCost("{W}"))))` + `addEffect(ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD, new SacrificeSelfIfEvokedEffect())` | Dawnfluke. Pure-mana alternate cost, so it can't be inferred from a sacrifice list — cast via `GameService.playCardWithEvoke`. The evoke flag rides `StackEntry`/`Permanent`; `EtbEffectResolver` resolves `SacrificeSelfIfEvokedEffect` to a `SacrificeSelfEffect` only when evoked (intervening-if, CR 603.4). Keep the actual ETB effect(s) as separate `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` entries. |
| "Emerge {cost}" (sacrifice a creature; pay emerge cost reduced by its mana value) | `addCastingOption(new AlternateHandCast(List.of(new ManaCastingCost("{6}{B}"), new SacrificePermanentsCost(1, PermanentIsCreaturePredicate())), true))` | Abundant Maw. The `true` is `reduceManaBySacrificedManaValue` — generic portion only (colored mana can't be reduced). Cast via `castCreatureWithAlternateCost` / `alternateCostSacrificePermanentIds`. |

## Conditional wrappers

| Oracle text phrase | Wrapper | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| "you may [effect]" | `MayEffect(innerEffect, "prompt")` | Player chooses |
| "if you control three or more artifacts, [effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new Metalcraft(), innerEffect)` | Metalcraft |
| "if a creature died this turn, [effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new Morbid(), innerEffect)` | Morbid |
| "if a creature died under your control this turn, [effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new CreatureDiedUnderYourControlThisTurn(), innerEffect)` | Controller-scoped morbid; checks `gameData.creatureDeathCountThisTurn` for the effect's controller (e.g. Essenceknit Scholar end-step draw) |
| "at the beginning of your end step, if a card left your graveyard this turn, [effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new CardsLeftGraveyardThisTurn(), innerEffect)` on `CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED` | Checks `gameData.playersWhoseCardsLeftGraveyardThisTurn` (set in `GraveyardService.notifyCardsLeftGraveyard`); reset each turn. End-step intervening-if handled in `StepTriggerService` (e.g. Primary Research) |
| "if you attacked this turn, [effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new Raid(), innerEffect)` | Raid |
| "if five or more mana was spent to cast that spell, [effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new SpellManaSpentAtLeast(5), innerEffect)` inside `SpellCastTriggerEffect` | Trigger collector snapshots mana spent into stack entry `xValue` |
| "[effect A] if {W} was spent to cast this spell. [effect B] if {U} was spent to cast this spell. (Do both if {W}{U} was spent.)" | one `ConditionalEffect(new ColorSpentToCast(ManaColor.WHITE), effectA)` + one `ConditionalEffect(new ColorSpentToCast(ManaColor.BLUE), effectB)`, both `SPELL` | Payment snapshots colors spent into `GameData.spellCastColorsSpent` (gated by `EffectResolution.hasColorSpentCondition`); each conditional re-checks at resolution. "Do both" is automatic. A targeted clause ("counter up to one target creature spell") uses `target(filter, 0, 1)` on the conditional-wrapped effect. Repel Intruders (SHM) |
| Opus "[base]. If five or more mana was spent to cast that spell, [upgraded] instead" (single target/self) | `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new SpellManaSpentAtLeast(5), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)` inside `SpellCastTriggerEffect` | Use for "instead" upgrades where a base+conditional pair would double a target (e.g. Exhibition Tidecaller `MillEffect(3, TARGET_PLAYER)` → `(10, TARGET_PLAYER)`; Deluge Virtuoso boost uses the additive `BoostSelfEffect(1,1)` + `ConditionalEffect(...)` since boosts stack). Player/self targeting and the mana-spent `xValue` are plumbed through the targeted-trigger interaction. Additive stacking effects (`BoostSelfEffect`, `PutCountersOnSelfEffect`) should still use base + `ConditionalEffect` |
| "Repartee — Whenever you cast an instant or sorcery spell that targets a creature, [effect]" | `SpellCastTriggerEffect(CardAnyOfPredicate(INSTANT, SORCERY), List.of(effect), new StackEntryTargetsPermanentPredicate(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate()))` on `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL` | The 3rd/4th-arg `castSpellTargetCondition` gates the trigger on the cast spell's chosen targets (a card-only `spellFilter` can't). Use the `(spellFilter, effects, TargetFilter, StackEntryPredicate)` overload when the resolved effect also targets (e.g. Graduation Day). Repartee itself is unmapped in Scryfall and adds nothing (Lecturing Scornmage, Rehearsed Debater, Stirring Hopesinger, Informed Inkwright, Inkshape Demonstrator, Forum Necroscribe) |
| "Ward—Discard a card" | `CounterUnlessDiscardsEffect()` on `ON_BECOMES_TARGET_OF_OPPONENT_SPELL` | Mirrors Ward {N} = `CounterUnlessPaysEffect(N)` (e.g. Frost Titan); the discard variant is countered immediately if the controller has no card |
| "if you've cast another instant or sorcery spell this turn, [effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new ControllerCastAnotherSpellThisTurn(CardAnyOfPredicate(INSTANT, SORCERY)), innerEffect)` | SPELL | Excludes the resolving spell; checked at resolution time |
| "This creature enters with two -1/-1 counters unless you've cast another red spell this turn" | `ConditionalEffect(new NotCondition(new ControllerCastAnotherSpellThisTurn(new CardColorPredicate(RED))), new EnterWithCountersEffect(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, new Fixed(2)))` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD | Hotheaded Giant. `NotCondition` negates any condition ("unless"); the enters-with replacement applies only when the negated condition holds |
| "if [base], [effect]. If kicked, [upgraded effect] instead" | `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new Kicked(), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)(base, kicked)` | Kicker replaces |
| "if this spell was kicked, [additional effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new Kicked(), innerEffect)` | Kicker adds |

## Own cast-cost reduction ("This spell costs {N} less to cast …")

All spell-self cost reductions use the single `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(DynamicAmount)` on `EffectSlot.STATIC`. **Never add a per-variant `ReduceOwnCastCostIf*`/`Per*` record.** See `COST_MODIFICATION_HANDLERS.md`.

| Oracle text phrase | Effect (EffectSlot.STATIC) | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| "costs {N} less to cast" (flat) | `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(new Fixed(N))` | |
| "costs {N} less to cast for each creature card in your graveyard" | `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(new CardsInGraveyard(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), CountScope.CONTROLLER))` | N=1 → the amount already counts once per card; use `Scaled` for N>1. Ghoultree |
| "costs {1} less to cast for each card type among cards in your graveyard" | `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(new CardTypesAmongCardsInGraveyard())` | Emrakul, the Promised End. Distinct card types (multi-type cards contribute each type) |
| "costs {N} less to cast for each creature on the battlefield" | `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(new PermanentCount(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), CountScope.ANY_PLAYER))` | Blasphemous Act. Use `CONTROLLER`/`OPPONENTS` scope for "you control"/"an opponent controls" wordings |
| "costs {2} less to cast for each basic land type among lands you control" (Domain) | `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(new Scaled(new BasicLandTypesAmongControlledLands(), 2))` | Draco. `BasicLandTypesAmongControlledLands` counts distinct basic land types (Plains/Island/Swamp/Mountain/Forest), respecting CR 305.7 land-type overrides; `Scaled(amount, 2)` for the {2}-per-type multiplier |
| "costs {2} less to cast for each card you've cycled or discarded this turn" | `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(new Scaled(new CardsDiscardedOrCycledThisTurn(), 2))` | Hollow One. Cycling is a discard (CR 702.29e); reads `GameData.cardsDiscardedThisTurn` for the controller |
| "costs {N} less to cast if you control a [permanent]" | `ConditionalEffect(new ControlsPermanent(predicate), new ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(new Fixed(N)))` | Academy Journeymage / Wizard's Retort / Wizard's Lightning (WIZARD), Lookout's Dispersal (PIRATE) |
| "costs {N} less to cast if you control three or more artifacts" | `ConditionalEffect(new Metalcraft(), new ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(new Fixed(N)))` | Stoic Rebuttal |
| "costs {N} less to cast if an opponent controls at least M more creatures than you" | `ConditionalEffect(new OpponentControlsMoreCreatures(M), new ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(new Fixed(N)))` | Avatar of Might (M=4, N=6) |
| "if an opponent controls more lands than you, [effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new OpponentControlsMoreLands(), wrapped)` | SPELL | Gift of Estates: wraps `SearchLibraryEffect(new Fixed(3), new CardSubtypePredicate(CardSubtype.PLAINS), LibrarySearchDestination.HAND)`. Condition is strictly-more (difference ≥ 1) |
| "costs {N} less to cast if one or more cards left your graveyard this turn" | `ConditionalEffect(new CardsLeftGraveyardThisTurn(), new ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(new Fixed(N)))` | Wilt in the Heat |
| "costs {N} less to cast if it targets [permanent/spell]" | `ReduceOwnCastCostIfTargetingPermanentEffect` / `…IfTargetingControlledPermanentEffect` / `…IfTargetingStackEntryEffect` | **Kept as their own records** — the reduction gates on the being-cast spell's chosen first target (resolved inline in `CastingCostService.computeTargetBasedCostReduction`). Ajani's Response, Savage Stomp, Brush Off |
| "if you control a [subtype], [effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new ControlsPermanent(new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(subtype)), innerEffect)` | Permanent predicate check |
| "if you control a [matching permanent], [effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new ControlsPermanent(predicate), innerEffect)` | Permanent check |
| "if you control a [subtype], [upgraded effect] instead" | `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new ControlsPermanent(filter), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)(new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(subtype), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)` | Resolution-time replacement |
| "if that/target creature is a [subtype], [upgraded effect] instead" | `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new TargetPermanentMatches(filter), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)(new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(subtype), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)` | Target permanent checked at resolution; falls back to base if missing or nonmatching |
| "Infusion — if you gained life this turn, [additional effect]" | `ConditionalEffect(new GainedLifeThisTurn(), innerEffect)` | Life gained tracked in `GameData.lifeGainedThisTurn` (via `LifeSupport`), cleared each turn; also valid as a static self-buff (`StaticBoostEffect(...GrantScope.SELF)`) e.g. Ulna Alley Shopkeep |
| "[base effect]. Infusion — if you gained life this turn, [upgraded effect] instead" | `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new GainedLifeThisTurn(), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)` | Resolution-time replacement, e.g. Withering Curse (mass -2/-2 upgraded to destroy all creatures) |
| "Infusion — At the beginning of your end step, [downside] unless you gained life this turn" | `ConditionalEffect(new DidntGainLifeThisTurn(), downsideEffect)` in `CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED` | `DidntGainLifeThisTurn` is the negation of `GainedLifeThisTurn`; for "sacrifice a permanent" use `SacrificePermanentThenEffect(new PermanentTruePredicate(), null, "a permanent")` (null thenEffect = no follow-up). E.g. Tragedy Feaster |
| "choose one —" | `ChooseOneEffect(List<ChooseOneOption>)` | Modal |
| "Whenever enchanted artifact becomes tapped, choose one — 1 damage to target player/planeswalker; or target player gains 1 life" | `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_TAPPED RelicBindTapEffect()` | Trigger | Modal *triggered* ability (no cast-time modal path for triggers): mode picked at resolution via `ChoiceContext.RelicBindModeChoice`, then the chosen mode's targeted effect routes through the `MayAbilityTriggerTarget` flow. Relic Bind. Generalize the collector/handler for other modal enchanted-tap triggers |
| "Whenever you cast a spell, choose up to one — return target spell you don't control to hand; or return target nonland permanent to hand" | `SpellCastTriggerEffect(null, List.of(new HullbreakerHorrorTriggerEffect()))` | `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL` | Hullbreaker Horror. Modal trigger at resolution (`ChoiceContext.HullbreakerHorrorModeChoice`) with SPELL / PERMANENT / NONE; chosen bounce routes through `MayAbilityTriggerTarget` (`ReturnTargetSpellToHandEffect` or `ReturnToHandEffect.target()`) |
| "choose two —" | `ChooseOneEffect(List<ChooseOneOption>, 2)` | Modal | Pass `choicesRequired=2`; cast with negative bitmask via `ChooseOneEffect.encodeModeSelection(2, mode0, mode1)`. Chosen modes resolve in card-text order (Austere Command). Per-mode targeting is supported: a mode's `targetFilter`/`targetFilters` declares its own target slot(s) (in chosen-mode order), so a choose-two spell can mix targeting modes — e.g. Incendiary Command (player/planeswalker + nonbasic land). Modes with no explicit filter keep their effects' intrinsic targeting channel — spell targetId / permanent targetIds (Cryptic Command) |

## Turn / phase

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "take an extra turn after this one. Exile [this]" | `ControllerExtraTurnEffect(1)` + `ExileSpellEffect()` | SPELL | Temporal Mastery. Pair with `addCastingOption(new MiracleCast("{cost}"))` for Miracle |
| "take an extra turn after this one" | `ControllerExtraTurnEffect(1)` | SPELL | Non-targeting |
| "take an extra turn after this one. Skip the untap step of that turn" | `ControllerExtraTurnEffect(1, true)` | SPELL | Savor the Moment. The extra turn's untap step is skipped (permanents stay tapped), but summoning sickness still clears so already-controlled creatures can act |
| "take an extra turn after this one. At the beginning of that turn's end step, you lose the game" | `ControllerExtraTurnEffect(1)` + `RegisterLoseGameAtEndStepEffect()` | SPELL | Last Chance. The register-effect schedules a `LoseGameAtEndStep` delayed action tagged with the current turn number; it fires at the controller's own next end step (skips the current turn's own end step and any opponent end step, landing on the extra turn's), pushing `TargetPlayerLosesGameEffect` onto the stack (respects can't-lose) |
| "End the turn. At the beginning of your next end step, you lose the game" | `EndTurnEffect()` + `RegisterLoseGameAtEndStepEffect()` | SPELL | Glorious End. Ending the turn skips the current turn's end step, so the delayed loss lands on the controller's *own* next end step (skipping the intervening opponent turn's end step — CR "your end step" only fires on your turns). `RegisterLoseGameAtEndStepEffect`'s active-player-gated drain enforces this |
| "untap all creatures that attacked this turn. After this main phase, there is an additional combat phase followed by an additional main phase" | `AdditionalCombatMainPhaseEffect(1)` | SPELL | |
| "Whenever a creature you control attacks alone, if it's the first combat phase of the turn, untap that creature. After this phase, there is an additional combat phase" | `ConditionalEffect(AttacksAlone, ConditionalEffect(FirstCombatPhase, UntapPermanentsEffect(ATTACKED_CREATURES)))` + `ConditionalEffect(AttacksAlone, ConditionalEffect(FirstCombatPhase, AdditionalCombatPhaseEffect(1)))` | ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ATTACKS | Finest Hour (ARB). Exalted itself is an auto-loaded keyword. The outer `AttacksAlone` is stripped at trigger collection (fires only when alone); the inner `FirstCombatPhase` intervening-if is re-checked at resolution so the extra combat phase it creates can't loop. `AdditionalCombatPhaseEffect` adds a combat phase with NO extra main phase (unlike Relentless Assault) |
| "that player skips their next combat phase" (combat-damage trigger) | `SkipNextCombatPhaseEffect()` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Non-targeting; the damaged player is baked in as `targetId`. Increments per-player `GameData.skipNextCombatPhaseCount`; that player jumps from precombat main straight to postcombat main. Blinding Angel |
| "Whenever ~ deals combat damage to a player, put a charge counter on it." | `PutCountersOnSelfEffect(CounterType.CHARGE)` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Lightning Reaver (ARB). `PutCountersOnSelfEffect` binds `SOURCE_SELF`, so the counter lands on the damage-dealing creature. Use the +1/+1-only `PutCountersOnSourceEffect(1,1,1)` for "put a +1/+1 counter on it" instead (Erdwal Ripper) |
| "Whenever ~ deals combat damage to a player, that player reveals their hand. You choose a card from it. That player exiles that card." | `ChooseCardsFromTargetHandEffect(1, List.of(), List.of(), HandChoiceDestination.EXILE, false)` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Ghastlord of Fugue (SHM). No `target(...)` — CombatDamageService bakes the damaged player in as `targetId`; the controller chooses the card. Empty `excludedTypes` = any card choosable |
| "Whenever ~ deals combat damage to a player, that player discards that many cards." | `DiscardEffect(new EventValue(), DiscardRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Needle Specter (EVE). Non-targeting; CombatDamageService bakes the damaged player as `targetId` and sets `eventValue = damageDealt`, which `EventValue` reads for the discard count. Fixed-count discard specters (Abyssal Specter) use `DiscardEffect(1, TARGET_PLAYER)` instead |
| "Whenever ~ deals combat damage to a player, you may draw that many cards." | `new MayEffect(new DrawCardEffect(new EventValue()), "Draw that many cards?")` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Cold-Eyed Selkie (EVE). CombatDamageService detects the wrapped `DrawCardEffect(EventValue)` and snapshots `eventValue = damageDealt` onto the queued may-ability stack entry; the resolution-time "you may" re-runs the same entry so `EventValue` reads the damage for the draw count |
| "Whenever equipped creature deals combat damage to a player, that player loses half their life, rounded up." | `LoseLifeEffect(new HalvedRoundedUp(new TargetPlayerLifeTotal()), LoseLifeRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Quietus Spike (ALA). No `target(...)` — CombatDamageService bakes the damaged player as `targetId`; the loss is computed at resolution from that player's *current* life (after combat damage). `HalvedRoundedUp` ceils where `Divided(_, 2)` floors |
| "Whenever ~ deals combat damage to a player, you may cast a spell from your hand without paying its mana cost." | `MayCastAnySpellFromHandWithoutPayingManaCostEffect()` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Maelstrom Archangel (CON). No `target(...)`. Offers each nonland hand card as a MayCastFromHandWithoutPayingManaCostEffect PendingMayAbility; casting one clears the rest (reuses the Counterlash routing). No `MayEffect` wrapper — the per-card may-abilities are themselves the "you may" |
| "Whenever this creature attacks and isn't blocked, you may cast an instant or sorcery spell from your hand without paying its mana cost" | `MayCastAnySpellFromHandWithoutPayingManaCostEffect(CardAnyOf(INSTANT, SORCERY))` | ON_ATTACKS_UNBLOCKED | Wildfire Eternal. Same free-cast routing as Maelstrom Archangel; optional `spellFilter` restricts eligible hand cards (null = any nonland). Pair Afflict N with `LoseLifeEffect(N, DEFENDING_PLAYER)` on `ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED` |
| "Whenever ~ deals combat damage to a player, create two 1/1 red Goblin creature tokens and sacrifice this creature." | `SequenceEffect.of(new CreateTokenEffect(2, "Goblin", 1, 1, CardColor.RED, List.of(CardSubtype.GOBLIN), Set.of(), Set.of()), new SacrificeSelfEffect())` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER | Kathari Bomber (ARB). One atomic entry. `SacrificeSelfEffect` reports `CombatDamageTriggerContextEffect.SOURCE_SELF` and `SequenceEffect` forwards the richest step context, so the trigger's stack entry binds the source and the sacrifice resolves (a plain combat-damage entry has no source) |
| "target player skips all combat phases of their next turn" | `SkipNextCombatPhaseEffect(true)` | SPELL | Targeted variant (`targetsPlayer = true` → player-targeting spec); caster picks the affected player. Same counter model as above. False Peace |
| "during target player's next turn, creatures that player controls attack you if able" | `MustAttackControllerNextTurnEffect()` | SPELL | Targets a player. Stored in `GameData.tauntedNextTurn`, promoted to `tauntedThisTurn` when that player's turn begins; `CombatAttackService` forces all their creatures to attack the caster if able. Taunt |
| "[Subtype] creatures attack each combat if able" | `MatchingCreaturesMustAttackEffect(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(SUBTYPE))` | STATIC | Global (any controller); read in `CombatAttackService.getMustAttackRequirementCount`. Goblin Assault (GOBLIN) |
| "creatures your opponents control get -1/-1 until end of turn. Those creatures attack this turn if able" | `BoostAllCreaturesEffect(-1, -1, new PermanentNotPredicate(new PermanentControlledBySourceControllerPredicate()))` + `MatchingCreaturesMustAttackThisTurnEffect(new PermanentNotPredicate(new PermanentControlledBySourceControllerPredicate()))` | ACTIVATED_ABILITY | Both one-shot, non-targeted; `PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentControlledBySourceControllerPredicate())` = "not controlled by you" = opponents' creatures. Sacrifice-cost ability (`SacrificeSelfCost`). Suicidal Charge |
| "Creatures target opponent controls attack this turn if able. During that player's next untap step, creatures they control don't untap." | `target(PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(PlayerRelationPredicate(OPPONENT)))` → `TargetPlayersCreaturesMustAttackThisTurnEffect()` + `SkipNextUntapEffect(TapUntapScope.TARGET_PLAYERS_PERMANENTS, new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate())` | SPELL (both bound to one player target) | Imaginary Threats. Cast on the opponent's turn before their combat. Player-targeted must-attack (locked at resolution, like Suicidal Charge's flag) + Sleep's player-scoped skip-untap. Plus `Cycling {2}`. |

## Copy

| Oracle text phrase | Effect | Slot | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| "copy target instant or sorcery spell" | `CopySpellEffect()` | SPELL | Filter on the Card's SpellTarget via `target(...)`. Add `StackEntryControlledByPredicate` for "...spell you control" |
| "copy target creature spell you control. The copy gains haste and 'at the beginning of the end step, sacrifice this token.'" | `CopySpellEffect(null, true, true)` | SPELL | The creature-spell copy becomes a token, gains `HASTE`, and is registered for end-step sacrifice (`GameData.delayedActions` (a `DelayedPermanentAction(SACRIFICE_AT_END_STEP)`)). Restrict targeting to creature spells you control via the mode's `StackEntryPredicateTargetFilter(StackEntryAllOfPredicate(StackEntryTypeInPredicate(CREATURE_SPELL), StackEntryControlledByPredicate))`. See Choreographed Sparks |
| "this spell can't be copied" | `card.setCantBeCopied(true)` (not an effect) | constructor | Honored by every copy handler (`CopySpellEffectHandler`, `CopySpellForEachOtherPlayerEffectHandler`, `CopyControllerCastSpellEffectHandler`) — the copy is simply not created. Choreographed Sparks |
| "choose one or both — copy target instant/sorcery you control • copy target creature spell you control" | `ChooseOneEffect` with 3 modes; the "both" mode uses `ChooseOneOption(label, List.of(copyIS, copyCreature), List.of(isFilter, creatureFilter))` | SPELL | Two distinct spell targets in one mode — see the "choose one or both with two distinct spell targets" row in CARD_PATTERNS_LANDS_SPELLS.md. | "choose one or both — counter target creature spell • return target creature card from your graveyard to your hand" | `ChooseOneEffect` with 3 modes; mode 0 `CounterSpellEffect` + creature-spell `StackEntryPredicateTargetFilter`, mode 1 `ReturnTargetCardsFromGraveyardToHandEffect(CREATURE,1)`, "both" mode `ChooseOneOption(label, List.of(counter, return), counterFilter)` (single-filter overload) | SPELL | Counter (stack target) + interactive graveyard return coexist via `graveyardTargetOperation.spellCounterTargetId` threaded onto the entry with `Zone.STACK`. See the "counter a spell + return from graveyard" row in CARD_PATTERNS_LANDS_SPELLS.md. Soul Manipulation |
| "copy target instant or sorcery spell. Flashback can target a spell on the stack |
| "you may choose new targets for target instant or sorcery spell. Then copy that spell. The redirect-retarget completion resumes any following effects on the same spell (`handleSpellRetarget` / `handleResolutionTimeMayChoice`) |

| "whenever enchanted player casts an instant or sorcery spell, each other player may copy that spell" | `CopySpellForEachOtherPlayerEffect(true, new StackEntryControlledByEnchantedPlayerPredicate())` | ON_ANY_PLAYER_CASTS_SPELL | Curse of Echoes — the `StackEntryControlledByEnchantedPlayerPredicate` filter gates to casts by the enchanted player; each other player *may* copy |
| "creatures enchanted player controls lose all abilities and have base power and toughness 1/1" | `LosesAllAbilitiesEffect(GrantScope.ENCHANTED_PLAYER_CREATURES)` + `SetBasePowerToughnessEffect(1, 1, GrantScope.ENCHANTED_PLAYER_CREATURES)` | STATIC | Overwhelming Splendor — enchant player Curse (auto-detected from CURSE subtype); layer 6 ability loss + layer 7b base-P/T set on the enchanted player's creatures |

| "whenever you cast an instant or sorcery spell, you may tap three untapped creatures you control. If you do, copy that spell" | `CopyControllerCastSpellOnSpellCastEffect(CardAnyOfPredicate(INSTANT, SORCERY), new TapMultiplePermanentsCost(3, PermanentIsCreaturePredicate))` | ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL | Aziza, Mage Tower Captain — snapshots cast spell, `MayPayTapPermanentsEffect` + `CopyControllerCastSpellEffect` at resolution |
| "whenever you cast a multicolored instant or sorcery spell, you may pay {1}. | "Storm (When you cast this spell, copy it for each spell cast before it this turn.)" | `StormEffect()` | ON_SELF_CAST | Dragonstorm. `TriggerCollectionService.checkSpellCastTriggers` snapshots the just-cast spell and queues a `StormCopyEffect(snapshot, caster, copies)` where `copies = gameData.getTotalSpellsCastThisTurnCount() - 1` (all players, minus this spell which is already recorded). Each copy may choose new targets |
| "Cascade (When you cast this spell, exile cards from the top of your library until you exile a nonland card that costs less. You may cast it without paying its mana cost. No hit → all exiled cards go to the bottom |

One trigger per granting permanent; the free cascade cast is the caster's 2nd spell so it never re-triggers |
| "whenever you activate an ability, if it isn't a mana ability, you may pay {2}. If you do, copy that ability" | `CopyControllerActivatedAbilityTriggerEffect("{2}")` | ON_CONTROLLER_ACTIVATES_NONMANA_ABILITY | Rings of Brighthearth — snapshots the non-mana ability after it's on the stack, `MayPayManaEffect` + `CopyControllerActivatedAbilityEffect` at resolution; single-target copies may be retargeted |
| "whenever an opponent activates an ability of an artifact, creature, or land, if it isn't a mana ability, ~ deals N damage to that player" | `TriggeringPermanentConditionalEffect(new PermanentAnyOfPredicate(List.of(new PermanentIsArtifactPredicate(), new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), new PermanentIsLandPredicate())), new DealDamageToPlayersEffect(N, DamageRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER))` | ON_OPPONENT_ACTIVATES_NONMANA_ABILITY | Harsh Mentor — fires on every permanent NOT controlled by the activating player; slot is reached only on the non-mana activation path so "if it isn't a mana ability" is automatic; the conditional wrapper filters by the activated permanent's type; the activating opponent is baked as the non-targeting `targetId` |

| "Whenever a creature dies, you may pay {N}. Cemetery Puca |

## Mana cost → test `addMana` reference

`ManaColor` enum values: `WHITE` (W), `BLUE` (U), `BLACK` (B), `RED` (R), `GREEN` (G), `COLORLESS` (C).

**Key rule:** Generic mana (the number in a mana cost like `{2}`) can be paid with any color. In tests, pay generic mana using the card's primary color for simplicity — one `addMana` call covers both the generic and colored portions.

### Single-color cards

For a card with one colored symbol, add total CMC of that color:

| Mana cost | `addMana` call | Breakdown |
|---|---|---|
| `{W}` | `addMana(player, WHITE, 1)` | 1W |
| `{U}` | `addMana(player, BLUE, 1)` | 1U |
| `{B}` | `addMana(player, BLACK, 1)` | 1B |
| `{R}` | `addMana(player, RED, 1)` | 1R |
| `{G}` | `addMana(player, GREEN, 1)` | 1G |
| `{1}{W}` | `addMana(player, WHITE, 2)` | 1 generic + 1W |
| `{1}{U}` | `addMana(player, BLUE, 2)` | 1 generic + 1U |
| `{1}{B}` | `addMana(player, BLACK, 2)` | 1 generic + 1B |
| `{1}{R}` | `addMana(player, RED, 2)` | 1 generic + 1R |
| `{1}{G}` | `addMana(player, GREEN, 2)` | 1 generic + 1G |
| `{2}{W}` | `addMana(player, WHITE, 3)` | 2 generic + 1W |
| `{2}{U}` | `addMana(player, BLUE, 3)` | 2 generic + 1U |
| `{2}{B}` | `addMana(player, BLACK, 3)` | 2 generic + 1B |
| `{2}{R}` | `addMana(player, RED, 3)` | 2 generic + 1R |
| `{2}{G}` | `addMana(player, GREEN, 3)` | 2 generic + 1G |
| `{3}{W}` | `addMana(player, WHITE, 4)` | 3 generic + 1W |
| `{4}{B}` | `addMana(player, BLACK, 5)` | 4 generic + 1B |
| `{W}{W}` | `addMana(player, WHITE, 2)` | 2W |
| `{U}{U}` | `addMana(player, BLUE, 2)` | 2U |
| `{B}{B}` | `addMana(player, BLACK, 2)` | 2B |
| `{R}{R}` | `addMana(player, RED, 2)` | 2R |
| `{G}{G}` | `addMana(player, GREEN, 2)` | 2G |
| `{1}{W}{W}` | `addMana(player, WHITE, 3)` | 1 generic + 2W |
| `{2}{U}{U}` | `addMana(player, BLUE, 4)` | 2 generic + 2U |
| `{2}{B}{B}` | `addMana(player, BLACK, 4)` | 2 generic + 2B |
| `{3}{R}{R}` | `addMana(player, RED, 5)` | 3 generic + 2R |
| `{3}{G}{G}` | `addMana(player, GREEN, 5)` | 3 generic + 2G |

**Pattern:** For `{N}{C}{C}` where C is a single color, use `addMana(player, COLOR, N + coloredCount)`.

### Multi-color cards

For cards with multiple colored symbols, add each color separately. Pay generic mana as COLORLESS:

| Mana cost | `addMana` calls | Breakdown |
|---|---|---|
| `{R}{W}` | `addMana(player, RED, 1); addMana(player, WHITE, 1)` | 1R + 1W |
| `{U}{B}` | `addMana(player, BLUE, 1); addMana(player, BLACK, 1)` | 1U + 1B |
| `{B}{G}` | `addMana(player, BLACK, 1); addMana(player, GREEN, 1)` | 1B + 1G |
| `{R}{G}` | `addMana(player, RED, 1); addMana(player, GREEN, 1)` | 1R + 1G |
| `{W}{U}` | `addMana(player, WHITE, 1); addMana(player, BLUE, 1)` | 1W + 1U |
| `{1}{R}{W}` | `addMana(player, RED, 1); addMana(player, WHITE, 1); addMana(player, COLORLESS, 1)` | 1R + 1W + 1 generic |
| `{1}{B}{G}` | `addMana(player, BLACK, 1); addMana(player, GREEN, 1); addMana(player, COLORLESS, 1)` | 1B + 1G + 1 generic |
| `{2}{W}{U}` | `addMana(player, WHITE, 1); addMana(player, BLUE, 1); addMana(player, COLORLESS, 2)` | 1W + 1U + 2 generic |
| `{2}{B}{R}` | `addMana(player, BLACK, 1); addMana(player, RED, 1); addMana(player, COLORLESS, 2)` | 1B + 1R + 2 generic |
| `{1}{W}{U}{B}` | `addMana(player, WHITE, 1); addMana(player, BLUE, 1); addMana(player, BLACK, 1); addMana(player, COLORLESS, 1)` | 3-color + 1 generic |

**Pattern:** Add exact colored amounts per color, then add generic as `COLORLESS`.

### X-cost cards

X is chosen at cast time. Add the colored requirement plus X of any color:

| Mana cost | `addMana` call for X=3 | Breakdown |
|---|---|---|
| `{X}{R}` | `addMana(player, RED, 4)` | X(3) + 1R |
| `{X}{U}` | `addMana(player, BLUE, 4)` | X(3) + 1U |
| `{X}{B}{B}` | `addMana(player, BLACK, 5)` | X(3) + 2B |
| `{X}{R}{G}` | `addMana(player, RED, 1); addMana(player, GREEN, 1); addMana(player, COLORLESS, 3)` | 1R + 1G + X(3) generic |

### Colorless / artifact cards

| Mana cost | `addMana` call | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| `{0}` | *(no mana needed)* | Free cast |
| `{1}` | `addMana(player, COLORLESS, 1)` | Any color also works |
| `{2}` | `addMana(player, COLORLESS, 2)` | |
| `{3}` | `addMana(player, COLORLESS, 3)` | |
| `{5}` | `addMana(player, COLORLESS, 5)` | |
